Et se tu vues, si cauterize a tot le cautere a III ners.	 And if you see, cauterize entirely with the cautery at three nerves.
Aprés le cure quant il a geteit porriture par lonc tens, et ce vaut mues que li autre des cures devant dites.	 After it has poured pus for a long time, and this is good that the other of the said treatments be applied next.
de ydropisie	dropisy
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	 Cauterizing does not help for dropsy, except in the manner called "asclytes.
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis;	 When you treat it according to the methods that we have said in the divisions, and your treatment does not help, then it is necessary that you make four cauteries around the belly, one above the stomach, one above the liver, one above the bladder, two behind the back near the spine, and one at the worst place.
et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	 and let the cauteries be close to the swelling of the cure.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere;	 After leaving the cautery open for long periods to let pus flow out, do not neglect the treatment of the patient after the cautery.
et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	 And healing will hasten, and the two intentions will be united with the help of God.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit;	 The shape of the fire cautery for the stomach is the clavicle that we have previously shown.
et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	 And it for the back is oleander-shaped, as it is described before.
de l’enfleure des piez	of the inflammation of feet
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire;	 When the feet are swollen in those who are edematous and full of citron juice, it is necessary to apply fire cautery on the back of the foot between the little finger and the ring finger.
et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	 And immerse your hand with the cauterizer without turning.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	 And do not go too deep, otherwise the yellow liquid will flow out forcefully; and let the cautery be of this shape:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire;	 After doing two fire cauteries in each leg, at the tip of the big toe.
et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe;	 And let the cautery be long, one below the knee in front and the other behind, within the leg;
et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse;	 leave the cauteries open for a long time without healing, because it helps the juice.
aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	 After the treatment of other ailments as we have said.
de la menoison	treatment of edema
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures;	 When inflammation of the abdomen comes from cold and moisture, as long as the digestive and retentive virtues that are in the stomach and intestines are blocked and cannot be cured by means of treatments;
et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule;	 and you see the patient suffering greatly and of strong nature, make a large fire cautery on the stomach as mentioned before (cautery of the stomach) in the circular cautery.
et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	 and three fine cauteries around the belly, subtle cauteries all around, and two cauteries on the flanks.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et .i. cautere sus chaicun yle, et .ij. petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	And if you see the moisture abundant and the patient suffering, do a cautery on the joint, and one cautery on each isle, and two small cauteries on the stomach near the large one, for the cure is beneficial when there is good aid.
de la cure des emorroydes	of the cure for hemorrhoids
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres:	 When hemorrhoids are on the foundation, one or more, and are old and consist of large cold and moist corrupted humors, and are cured as mentioned in "divisions", but it does not help, make cauteries.
III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois;	 III at the base of the spine on the back, that which is completely dislocated above Almecgate little by little in a triangular shape, and the fire cautery below the hump should be applied.
et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile;	 If you think that his stomach is cooled and the meat does not cook, and his face swells, then the large fire cautery should be applied on the stomach as stated before, and another one on the liver, and another one all over the spleen with a sharp-pointed cautery.
et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	 leave the cautery open for a long time.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	 After curing the shoulder when it is healthy.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	of the charnoisiteit which is called "thelul"
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit;	 When you cut Althelul, if the cautery resembling a razor is heated, then put it all over what you have cut.
et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort;	 and leave your hand so that the cautery reaches the opening of the vein, so that the wound does not close.
fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit;	 Do this once or twice, and if there is much swelling, cauterize each one as we have said.
aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez;	 after the cures of useful ointments while they are clean;
et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	 and if you cauterize with a large cautery on alum, it will have more help.
de plaie mal curee	From an improperly healed wound
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	If the patient cannot endure cutting or opening, which we will describe in its place, this disease comes that can only be healed by cauterization.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	 If any abscess comes, and it is filled with pus and corrupt moisture, you must test the entire tent (or cavity) with extreme caution, and ensure that you understand the entire extent of the corruption.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing;	 After heating the cautery which seems like a razor, and insert it into the fistula according to the quantity that it has entered, and continue the cauterization until the flesh boils and corrodes, once, or twice, or three times, according to the amount of sore needed.
et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	 And beware not to burn the nerve that is within them, and the great veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans;	 If the fistula goes to the body of the bladder and the intestines, beware of these places, and do not do anything foreign except in a charnel house, and think that it is not safe.
aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement;	 After healing the place until it is healed, and if the place is ulcerated and the matter has been removed for a long time, then know that the place is completely healed.
et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font;	 and if the matters are not removed, know that the place is rotten, and the bones are destroyed.
et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	 And similarly as one of these we will say in its place.
de la maladie des reins	of the disease of the kidneys
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit;	 When cold pain comes to the eyes and from strong wind and does not take on a female form, then you must perform cautery on the eyes on both sides with the cauterizing iron as we have previously mentioned.
et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	 And if we cauterize it with hot metal, it will have three cauteries in a row, and they will do more good.
de la vessie	of the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce;	 When the bladder is weak and soft due to coldness or moisture, causing the patient to retain urine, then make a cauterization in the area outside of the bladder where the pubic hair begins, on both sides, each cauterization being as long as one's thumb.
et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing;	 and make the cauterization behind the back, if needed.
et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	 and let the cauterizations be shaped like a nail as previously mentioned.
de la marris	of the kidney
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde;	 When the womb is cold and moist, it does not allow conception to take place, and the flowers are corrupt and their terms are delayed.
et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor:	 And when they come, they feel great pain:
adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos;	 Then it is necessary to do three cauteries around the boil, as we have said, or the cautery of the bladder, and two cauteries behind the back.
et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	 and let the cautery be with a clamp, as we have said.
de la hainche	Of the wound
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble;	 When the viscous humors descend into the bladder and hence move from its place, and this is shown by the fact that the thigh is longer than the other when measured together;
et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle;	 and the location of the departure is found, it is necessary to cauterize the patient above the bladder at the cautery similar to a circle, and mark the spot in front of the location around the bladder so that the bladder is within the circle.
et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	 And if [the fire cautery] is similar to those from which the stomach has been cauterized.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs;	 If [the fire cautery] is not present, make three large olive oil cauterizations, and let the cautery be as deep as all the others.
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And heal it until it becomes healthy.
de la dolor de la hainche	Of the pain of the haunch
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene:	 When pain occurs in the abdomen of the hernia, and it is caused by coldness or moisture, the patient is treated as we have said in the previous section, but the treatment has no effect, and the illness is chronic.
adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	 Therefore, you must purge the patient of gross humors using foul-smelling pills or other good-looking pills.
Aprés li fai cautere;	 After that, make a cautery.
et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres:	 And the manner of the cautery is according to two methods:
c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	 that is to say with burning substances and fire cautery.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz:	 Fire cautery can be done in various ways, one of which is:
que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire;	 You shall apply fire cautery on the boil of the hernia. Three triangular cauteries according to this form, make a good and deep incision and wide, with space between each cauterization equal to the thickness of a thumb, and let the cauteries be olive-shaped.
aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	 Sometimes a fire cautery is made in the middle on the hernia's head, for which there are four according to this form.
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche;	 And if you see, cauterize with the circular cautery as we have said earlier in the dislocation of the hernia.
mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	 But do it in such a manner that the circles encompass the entire hernia and all its thickness is burned.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	 And this is the way it is done in sciatica, when the pain remains in the haunch and does not reach either the thigh or the leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc;	 And if it comes up to the thigh and the leg, make two cauteries there where the patient says the pain is, and four on the ankle, three-quarters of an inch on the left side.
et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur;	 And let the cautery be a cutlery, and let the thickness of the coal be heated.
et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	 And if the patient feels that the pain extends to the thigh or near it, cauterize it three or four inches with a cautery called "poins".
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus;	 And if necessary, make more of it.
et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	 And if the pain is below the knee towards the thigh, cauterize with a cutlery or circular cautery, and be careful in all your cauteries that you do not let the cautery burn the nerves and large arteries, and do not cause more harm and contraction to the patient.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	 I myself have seen more who made a cautery above the ankle on the foot and allowed it to remain until the leg swelled completely and the toes also, and they were pierced and corrupted all the toes.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	 After a stomach solution, he died.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	 If the pain is in two parts together, perform cautery on one and the other, according to this method.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce;	 And the wise men say about the cautery of the ankle, in this way, make a nail as thick as a little finger or a bit smaller, and between cross-pieces or from one crosspiece to another of a space equal to the size of a nut.
et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait;	 And the joints above the two parts should be over the bones, and they should be like knuckles, and it should have one iron handle well made.
et c’est li forme:	 and this is its form:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit;	 and let it be scorched until they are all red and blistered, and then place it upon the patient's sick side, and turn it on the healthy side.
et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors;	 and let the fire cautery be applied once, and leave it for three days;
et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens;	 and then apply a plaster of butter, and keep the wound open for a long time.
aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	 after the treatment with salve until it is healed.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent;	 Al-Zahrawi says that we should not use this cautery too much due to fear of its gaze, and few people who use it.
et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	 And indeed, this is one of the good cauteries, which can endure it, and there where he feels it.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi;	 The medical cautery is made by heating an instrument between the joints, and it should be of iron or steel with a long shaft, and at the top have two arms, and between each arm, the thickness of a finger joint.
et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	 And they are open on both sides and above, and they join together in this way:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche;	 After placing the iron device on the patient lying on the sick side, put your hand a little above the iron device.
aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	 After pouring the hot liquid between the two circles of the heated iron and letting it sit for an hour, let the patient endure the heat and burn of it.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu;	 It burns as if with fire; [or] It bites like fire.
et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit;	 And when the biting [pains] have passed, place your hand with the tool and gently lift the blister from below, leaving it so for three days, and apply butter until the blackness of the burn is removed.
et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait;	 and leave it for three days to draw out pus.
et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And this will be the last aid after the ointment treatment until it is healed.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument;	 And if the pain has spread to the thigh or leg, make the instrument that burns like the blister as you did in the blister [treatment].
et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	 This is the method of hot water, and I have written or treated it regarding the correction of medicine.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	 Take quicklime and hot coals, equal amounts of each, grind them together, and put them in a new pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir;	 If there is a small opening exposed, let the point of a finger enter it.
et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main;	 Then remove that pot with another pot well weighted down, and put on top of it alum and salt and soft ash until there is enough powder above for you to grasp hold of it with your hand.
et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	 and leave it so until it dries up with ash and heat or sinks down or is weighed down, then take all that ash and throw it onto salt and onto alum as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres.	 And afterwards, it will become very dry and be administered in the service of medical work and in cauteries for other limbs.
Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	 For it performs the same work as fire, and if used with other medicines from which you cauterize a boil like this, with honey, acacia, salt with soap, all these things mixed together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	 Galen tells us of a cure by which a nobleman was cured of the pain in his leg and sciatica, and he praised it highly, saying that no other cure was made for it, and that it was cured once when this cure was made, and he was bathed as he instructs below.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie;	 And he says in this way that you take the fresh and dry green litharge powder, grind it very well with a bit of fat, and put it on the wound (sores) and on the thigh and on the leg where there is pain, and hold it there.
et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	 And let it stay for three hours and in the quantity that the patient no longer feels the burning sensation.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	 And then make him enter the bath until his body is slightly warmed up, and let him lie in it, and the pain will leave completely and he will be cured.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	 Know that no one should use such fire cautery medicine unless after the evacuation of the body.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout;	 And Dioscorides says that when the sciatic vein is cauterized with goat horns, it helps a lot.
et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	 The cautery must be done in this way.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	 Take linen and beat it with old oil, and put it on the depression that is between the toe of the foot and the one called the foscile.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains;	 Take dry goat horns, heat them until they are charcoal, and put them on flax (linen), and leave it there until it becomes stained.
et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee;	 And fix again thus, and continue to do so until you think by feeling that it comes to the bone, and that the pain is stopped.
et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	 This method of cautery is called "cautery of goat.
de la dolor dou dos	Of the pain in the back
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, whether it be from falling or impact or too much evacuation, or like the effects of cold matter spreading, none of these symptoms call for cauteries, except in the case of cold matter infusion.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir;	 Afterwards, it is necessary that the patient is emptied of putrid pills or similar, which are made on the back, where the pain is, three lines marked with incisions, and in each line V cauteries or more according to the strength and quantity that the patient can tolerate.
et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»;	 and the cautery should be done according to the cautery called "point.
et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	 If you see, make III or IV cauteries at the intermediate cautery in this form:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor;	 Often this disease comes to small children, and the signs of its beginning are that they have narrow anus when they strain, and fear.
et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	 and you find it in the lower spine of the back and in its appearance which comes above the other spines.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this and wish to cure it, cauterize it with the cautery of this shape.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	 The cautery increases each part of the spine.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	 And if you see, cauterize around the spine with the cautery pointed at intervals of 2 or 3 lines and let the points be close to each other.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	 After healing the joint when it is healed according to what we have said, ensure that you do not apply caution in a sciatica state that is in the nerve.
de la dolor des jointes	"of the pain of the joints"
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere:	 When joint pain is due to moisture that affects all members of the body, and when pain comes in the feet, which are called "gout" properly, and when it is caused by cold and cures with medicines cannot be cured, it is cured by cauteries in this manner:
fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	 make a mold for the cautery around the joint of the foot, and let the cautery be olive-shaped according to this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	 And if it is necessary to prick on the thigh, let it be cauterized all over with the cautery called "point".
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire;	 And if the pains come up to the knees and other joints, which happens often, make fire cautery on each knee three or four times on each side, using all olive oil.
et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	 and if you need more, do more, but don't hold your hand beyond the burnt part.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	 And if the pains descend to the genitals and back, administer the fire cautery as we have said in its chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes;	 And if the pains are in the hands, make incisions around the wrist two lines deep.
et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main;	 and if there remains a point of pain in the elbows, make incisions above each joint and on the hair of the hand.
et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	 And if the pains come up to the ribs or shoulders, cauterize each part and take good care of the patient, considering the medications.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	 For if you take good care of him and purge the fever, he will be healed with God's help.
de la routure dou syfac	of the breaking of the nose
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor;	 When rot begins in wounds, and the bowels descend into the joints and it is newly formed, then, when you see it to be cured, it should not eat that day;
et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre;	 and use things that relax the stomach, so that the bile descends from the stomach;
aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors;	 after doing so, make him sit on his back between your hands, and command him to bear down on his anus until the bowels are repaired, and then remove them to your sides, and press under the wound on the bone of the fist, and at every sign that is similar to half a circle above the chest;
puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	 then heat the iron in the form as follows:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	 as long as it is white and it exudes pus.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu;	 Then pull out the bowels to their place;
et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier;	 And the minister presses his hand so that it does not return.
et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains;	 Work the thighs well on the patient, and put the cushion and the sergeant beneath him on the thighs, and another one to hold his hands.
puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os;	 Then put the cautery on the spot with your whole hand, hold it straight and keep holding until you reach the bone; if you do not reach it the first time, try again until you reach the bone.
et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere;	 And be careful that the boil does not burst when you are doing the cautery.
que tu ne le brulasses;	 do not burn it.
et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	 and so that the patient may not die or suffer harm.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	 And know that when you do not reach the bone with the cautery, your work is worth nothing.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure;	 The cauteries for children should be subtle according to their size, and those for large people should be as big as them.
aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	 After three days, treat the shoulder with the boar's fat until the burn is healed.
aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee;	 Treat with other remedies until it is healed, and have the patient lie on his back for 40 days, so that the wound heals well.
et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	 And it is necessary to let his excrement be delayed for a long time, so that the boils do not protrude when he gets up to go to the rooms.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors;	 And after forty days, when he wants to get up, bring him a well-made sheet and keep it for 40 other days.
et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire;	 Let him have rest, so that he works little and is careful not to overfill himself with drink or food, and not to laugh too much.
et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	 And when he performs this teaching, he becomes completely healthy.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	 And I shall tell you next about the treatment of amputation in its chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	of the wound from the belly
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur;	 If roundworms appear in other wombs and are known, and you see that they do not grow anymore, then you should perform the cautery of the cautery according to their quantity, and burn the third part of it.
aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit;	 after the treatment as we have said.
et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	 and none of the old ones have said that it should be cauterized at the three-cornered cautery in this shape:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	 but first mark the place of entry and make a line above the worm, and another below, and then press your hand on the whole three-angled cautery.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	 But the first cauteries are lighter and more movable.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	of old pain in any limb
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	 When pain comes in any limb, either from falling or being hurt, and this pain lasts a long time, and the medicine cures do not help, then it should be cauterized with the cautery called "poins", and the cautery should be according to the length of the limb, its smallness and weakness, and its virtue and location for twisting and its pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien;	 if he is healthy after the first cautery, it is good;
se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	 if that part, repeats the other cautery on it, because custom is that it should change to the member that is nearby, so you must do the cauterizations as many times as the patient is getting healthy.
de meselerie	To mix (or compound) medicine
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	 These illnesses are sometimes helped by cautery with great effort, and especially the diseases that come from the corruption of phlegm and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief:	 Can you see the patient to perform a fire cauterization, take care if the patient is at the beginning of the illness, and if it has been cured according to what we have said in the division, and he neither sinks nor remains; if you doubt that corruption may affect the entire patient, then perform V cauterization on the head.
I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous;	 I hold the head to me and the other towards the forehead at the end of the hairs.
et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel;	 And (I) on (them) over the two horns, and (he) behind the nape.
et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir;	 And leave your hand thus that the cautery reaches the bone, and so that the bark comes out of it so that the vapors of the large humors can escape.
et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	 And apply the fire cautery on the swelling, as described earlier.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse;	 If the measles have spread everywhere;
et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules;	 And it loses [the dislocation] clearly, so you must burn with these cauteries that we have said on the head, and one cautery is the neck, and two cauteries on the spine of the neck, and six cauteries on the spine of the back, and one great one on the crotch and another small one, and two on the two shoulders;
et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains;	 And two on the hips, and two on the tendons of the thighs, and one on each joint of the hands and feet, and on the hollows of the hands;
et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler;	 And protect the nerves that are under the last bone, so you don't burn them;
et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	 And sometimes make one cautery on the bone of the handle, and one on the bone of the stomach, and one on the liver;
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite;	 And know that when you do more of the fire cautery, more aid is done, and it benefits them more;
et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	 And know that patients feel no pain from the cautery as the body is already completely corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	 The cautionery should be deep and shallow according to the members and joints, as you will find in ways of using irons.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	 After curing the shoulder with flour and honey, and other treatments until it is healed.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre;	 When a swelling appears in any member and is cured with medicine, oil, and plasters, but it is not healed, then cauteries are done on the member according to the size and smallness of the member;
et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur;	 and let the cautery be a slight incision in the flesh.
puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	 then heal it with ointments until it is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure;	 And sometimes they perform a cautery on the hand, foot, and back, at the nerve endings that paralyze the member, and in this way the swelling is removed.
et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	 And no one should interfere unless they are knowledgeable about members and the movements of the nerves guiding the body.
de albaras	From the linen cloth [or fabric]
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color;	 When the disease called "albaras" is developed, the instrument of medicine is of no use, therefore cauterize with a shallow cautery to the extent of the deep burn until the white spot is removed and its color changes.
puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie;	 Then cure with flour and lentils with rose oil and banana leaves, blood of the colon and blood of the almond, each in turn.
et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And mix all together, tie it up with a cloth, and apply to the place until it heals.
li cure de chancre par cautere	treating canker with cauterization
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	 When the boil starts and you see it begin to spread, if you want to stop it, you should cauterize with a fire cautery that resembles a circle around the boil.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre;	 And wisely, they would say that you perform a cautery also in the middle of the boil;
et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois;	 and it seems not good to me, for I believe it should not be ulcerated and corrupted, and I have often seen this happen.
et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	 and it is more proper that it be cauterized around, at the cautery called "circule", as we have said in our discussion on cauteries.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	of the swelling that cannot grow
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens;	 When someone has a disease called "adubelati", and it is slow to heal due to its excessive nature or due to the age of the patient when they are already weakened (meaning too old) and have little blood, or due to the time;
et tu la vues haster de meurer:	 And you see it hasten to measure:
adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant;	 Then cauterize it around with small hot needles by pricking.
aprés le laisse ensi.	 After that, let it be in this state.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	 It will heal.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you see it pierced entirely with the fire cautery, heat the cautery as shown here:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	 Place your hand in the middle of that disease called "adubelati" until the cauteries have pierced the core, and let the cauteries be such that the patient feels them outside in such a way that the course of the pus is made more evident.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	 After the cure until it is perfectly healthy.
li cure dou feu par fer	the treatment with fire by iron
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	 Another kind of disease is called "corrodens," and it is nothing other than the consumption of a limb, as it corrodes them as fire dries up wet things.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est;	 If you see this disease in a place that can endure cauterization along with fire, then heat the small and large needles accordingly according to where the disease is.
aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	 After that, cauterize everywhere until all the corruption is reached and there remains nothing of it, so that everything that is corrupt is removed.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	 And then leave it for three days, and apply soft soothing cauterized with oil on the wounds from fire and all corruption.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	 After the cure of onions producing charcoal.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin;	 And if after three days you see charred flesh not growing, it is good;
et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	 and if that does not happen, then cauterize again on the remaining corrupt parts.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu;	 And this wound has sometimes been healed with medicinal juice instead of fire cautery;
mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division:	 But nevertheless, fire cautery is of greater aid, and I have already said the treatment with medicinal juice in the section on treatment;
pren la quant tu en as mestier.	 take it when you need it.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	The coming pricks to the feet
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	 Very often a disease called "closed" (according to our understanding) arises from the feet, which is a large thing swollen that presses on the foot.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	 And the cauteries of this disease are according to two ways.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	 This is to know fire cautery and water hot cautery.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges;	 Heat the fire cautery in the same way as a feather from a goose is heated, and it should be made of good iron to the size that it can penetrate the nail completely, and that it has fine edges;
aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou;	 After putting it very hot on the nail, turn your hand all around the nail until it reaches the root of the nail;
et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture;	 and leave it in this way for three days until it begins to emit pus;
puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	 Then make a plaster of evil savage herbs crushed with oil, and leave the plaster on it all night, and the nail will shrivel and be uprooted from its roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then heal the shoulder with soothing salve until it is healed.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude;	 And if it has been converted by the outside of the body, and this happens in many cases, whether on limbs or feet, then you must apply a hot cautery.
et est en teil maniere:	 And it happens in this manner:
pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues;	 Take a cable of iron or wood, or a feather from the plume, and place it on the nail and the alcohol, that is to say, for treating warts.
et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine;	 place the cable around it so that it surrounds entirely, then put some hot oil on it and hold your hand well, press your hand while turning so that the edge of the cable comes to the base of the nail, and may find the hot oil deep enough to the root.
et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre;	 let the patient suffer a little bit of the hot oil bite for an hour;
puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	 then leave it like that, and it will fall off with all its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	 Thus, do after another, as long as you heat all those who are in the body, then cure them with ointments that soften flesh.
li cure dou trembler	The Cure for Shaking (or Trembling)
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee;	 When some tremble from cold or nerves, or from quartan fever or something else, it is necessary that you make four cauteries, or four on the spine of the back, one between each vertebra.
et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire;	 and the cautery for the genitals, and the olive oil cautery on the stomach.
si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	 let him tremble, and hasten the health from the cold disease.
des pustules puans	of putrid pustules (or boils)
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	 Sometimes on the outside of the body appear baths, or pustules rotten, which come from large corrupt matter.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule:	 it is necessary at first when they appear that a cautery be made over each head of the boil:
un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	 a subtle cautery made from the branch of the myrtle, so that it may be gripped by fire, or from the long root of arum lily, or to the lenticular cautery.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez;	 And sometimes they cauterize at the beginning when it appears in this way, and they cannot grow from then on, but the superfluous parts that come from it are broken off, and they heal.
mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	 but it must be done after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	When the artery is cut
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses;	 Often there are great hemorrhages from the artery that is cut at the wound which penetrates through, or in the incision of an abscess, or in the cautery of a limb, and similar things.
et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	 And it is a very bad thing to bleed internally.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus;	 Furthermore, when this happens to someone, hasten to place your finger on the wound of the vein, and hold it very tightly until the blood is stopped from flowing out beneath your finger, and no more blood comes.
puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge;	 Then place the olive oil cauteries, both small and large, until they are all red.
puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	 Then apply the hot cautery to the affected area, taking care to avoid large blood vessels, and hold the cautery in place until the flesh has been burned through.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement .i. autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	And if a jump occurs when you place your hand on the vein, and the fire cautery is extinguished, take immediately another cautery that is near the fire.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez;	 And continue with one procedure after another until the flesh is seared.
et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide;	 And ensure that you do not burn the nerve and that no further harm befalls the patient.
et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit:	 And understand that when the flesh separates from an artery, it cannot be properly cauterized if the artery is large, unless one of the four methods we have mentioned is used.
ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc;	 or by cautery, or by extraction when not treated, or by tightly binding with thread, or by medicines applied which have the power to stop blood.
et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	 and tied and constricted as necessary.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	Whoever brings about the constriction of a narrow ligature or placing hot things on it, or similar things, will not benefit if it does not help.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne;	 And if this happens without a mirror or medicine being present, then he should place his finger on the wound of the vein as we have said, and tighten it firmly until stopped above the wound and the vein.
et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez;	 and it must not be moved, but the wound should be often moistened with cold water frequently so that the wound becomes very cold, frozen, thickened, and stopped.
et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	 and make inquiries ahead about those who need cauterization and medicine.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	Here begins the second book of surgeries (or heals)
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres;	 We have told you in the first chapter about every disease in which fire cautery or hot medicine is needed, and the types of eyes [cauterized areas], their causes, instruments, shapes, and forms of the cauteries.
et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	 And I have placed that chapter up to the feet and will proceed in this chapter through the same path because it is easier to find what we are looking for.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	And so as I begin this, it is necessary, dear child, that you learn that in this chapter there is more danger and fear than in the first of the cauteries, and because of this, greater caution is required.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses;	 For in the work of this chapter, there is often the evacuation of blood when opening a vein, and incising an abscess, and in the treatment of wounds, and in the extraction of arrows, and in cutting into stones, and similar things.
ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	 Where there is doubt and fear, and many die.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	 And I warn you to not undertake folly.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	 For many ways of men come in treatment.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice;	 If those come who sicken themselves so much with their disease that they die quickly due to the fury that their illness brings, and the great severity of its malice;
et de ces doit on avoir paor.	 And one should fear such things.
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit:	 And of these you give your sense to someone, and say:
«atendez, je sui garis»;	 "Wait, I am cured";
et li maladie est despitouse.	 and the illness is spiteful.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los;	 You must not easily consent to those who come to you who have this manner, but put more trust in your honor than in your desire, and do not rashly believe but wisely of those from whom you are certain, and from which you can take and lose.
et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie;	 and use prognostication and indication in the treatment of your patients to lead salvation.
et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	 And this will help you to acquire good reputation, glory, and memory of praise.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	Dear child, Our Lords grant you good understanding and righteousness, and if you wish to inspire from the holy inspiration of His hand, come.
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	Moreover, I have ordered this chapter by dividing it into sections, according to that which is before the chapter of cauteries, which I have explained from head to feet, because you will find it easier to understand those matters from which you will need assistance.
dou chief plein d’aigue	The head full of water
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant;	 Know that this disease often comes to children during childbirth, and when the birth canal is too tight for the head of the child.
et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	 And sometimes it happens for reasons unknown.
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors;	 I have never seen this disease in anyone except children, and all those I have seen, death was swift.
et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	 And for that reason, it seems to me that I should devote myself less to these kinds of treatments.
Et je vis I enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir;	 And I saw a child whose head was full of water, and it grew larger every day until it could no longer support it.
et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os;	 And the moisture was so great that it caused his death, and this moisture is assembled beneath the bone near the cartilage.
et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large;	 And the operations are such that if there is moisture between the cartilage and the bone, and the abscesses are small, you make an incision across the top of a wide opening.
et soit ausi longe com II nous, tant que li mostor corre;	 And let it be as long as we can, until the moisture recedes.
et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	 Here is the shape of the spatula:
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai .ij. fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	If the moisture is more swollen, and the abscess is larger, make two cuts in the shape of a cross, according to this form:
Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut:	 If the moisture is beneath the bone, and you see the openings of the mouths on each side, and it has no response when you press it from within with your hand, then:
si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief III fendures selonc ceste maniere:	 You must make three incisions in the middle of the bone in this manner:
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	 And after the incision remove all the moisture.
Aprés estraint les fendures de drapelz et de poudres, et i met vin et oile, et laisse ensi jusc’a cinquieme jor;	 After straining the slits of linen cloths and powders, put vinegar and oil in it, and leave it so until the fifth day.
puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.	 Then loosen (it), and heal the wound with bandages and ointments, and let the head swell to a certain extent, and give the patient dry meat without moisture until the limb is comfortable and healed.
Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue;	 And another way of incising is to look at where the abscess swells the most, and where the water collects.
car aucune fois est elle devant;	 because sometimes it is in front;
aucune fois derrier;	 sometimes it is behind.
aucune fois en destre;	 sometimes on the right side;\]
et aucune fois en senestre.	 And sometimes on the left side.
Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir;	 Therefore, open the abscess or wound, drain the pus, and do what you can with it.
et warde que tu ne coper l’artere;	 And be careful not to cover the artery.
et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.	 If blood comes out, let it flow so that the patient dies from bleeding and evacuation of fluid.
de reume	of remedy
Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les .ij. arteres.	When it happens to someone with a disease called "catarrah" in the eyes or at its worst, and the disease is old, and medicine does not help, then the last cure is the cautery on the two arteries.
Il covient donques, cant tu les vues coper, que li malaides faice rere son chief;	 Therefore, when you see them covered, have the patient lay down on his back;
aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel;	 After that, rub the area with a rough cloth until the arteries appear, then grab the patient's neck with the cloth.
puis regarde ou li voine bait, et li leus de l’une et de l’autre sont aprés les oreilles, et poc sont reponues;	 Then look for the artery where it is visible, and the left and right ones are found behind the ears, and both will return.
puis signe les leus d’enche, puis cope l’une et l’autre d’un spatumile agut de II pars, tant que li taille veigne jusc’a l’os, et ceu soit par lou large dou chief.	 Then mark the joints with a sharp spatula of two parts, then strike one and the other until it reaches the bone, and this should be done through the wide part of the joint.
Et se tu vues, boute le spatumile desoz l’artere et la cope au desus, en taillant ausi com .ij. dois au traver.	And if you see it (the artery), push the sharp spatula under the artery and cut above it, cutting as you would through two.
Et quant li voinne est copee, si saut li sans en haut continuelment fuers.	And when the vein is cut, it jumps up without ceasing continuously.
Et se li artere n’apert au sentir, si covient que tu mesures la quantiteit de l’espaice de III dois, puis seigne d’enche et fent jusc’a l’os;	 And if the artery does not open upon feeling, you must measure the space of three fingers, then mark and strike until it reaches the bone.
et ceu qu’il covient dou sanc mettre fuers si est VI c/, et par aventure un poc plus ou moins, selonc ce que li malaides puet soffrir, et la repletion de l’artere;	 And it is necessary to force the blood out with a cupping glass of six centimeters, and perhaps a little more or less, according to what the patient can endure, and the filling of the artery.
puis regarde la plaie:	 Then look at the wound.
s’il remaint sus l’os point dou syphac, si le cope que apostemes chaus n’i veigne, puis estrain la plaie et lie, et la cure d’oignement tant qu’ele soit sanee.	 If the wound remains on the bone tip, if an abscess does not form, then hold the wound closed and bind it with a dressing until it heals.
de emigrainne	of emigration
Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	When an old emigration comes and acute catarrh arrives, due to the moisture of tears and the heat in the temples, and an old foolish person becomes senile with similar things; it is treated by methods of medicine, but it does not help at all. If the arteries in the temples are opened and cauterized, as we have mentioned, it will help.
Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit;	 And the manner of extracting them is that the patient pulls back the hairs on his temples, and listens for the artery that opens in the temple, because it opens well by beating, and it is slightly retracted outside except in some men who are too cold.
et s’elle est reponue, si estraigne son col li malaides d’aucuns drapelz, puis frote le leu d’aucun aspre drap, et arose le leu d’aigue chaude tant que li artere apere manifestement;	 and if it is retracted, the patient pulls his neck with some cloths, then rubs the area with harsh fabric, and strokes the area with warm water until the artery appears clearly.
puis pren le spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	 then take the spatula as shown in this form:
puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie;	 then gently peel the skin so that you see the artery, then draw it towards the prongs and separate well the threads that are underneath each part.
et se li artere est subtilz, si la torne a la pointe de l’uncine, puis la cope de celle partie selonc la quantiteit des II chiés.	 And if the artery is subtle, turn it to the point of the unguis (or nail), then strike that part according to the quantity of the two heads (shoulders).
Car s’elle n’est copee, si ne saut mie li sans dou tout en tout.	 If it is not cut (or punctured), it will not heal at all.
Et trai dou sanc des VI c/, jusc’a III;	 Draw blood from the VI c (vein) up to the III (cubital vein or median cubital vein).
et se li artere est grans, si covient que tu la lies en II leus d’un fil double fort de soie, que porriture n’i veigne devant le soudement de la plaie, et veigne decorremens de sanc;	 And if the artery is large, you should tie it with a strong double silk thread at two lengths, so that pus does not come out before the stitching of the wound, and there is a flow of blood.
puis cope la superfluiteit qui est entre les II liiens en celle houre meisme, et puis, se tu vues, si lou cauterize dou cautere cutellaire jusc’a l’os tant que li chiés soient copez;	 Then strike the excess between the two ligatures in that hour itself, and then, if you see, cauterize with the cautery knife up to the bone until the shoulder is severed.
et c’est li muedre oevre, se li malaides n’a fievre et il est de chaude complexion.	 This is the mature work, if the patient does not have a fever and has a hot constitution.
Car li cauteres est aide por finir les moistors:	 The cauteries are helpful to treat moisture (diseases):
por ceu est il de plus grant aide as moistors.	 for this is of greater aid against diseases (moistures).
Ou il covient por l’estraction des arteres que om emplisse lou leu de viel coton et mette on sus tentes bien faites;	 For the extraction of arteries, one should fill the area with old cotton and place it on well-made tents.
et quant on les desliera, si soit curez de medicines seches que font naistre char, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez;	 and when they are separated (the arteries), you should cure them with dry medicines that cause healing, and tents until it heals.
et se sans cort de l’artere tant dis com tu i oevres, si te haste dou coper par cautere, ou tu emple lou leu de vitriole et l’estrain a ta main que li sans soit estainchiez;	 If you do not perform the operation on the artery as instructed, hasten to cover it with cautery or apply vitriol and hold your hand over it so that it stops bleeding.
et se tu n’as ceu present, si met sor le leu ton doit tant que li sans soit congelez, et arose le leu d’aigue froide tant que li sans cesse, et soit estraint si com il covient;	 If you do not have that (the cautery or vitriol), place your hand on the area until it freezes, and rub the area with cold water continuously, and hold as necessary.
et ceu qui est muedre et plus legier en l’estraction de l’artere est que tu cauterizes la voinne de cest cautere trenchant de II pars, mais li trenchant soient bien espés por warder plus longement lor chalor.	 And the one who is moving and lighter during the extraction of the artery should be cauterized with this cautery cutting through it in two parts, but they should be well thick for holding the heat longer.
Car quant li estrumens est trop tenves, si tient moins sa chalor.	When the thermometer is too thin, it retains less heat.
Et doit avoir entre les II coutelz I doit de gros d’espaice, et puis quant tu as signiet d’enche les II leus, et tu mes lou fer ardant sus tant qu’il viegne jusc’a l’os, et cope la voinne en II leus;	 And between the two blades it should have a thick gap, and when you have positioned them properly in the two places, and the iron is heated hot enough to reach the bone, then strike the vein in the two places.
et soient esloigniet entre les II chiés car il n’est mie soudez de cest cautere dou tout en tout;	 And they should be separated between the two heads because it is not welded all over by this cautery.
et c’est li forme dou cautere:	 and this is the form of the cautery:
des larmes	tears
Quant les larmes des eulz sont dessendans des voinnes que sont sus lou test dou chief de fuer, et il ne profite mie cure de medicine c’on i faice, et tu vois la faice dou malaide enrougir, et sent ou front ambulation si com de fremis;	 When the tears from the eyes are running down the veins that are on top of the head of fire, and medicine cure does not help for it, and you see the patient writhing in pain, and feel his forehead to be cold like shivering.
et sui oil sont tenve et moiste si que li poil des papieres sont cheut, et sont eschaufees les papieres, et escorchies de l’ardor des larmes, si ait mestier de ceste cure.	 And if the eyes are soft and moist so that the eyelashes fall out, and the eyelids are scalded and burned by tears, this remedy is needed.
Et l’apelerent li ancien «cure contuse», et est que tu faices a rere au malaide qui a ceste maladie les poilz qu’il ait ou front, puis li fai III fendures ou front igalment selonc la longesce dou front;	 And it was called by the ancients "contused cure", and you must do this to the patient who has this disease: shave the hair from the forehead, then make three equal incisions in the forehead according to its length.
et soit l’une des fendures ausi com II doi tout emmi lou front en avalant aval jusc’a neif, et les autres II as II costelz par desus les papieres, et te garde de l’incision des arteres que sont as II costez par desus les papieres;	 And one of the incisions should be as deep as necessary along the forehead from top to bottom, and the other two shall be along the eyebrows, but take care not to cut the arteries that are on the sides above the eyelids.
et aloigne ta main de la continuation des II mandibules, et soit chescune plaie la quantiteit de III dois au traver joins;	 And remove your hand from the junction of the two jaws, and let each wound be the length of three fingers joined together.
et aies apparillie une piece d’esponge et mout de drapelz ses por essuer lou sanc, puis boute le spatumile agut de II pars de coi ci est li forme:	 And prepare a piece of sponge and a lot of cloth for wiping the blood, then insert the sharp spatula of about two fingers as shown here:
des l’incision qui est dever la temple jusc’a la seconde incision;	 From the incision which is from the temple until the second incision;
et escorche tout le keur qui est entre les II fendures a tot lou syfac qui est sus l’os, puis fai autreteil des la moiene incision jusc’a l’autre seconde, et puis estrai fuer cest spatumile.	 And scrape the whole core which is between the two incisions all along the bone, then do the other side from the mid-incision to the other second one, and then pull out this splinter.
si boute en la premiere fendure l’estrument qui est apelez «cultellaire», et est tresbien trenchans d’une part, et d’autre part est souef, ne mie trenchans, et c’est li forme:	Insert the instrument called "cultellaire" in the first incision; it is well sharpened on one side, and on the other side it is soft, not sharp, and it has this shape:
Et met le costeit taillant vers la char aerse au keur, et lou costeit souef vers l’os, et lou boute tant qu’il veigne a la moiene fendure.	 And cut the bone towards the flesh at the chosen spot, and the bone becomes soft towards the bone, and push it until it comes to the mid-split.
Et cope toz les vasselz que dessendent dou chief as eulz tant que l’incision soit continue jusc’a ceu qui apert dou keur, et puis autreteil fai en la moiene fendure jusc’a l’autre defuer;	 And cut all the veins that descend from the head towards the eyes as long as the incision is continuous until it opens the core, and then do the other side in the middle fissure up to the other side.
