et puis estrai dou sanc igalment, et espresse lou leu por le sanc pris;	 And then drain the blood evenly, and press the place for the blood taken;
puis met en chescune fendure une tente de viel coton, et met sus drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile et en aisil, et garde que apostemes chaus n’i veigne;	 and put in each fissure a tent of old cotton, and place damp linen cloths soaked in vinegar and oil and ashes on top, and ensure that no pus comes.
et au tier jor deslie lou liien, et i amenistre grant planteit d’aigue tede, puis lou cure d’oignement basilicon avec oile roset, et d’autres cures dont on cure plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And on the third day separate the ligament, and apply a large poultice of cold water, then the healing ointment of basilicon with rose oil, and other treatments for wounds until it heals.
dou reume des eulz	The root of the hairs
Quant a aucun vienent catarre agut acostumeement, et tu vois les eulz tenves et petis, et afoiblir la veue, et les papieres brulees;	 When an acute catarrh comes, you usually see the eyes become thin and small, and weakened vision, and burnt paper.
et li poil chieent, et ou chief en parfont a dolor ague, et li malaides esternue;	 And the hair falls out, and they make holes in the head with pain, and the patients cough.
adonques saiches par ces accidens que celles matieres et cil catharre ne vient fuer que de maintes voines, et li muedre cure que i est, si est ceste.	 Therefore, you understand from these signs that those matters and this catarrh come only through many veins, and the medicine to cure it is this.
Et est que tu comande au malaide a rere son front, puis fai une grant fendure emmi lou front, et une autre dou large I poc.	 And you command the patient to bend his head back, then make a deep cut along the forehead and another wide one at the temples.
Et comence des la fendure de la temple senestre a la temple destre, et soit li incision jusc’a l’os;	 And start from the hollow of the left temple to the right temple, and make the incision up to the bone;
et esloigne ta main des ners des temples que muevent au mengier;	 And move your hand away from the nerves of the temples that move while eating;
et quant li os est descovers, si essue tout le sanc a une esponge, et puis desevre entre les II levres de la fendure et i met coton viel, et tentes de lin;	 When the bone is exposed, squeeze all the blood onto a sponge, then force it apart between the two lips of the fracture and put old cotton in there, and bind with linen.
puis lie desus drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile, et te garde d’aposteme chaut;	 then cover with damp cloths soaked in wine and oil, and guard against hot abscesses.
quant il est ostez, si covient que tu frottes l’os tant que chars i comence a naistre, puis le cure de choses exiccatives, que font enjanrer char.	 When it is removed (the bone), you must rub the bone until char becomes visible, then treat with things that are drying, which promote the formation of scab.
En teil maniere:	 In this manner:
pren II parties de flor de froment, et de colofoine IIII parties, et en fai emplaustre;	 Take two parts of wheat flower and four parts of colophony, and make an ointment.
et l’aministre en ces plaies por enjanrer char per tout.	 And administer linen cloth for dressing all wounds.
de l’estoupement des oreilles	of the earstopping
Tout ceu que chiet ens oreilles est une des IIII choses:	 Everything that falls into the ears is one of the Four Things:
ou grains, ou beste, ou piere de mine ou semblans chose si com fer;	 or grains, or beast, or stone from a mine, or similar things like iron.
ou semence, si com jaisses, feves, pois;	 or seeds such as lentils, beans, peas.
ou chose defluans si com aigue et aisilz et semblans choses.	 or flowing things like water and syrups and similar things.
Quant il chiet en l’oreille piere ou autre maniere de chose que ne s’ajoste mie a l’oreille, ne ne croist en l’oreille, si met l’oreille au solel.	 When it falls into the ear, stone or otherwise, if it does not fit in the ear or does not grow within the ear, place the ear on the sun.
Se tu vois la piere, si distille aucun poc d’oile violet ou oile de sisament, puis i amenistre extraction;	 If you see a stone, apply a little purple oil or camphor oil, then administer extraction.
et lou fai esternuer de condisi, et li estoupe les narines quant li esternuemens vient, et met entor l’oreille pieces de drapelz ou laine;	 and make him vomit with mustard, and stop the nostrils when vomiting occurs, and place around the ear cloth or wool.
et estent l’oreille au desus.	 stretch the ear upward.
Mout de fois vient fuer par ceste cure;	 Much often comes fever by this cure;
et s’elle ne vient fuer, se li amenistre extraction as pinceures subtilz, de coi ci est li forme:	 and if it does not come fever, let it be administered the extraction of leeches, as follows:
S’elle saut fuer as pinceures, c’est boin;	 If it jumps to leeches, that is good;
se ceu non, si amenistre extraction a l’oncine subtil de petite doubleure;	 if not, let it be administered the extraction of the onion juice in small doses;
et s’elle ne saut par ceu, si fai une caine d’arain et boute lou chief de la cainne ou pertuis de l’oreille fort, et estoupe ceu qui est entor la cainne de cire mole si que li vens n’i puisse entrer avec la cainne;	 and if not, make a candle of beeswax and press the head of the candle or ear tube firmly, and stop up that which is around the candle with soft wax so that the vein cannot enter it with the candle.
puis le trai fuer forment, car mout de fois vient fuer si com nos avons dit;	 then draw it out carefully, for much often comes fever as we have said;
et s’elle ne vient fuer en teil maniere, si prent glut de coi en prent les oisiaus, et met en som aucun estrument qui soit a point por ceu faire, et met un poc de coton entor;	 and if it does not come fever in this way, take glue from the source and take birds, put them in any device that is sharp for this purpose, and put a piece of cotton around it.
puis presse le glut sus la piere ou quel chose que ce soit, et trai fuer.	 Then press the glute (buttock) on the bone or something, and draw it out (pull hard).
Et s’elle ne saut fuer de toutes ces choses que nos avons dit, si te haste de fendre l’oreille ainsois que aposteme chalz i veigne, et spasme;	 If it does not pop out from all the things we mentioned, then quickly cut (make a small incision) in the ear so that pus comes out and there is a spasm.
et li maniere de la fendure si est que tu faices premier sainier lou malaide de la cephalique, et estrai dou sanc selonc la mesure de sa vertu, puis fai seoir lou malaide entre tes mains et li torne l’oreille au desus, et fent une petite fendure en la racine de l’oreille a la graisse ou leu dependant;	 And the method of the incision is that you first make the patient drain the skull, remove blood according to the strength of its power, then sit the patient between your hands and turn the ear upside down, and make a small incision in the root of the ear where the fat or flesh hangs.
et soit li fendure ausi com une lune, tant que tu viegnes a la piere, puis l’oste selonc ton pooir, et la suce hastanment a ta bouche;	 And the incision should be like a crescent moon, reaching the bone, then remove (extract) the bone as strong as you can and suck out the pus quickly with your mouth.
et la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And the treatment until it heals.
Et se c’est grains qui est ens et il enfle, si aministre extraction;	 If it is swollen with grains (possibly boils), administer extraction;
et si’il ne puet issir, si amenistre I spatumile tenve subtil selonc ceste forme:	 and if it cannot issue, administer the thin, subtle sponge according to this form:
et amenistre incision de celui grain.	 and make an incision of that grain.
Mais ne faire mie ceu quant tu penses que li grains est moistes por la moistor de l’oreille, tant que tu en aies fait maintes pieces;	 But do not do that if you think the grains are moist from ear moisture, as long as you have made several pieces;
puis l’estrai as pinceures subtilz et au succier, si com nos avons dit, si que li estractions soit aligie.	 Then extract with subtle tweezers and the sucker, as we have said, to ensure proper extraction.
En l’aigue donques que chiet en l’oreille covient que li malaides use d’esternuement de condisi premiers, et ample l’oreille de viel coton.	 Therefore in case of water that falls into the ear, the patient should use earwax drops first and stuff the ear with a large cotton ball.
Et soit gisans sus celle oreille meisme ou li aigue est.	 And let it lie on the same ear where the water is.
s’elle saut fuer per ceu, c’est boin.	 If it jumps out due to this, that's good.
se ceu non, si prent maintes pieres selonc li longesce de ton doit tenves et legieres, et les eschaufe un poc au feu;	 If that does not work, take many small and slender stones according to the length of your finger, heat them slightly in the fire;
et em mette li malaides une ou pertus de son oreille, et saille sus i. de ses piez d’autre part, et fiere d’une autre piere sus la piere qui est en l’oreille;	 and make the patient place one or a pierced ear on it, and press from below with his feet, and strike another stone on the stone in the ear.
et ne cesse de faire ceu de piere em piere tant que li aigue isse toute fuer, et ensi saut elle toute fuer;	 And it does not stop making them pierce one stone after another until the fire goes out completely, and thus it leaps out completely.
et se tu vues, si prent I jonc, et boute l’un des chiés en l’oreille, et l’autre chief emprent de feu tant que li plus dou jonc soit ars;	 And if you see it, grab the cord and push one of the shoulders into the ear, and take hold of the other head with fire until the more distant joint is burned.
puis refai autreteil d’autres jons tant que li aigue isse toute, si com nos avons dit en la piere.	 Then make the same procedure for the other joints until the fire goes out completely, as we have said in the previous section.
En l’estraction de la beste, s’elle est de petit cors, si com puce et semblans chose, cure la si com nos avons dit en la division;	 In the extraction of an animal with a small body, such as a flea and similar creatures, treat it as we have said in the classification.
mais s’elle est de grant cors c’on la puisse sentir, si amenistre extraction de pinceures;	 but if it has a large body that can be felt, bring the forceps extraction;
et c’est li chose plus legiere a oster qui soit en l’oreille.	 And it is easier to remove what is in the ear than what is on the body of the animal.
En l’estraction des vers enjanrez as oreilles, quant tu lou cures si com nos avons dit en la division et ou traitier des distillations, et li cure ne profite mie, si covient que tu regardes l’oreille au soleil:	 In the extraction of worms in the ears, when you care for it as we have said in the section and in treating distillations, and the patient does not improve; if this happens, you must observe the ear under the sun.
s’il i apert nulz vers, si les trai as pinceures subtilz, et s’il n’aperent, si prent la cainne de coi ci est li forme:	 If worms appear, take them with fine tweezers, and if they do not appear, take the cane that has the following shape:
Et soit estroite desoz et large desus.	 And narrow below and wide above.
Et boute lou plus subtil chief en l’oreille selonc la quantiteit de la soffrance dou malaide, puis succe forment a tot la caine;	 And insert the more subtle tip into the ear according to the quantity of pain in the patient, then move it completely along the cane.
fai ceu sovent tant que tuit li ver issent.	 Perform this often until all the worms come out.
Et s’il n’obeissent a issir, si estoupe entor la cainne de coton si com j’ai dit en la piere;	 And if they do not obey and come out, stuff the cane with cotton as I said in the previous section.
et s’il ne saillent fuer si com nos avons dit, si aministre distillations que li ancien ont esprovees en l’ocision des vers, et tu les troveras ou traitier des distillations;	 And if they do not protrude as we have said, administer distillations that the ancient ones have proven in the treatment of worms, and you will find them or treat with distillations.
et si distille tes oiles et tes medicines en l’oreille a tout cest estrument, de coi ci est li forme si com tu vois:	 And if you distil oil and medicine into the ear in this manner, here is the form as you see:
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain estrois desoz a I petis pertuis, et desus overs por distiller;	 Let it be made of silver or tin narrowly placed under the small openings, and covered above for distillation.
et por presser dedens la distillation a I estrument d’arain bien fait por ceu, et se tu vues pren I raseur et envoloupe entor la pointe avenanment coton;	 And to press within the distillation apparatus of tin well made for this purpose, and if you see take a razor and wrap it around the tip with cotton.
puis i giete ton oile ou ton jus, et ceu que tu vues de tes medicines en la cainne, et li caine soit en l’oreille;	 Then pour in your oil or juice, and whatever medicine you wish into the cane, and the cane should be in the ear.
puis boute dedens lou raseur a tout lou coton, et presse ta main tempreement tant que li oile soit distilleit ou chevement de l’oreille;	 Then push inside the strainer with all the cotton, and press your hand moderately until the oil is distilled or the ear's opening enlarges.
et lou sente li malaides dedens, et soit li distillations I poc eschaufee au feu ainsois c’on la distille en l’oreille;	 and feel the patient's senses inside, and heat the distillation container near the fire so that it is heated in the ear.
et garde qu’elle ne soit trop froide, car li medicine ne seroit mie si bone.	 and make sure it is not too cold, for the medicine would not be as good.
de l’estoupement des oreilles	of the earstopping
Aucun enfant naissent qui n’ont nul pertus ens oreilles;	 No child is born without some birthmark in the ear.
et ceste meisme chose avient as homes par estoupement de plaie, ou de char nee dedens l’oreille, et cist estoupemens vient aucune fois em parfont en l’oreille, si c’on ne lou puet veoir;	 And the same thing happens in men by ear wound or pus discharge from within the ear, and this discharge sometimes completely fills the ear, if it cannot be seen.
et aucune fois avient I poc defuer lou pertus, et lou voit om bien.	 And sometimes the birthmark disappears, and it can be clearly seen.
Celle donques que vient em parfont, si c’on ne la puet veoir, est de grief sanation em plusors dispositions, et en cele c’on voit covient que tu mettes l’oreille dou malaide au soleil;	 Therefore, when it comes from the font (source), if one cannot see it, is a grave healing in many situations, and in such cases, you must place the patient's ear towards the sun.
et regarde dedens:	 and look within:
se tu vois l’opilation apparent, si la oevre a tot cest spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	 if you see the abscess appearing, work with this spatula of which form is as follows:
Et soit agus et trenchans devant et derrier tout plain, si qu’il ne blece l’oreille;	 And be sharp and pointed both front and back, so that it does not pierce the ear.
se li opilation est de char nee ou cors de l’oreille, si la tien as pinceures subtilz, et la cope legierement, tant que celle chars soit toute ostee.	 if the abscess is of flesh or bone from the ear, hold it with subtle forceps and strike gently until all the flesh is removed.
Et se li opilations est em parfont en l’oreille, si pren I raseur subtil legier et l’eschaufe un petit au feu, puis li met ou cors de l’oreille.	 And if the swellings are entirely in the ear, take a fine razor lightly and heat it slightly with fire, then place it in the ear canal.
Se tu sens l’opilation dont li malaides sent grieteit a l’oïr, perce legierement, et garde que tu ne grever les ners de l’oreille;	 If you feel the abscess from which the patient feels pain in the ear, pierce gently and ensure that you do not harm the nerves of the ear.
puis met en l’oreille une tente selonc la largesce dou pertus, et la moille en l’oignement egyptien.	 Then put a plaster of suitable size in the ear according to the wound's width, and apply the Egyptian ointment to it.
Fai ceu aucun jor tant que li plaie soit soudee, ou tu pren une tente et la moille en aigue rose, et poudre sus vitriole broiet;	 Every day until the wound is healed, take a plaster and apply it with rose water, and powdered crushed glass on top.
et se tu vois enflee l’oreille, si couvient que tu traies la tente et remue une autre tente moillie en cerote qui soit fait d’oile roset et de cire, tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	 And if you see the ear swell, it is necessary that you remove the plaster and apply another damp cloth made of rose oil and wax until the swelling disappears.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then heal it until it is healed.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si plonge une esponge et drapelz en aigue froide, et le met sus l’oreille, et use d’autres cures qui oste lou decorrement de sanc qui sont ou traitier des destillations.	If there is a flow of pus, immerse a sponge and cloth in cold water, place it on the ear, and apply other treatments to remove the flow of pus which are either distillation methods.
de la char des papieres	of the wood from paper
Cist althelul que vienent em papieres des eulz quant ils sont moiste et sont sec, si covient que tu les estendes de tenailles et de pinceures, et le cope d’un spatumile de ses racines;	 This is the method that comes on paper when the hairs are moist and dry. It is necessary that you stretch them with tweezers and forceps, and cut off their roots with a spatula.
puis met sor le leu vitriole broiet.	 Then put vitriol powder on its place.
Et se sans en decort, si le cauterize dou cautere lenticulaire subtil, et li cauterizeir aprés l’incision vaut mues;	 If not scabbed over, then cauterize with the subtle lenticular cautery and after incision is beneficial;
et maintes fois repairent, cant aucune chose demoure de lor racines;	 And many times they recur, where nothing remains rooted from them. (in context of dislocated limbs or shoulders)
et quant elles sont cauterizees par feu, si sont arses celles racines et ne revienent mie.	 and when they are burnt with fire, the roots are burned away and they do not return. (in context of cauterizing)
de la gresle	of the hailstone
Maintes fois vienent em papieres des eulz unes choses que semblent gresle en sa forme et en sa duresce, et por ceu est ceste maladie apelee «grandine», et est une assemblee de moistor grosse en la papiere desus et desoz;	 Many times they come in the form of gravel, appearing hard and solid, for which this disease is called "hail", and it is an accumulation of thick moisture in the paper above and below. (this appears to refer to a skin condition or infection)
li ovraiges est telz:	 The operations are as follows: (beginning a list of medical procedures, possibly related to the previous sentences about dislocations, cauterizing, and hail-like lesions)
pren warde se li grandine se muet d’une part et d’autre, et c’est legiere chose a savoir;	 Take care to let the "hail" disappear on both sides, and this is an easy thing to know. (still in the context of skin lesions/infections)
fent la donques dou large, puis l’escorche de chescune partie legierement, puis la prent as pinceures, et la cope.	 Cut (it) open then widely, next scrape gently from each part, then take with the forceps and crush it.
se tu ne la pues coper sens percier un poc la papiere, si ne grieve rien au malaide;	 if you cannot cover it without piercing a little the paper, do not worry the patient.
et se li fendure est grans, si l’assemble a une costure, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee;	 and if the wound is large, join it with a stitch, and treat it until it heals.
et s’elle est petite, si n’i faire point de force, car li oignemens la restoure tantost et enjanre char.	 and if it is small, do not apply any pressure, because the ointments restore it soon and improve the flesh.
Et se li grandine est dessendans au dedens de l’oreille vers la partie desus, si enverse la papiere, et estent la grandine a unes pinceures, et la cope et presse d’une part et d’autre;	 And if the pus is descending inside the ear towards the upper part, turn the paper and extract the pus with forceps, and press it from both sides.
et se li papiere est esloignie par l’incision, ce ne grieve rien;	 and if the paper is moved by incision, do not worry.
et quant li grandine est copee, si leive l’oil d’aigue salee, et cure le leu de ceu qui enjanre char tant que li malaides soit sanez.	 And when hail is struck, apply oil of salty water to it and heal the wound of those who are injured by it until the patient recovers.
de la graisse des eulz	of the fat of the hairs
Exinach est une graisse qui est enjanree en toiles des papieres desus, et ce avient plus as enfans c’a nules gens, et grieve mout a lor eulz, et li vienent li catharre as matinees, et ne pueent regardeir la lumiere dou soleil por ceu que les larmes se hastent a lor eulz;	 Exinach is a grease that is rendered in paper towels above and it happens more with children than with adults, and it causes great pain to their eyes, and they come down with catarrh in the mornings and cannot bear the light of the sun because tears hasten to their eyes.
et por ceu se couchent il sor lor faices adés, et dorment sus, et sont lor papieres desoz lor sorcilz moistes que li enfleure et li apparance ont covert de l’exinach qui apert en l’oil.	 And because of this they lie on their faces right away and sleep on them, and their papers are beneath their eyelids moistened with exinach which spreads in the oil.
Et quant tu presses lou leu a tes dois et sent l’exirnach entr’ous.	 And when you press the joint with your hands and feel the dislocation emerging between them.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain;	 And the manner of work is that the patient holds their head on your hand;
et puis pren I drapeil de lin, et appareille une tente em maniere d’un cercle selonc la quantiteit que conteigne exirnach de chescune partie, puis le met sus li;	 Then take a linen cloth, and prepare a tent in the shape of a circle according to the size required by each part (Exirnach), then place it over him;
et presse a tes dois d’une part et d’autre, si que li exirnach soit assemblez emmi le cercle;	 and press with your arms from both sides so that the Exirnach (a surgical instrument) is assembled within the circle;
puis fent em mileu de la moistor au spatumile trenchant une fendure dou large, et ne soit mie plus grans que li plaie c’on fait a la sainie de voinne;	 then make an incision in the middle of the Exirnach with the moistor (spatula-like tool) cutting a slit wide enough, but not larger than the wound made for vein opening;
et fent le cuir em parfont tant que tu veignes a l’exirnach;	 and cut the skin all the way through to expose the Exirnach;
et em plusors dispositions vient exirnach de la fendure, selonc la forme d’une piece de graisse blainche.	 And in many positions, an extrusion comes out from the wound, according to the shape of a piece of white fat.
Estrai la donques a tout une piece de drap charpit entre tes dois au defuer, et torne ta main a destre et a senestre tant qu’il soit espars;	 Place then a piece of rough cloth between your hands at the wound and turn your hand to the right and left until it is spread.
et garde que tu n’ajoster en la fendure, que tu ne viegnes a tout le spatumile jusc’a l’oil, que tu ne le bleces.	 And ensure that you do not insert anything into the wound, nor come all the way to the fatty tissue, nor prick it.
Et se li exirnach n’apert en l’encomencement de la fendure, si acroi un poc la fendure legierement tant qu’il apere;	 If the extrusion does not open at the beginning of the wound, lift up the wound slightly to make it appear.
puis l’estrai si com nos avons dit, puis moille drapelz en aisil et en aigue, et met sus le leu, et estrain de bendelz.	 Then pull out as we have said, then wet cloths in oil and water and place on it, and press down with bandages.
Et si a de tels homes qui broient seil et mettent sus por corrompre cele moistor qui est demoree.	 And for such people who grind salt and put it on to corrupt the moisture that remains.
Puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then heal him until he is healthy.
Et s’il vient au leu aposteme chaut, si lou cure d’emplaustres assouajant tant qu’il soit sanez.	 If an abscess forms at the joint, then heal it with plasters softening it until he is healthy.
des poilz des papieres	hair of the papyrus (meaning: plants or fibers resembling hair)
Quant em papieres naissent poilz ajostez autre que li naturez, et sont enveillit, si nuisent as eulz, et font venir manieres de maladies si com larmes acostumees et mollifications des papieres et albugine, tant que c’est cause de la destruction des eulz;	 When paper-like growths appear on the eyelashes and are nourished, they harm the eyes and bring about types of diseases such as constant tearing and swelling of the eyelids, up until this is the cause of the destruction of the eyes.
et est li cure selonc IIII manieres:	 and the cure follows according to four methods:
ou par cautere ensamble feu, ou par medicine ague selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre de cautere, et est fais ou par incision et costure ou par caines, selonc ceu que je dirai.	 or by a cautery combined with fire, or by medicine hot according to what is before in the chapter on cautery, and it is done either by cutting and stitching or by blisters, as I shall say.
Il covient que tu mettes lou chief dou malaide en ton sain, puis torne la papiere de l’oil a ta main senestre;	 You must place the head of the patient in your lap, then turn the paper from the oil to your left hand.
s’elle est convertie, c’est boin;	 if it is turned over, that's good.
se ceu non, si i boute une aguille a tout I fil desus;	 If not, push an awl through the hole above [it].
et soit ce delez la marge de la papiere ou li poil naissent delez ces poilz, et trai I fil au desus a tout la papiere, et la torne au raseur;	 and shave the edge of the paper where the hairs grow from the hairs, pull the thread to the top of the paper, and smooth it with a razor.
puis fent en la partie desoz la papiere, desoz les poilz ajostez, a tout le spatumile copant, des le grant larmier jusc’au petit;	 then make a groove in the part underneath the paper, under the hairs, along the entire space, from the large incision to the small one.
puis estrai I fil, et met desoz la papiere une petite tente de couton et de drapeil, puis seigne sus la papiere une figure d’enche, si com la fuelle de mirte, et toutevoie il covient que li figure soit selonc la quantiteit que tu vues eslever la papiere qui est devisez a toz.	 then pull the thread and place a small tent of cloth and linen underneath the paper, then draw a design on the paper of a hook, like the briar rose, but the figure must be according to the amount you want to raise the paper that is specified for all [patients].
Et si a teil qui a mestier c’on cope grant quantiteit de la papiere selonc ceu que li papiere est mollifie;	 And if it is necessary to apply a large quantity of paper as softened by them, [it should be done] thus:
puis fent a tout le spatumile sus les II lignes que tu as signiet, et comence des lou grant larmier jusc’a petit;	 then spread the plaster all over the area spanning two lines that you have marked, and start from the large tear down to the small one;
et soit li une des fendures pres des poilz naturez en la groissece d’un raiz, puis boute l’oncine en l’un des II angles dou keur, puis l’escorche toute;	 and one of the cracks should be near the natural hairs in the thickness of a root, then push the onion into one of the two corners at an angle, then peel it all;
puis assemble les II levres a une costure d’une aguille a tout I fil de laine subtil, et essue le sanc, et fai aerdre la superfluiteit des filz sus les II sorcilz a tout aucunes choses gluans, se tu vues faire ce;	 then bring the two lips together with a stitch of a single awl thread made of fine wool, squeeze out the blood, and make the excess threads adhere to the blisters using any suitable substance if you wish to do so.
et se ce non, si n’en aies cure, puis laisse la costure et les filz jusc’a III jors ou IIII;	 And if this is not the case, without care, then leave the stitching and the threads for three days or four.
puis cure la plaie sens costure de choses sechans et constrignans, car li papiere se relive au soudement de la plaie et l’assemblement de li, mais li costure est muedre (si com dirent li ancien), et c’est ovraiges sens paor;	 Then heal the wound without stitching with drying and binding substances, as paper revives at the edge of the wound and its assembly, but the stitches are rotten (as the ancients say), and it is laborious without fear.
et si a une autre maniere:	 and in another way:
et est que tu seignes la papiere d’une figure qui soit ausi com li fuelle de mirte, si com nos avons conteit, a III oncines desevrez selonc la forme qui est ci:	 And it is that you cut a piece of paper into a shape like the fennel seed, as we have said, in three times divided according to the form below:
puis cope ceu qui sormonte as petites forces igalment selonc la forme qui est ci:	then cut that which stands above the small sections equally according to the following form:
Et se tu n’as pooir de tenir les tenailles, et li chose n’est mie igalz, si prent une aguille ou il ait I fil, et la boute emmi la figure;	 And if you do not have the ability to hold pliers, and the thing is not even, then take a needle with thread, and place it within the shape.
et boute I autre fil delez lou grant larmier, et lou secont fil delez lou petit, et assemble entre tes dois les filz igalment;	 and bring out the other thread from the large hole, and the second thread from the small one, and assemble the threads evenly between your fingers.
puis lieve ta main igalment, et lieve tout le cuir sus coi tu as signiet, si com nos avons conteit, puis assemble les II levres de la plaie par costure, et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	 then place your hand evenly and lift the entire skin over which you have signed, as we have said, then bring together the two lips of the wound by stitching, and heal it until it is healthy.
et se aposteme vient a ton incision, si l’apaise de cerote et de semblans oignement assouajans;	 And if an abscess comes to your incision, calm it with cerate and similar soothing ointments.
et aucune fois avient que li poil de la papiere sont convertit:	 Sometimes the hair of the papier is converted:
si covient que tu uses ceu que nos avons dit de l’incision;	 it is necessary that you use what we have said about incision;
mais li costure en l’une et en l’autre est plus artificialz.	 however, the stitching in one and the other is more artificial.
Li cure des caines si est selonc ceste forme:	 The treatment of dogs follows this form:
et est que tu convertisses la papiere et la fent dedens selonc ceu que j’ai dit, et puis fai II caines par art, et II liiens subtilz ausi lonc com li papiere et li largesce dou spatumile est;	 and it is that you convert the paper and place it within as I have said, then make two dogs by craft, and two thin strings as long as the paper and the width of the staple is.
et cope as II chiés de II pars ou tu tiens les filz;	 and cut the heads of the two parts where you hold the threads;
puis assemble l’un et l’autre subtilment sus ceu que sormonte de la papiere de l’oil, et estrain les II cainnes des II parties forment;	 then assemble one and the other subtly above where the paper is covered with oil, and press the two dogs made from the two parts together.
et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, et li cuir qui iert estrainte morra et nercira et porrira, tant qu’il cherra par lui.	 And leave it so for some days, and the skin that is strained will die and rot and fall off when it rots through.
S’il tarde, si le cope a unes forces, puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	 If it remains delayed and becomes necrotic, then heal it as long as it is healthy;
et quant li plaie iert soudee, et si ert levee li papiere, et ne poindront plus li poil;	 And when the wound heals and the paper rises, and the hairs will not grow back.
et c’est li forme des II cainnes que tu feras selonc ceste figure, et selonc ceste quantiteit de lonc et de large:	 And this is the shape of the two canines that you will make according to this figure, and according to this length and width:
li ovraiges est telz que tu preignes une aguille subtil, et i boute I fil de soie souef et subtil;	 You take a thin needle and insert the silk thread and make it thin.
puis assemble les chiés et noe l’un et l’autre subtilment, et soit li longesce des filz une palme de lonc;	 then bring together the heads and attach one to another thinly, and let the length of the threads be a palm-length.
puis ordene en la chasse I autre fil subtil de soie briément, et noe les chief dou fil;	 place the other silk thread in the canine shape briefly, and attach its head.
puis mette li malaides son chief en ton sain;	 then put the patient's head on your lap.
et soit delez lou soleil si que li ovraiges soit declairiez, car c’est uns ovraiges subtilz et menus, puis boute l’aguille a tout la chasse en la racine dou poil ajosteit, et la fai percier en la papiere hastanment tant que tu la traies desus lou poil natureil;	 let the patient be in the sun so that the work is clear, for this work is subtle and small. Then push the needle through the entire canine shape to its root alongside the natural hair, and make it pierce the paper quickly until you draw it over the natural hair.
puis estrai le poil jusque sus la chasse, et boute en la chasse celui poil, s’il en i a I ou II ou III ou plusors;	 Then pull the hair up to the skin, and push the hair into the skin if there is one, two, three or more of them.
puis estrai ta main tant que li poilz veigne fuers a tout la chasse en la papiere avec lou poil natureil.	 Then pull your hand along with the hairs as far as they reach the skin to the paper, taking out the natural hair.
Et se li chasse est traite et li poilz ne vient fuer avec li, si trairas la chasse au desoz a tout le fil que tu i as ordeneit, tant que li chasse veigne fuer dou pertus desus et que tu la voies par la vision de l’oil;	 And if the skin is treated and the hairs do not come out with it, you will pull the skin down to its full extent according to what you have prepared, until the skin comes out through the hole above and you see it through the eye's sight.
adonques si trairas la chasse et le fil, et clo l’oil et lou laisse clo II jors ou III, tant que li poil s’aerde en son leu et naisse li char sus;	 Then you will pull the skin and the thread, close the eye and leave it closed for two or three days, until the hair adheres in its place and a blister forms above.
et se li poilz est petis, si acompaigne I poil lonc des chevoulz naturez, et soit alevez avec celui ou tu le laisse, tant qu’il soit eslongiez et puis le lieve.	 If the hairs are small, let the long hair of the head grow along with it, and raise them together until they are lengthened, then shave them.
de la porriture de l’oil	of the purulence of oil
Quant ceste maladie qui est apelee «aleacrati» ou li porriture vient en l’oil, si en i a de II manieres:	 When this illness called "alecrati" or the boil comes in the eye, it occurs in two ways:
l’une natureil, et l’autre innatureil.	 One natural, the other unnatural.
Et avient par soudement de plaie, ou de tailleure ou de cautere, et par semblans choses.	 And it happens due to a sudden wound, or incision, or cauterization, and similar things.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige en li est que tu fendes celle soudure, et dessevre les levres de li, et met dedens tentes de lin, et la lie tant qu’elle soit sanee;	 And the manner of work is that you split that joint, separate the lips from it, and insert linen bands inside, and keep it until it heals.
et ne covient mie que tu uses en la cure de li de choses que sechent et restraignent.	 And you must not use in the treatment of it things that dry and restrain.
Car se tu fais ceu, si revient li maladie pire que li premiere;	 For if you do this, the illness becomes worse than the first one;
mais i oevre de choses amollissans, si com fenugreic;	 but the work of softening things, such as fenugreek;
et l’arose d’aigue ou altee et semence de lin soient cuites, et oignemens dyaquilon fondut en aucun des oiles, et i envoloupe une tente, et le cure de ceu.	 and the rose water or ale and flaxseed should be cooked, and dilute a bit of Dachshund oil in any oil, and wrap it in a linen band, and treat this.
Et li tresors de ta cure si est que tu te dones en garde qu’ele ne soude mie selonc la forme qu’elle fut devant;	 And the treasures of your care are such that you should take care not to suture it in its former shape;
et cist ovraiges que nos avons dit nen est fuers que adresemens de ceste maladie, qu’elle ne reviegne selonc la forme qu’elle fut devant.	 and this work that we have said is not without the correction of this disease, so that it does not recur in its former shape.
de la char qui vient en l’oil	Of the flesh that comes into the oil
Ceste maladie que est desoz qui vraiement est apelee «axacrati», et est naturelz et accidens.	 This disease which truly is called "axacrati", and is natural and accidental.
Li accidens vient de plaie et de fendure et de cautere et de choses semblans;	 The accidents come from wounds, cuts, cauterization and similar things;
et li voie de l’ovraige en li si est que tu preignes un aguille, en coi il ait I fil double, et la fiche en la char, et li fai percier des le senestre larmier tant c’a destre, si que li filz veigne en II chiés de la char;	 and the path of the work is that you take a needle with double thread, and pierce it through the skin from left to right so that the threads come out in two holes in the skin.
puis estent la char au desus a tout l’aguille, et la cope a I spatumile large.	 Then, raise the skin over the whole needle, and apply the spatula wide.
Et se li figure de la papiere revient selonc ceu qu’il covient, c’est boin;	 And if the shape of the bone returns as it should, it is good;
se ceu non, si pren I raseur et le met en la fendure, et torne la papiere, et fent II fendures ou costeit dedens la papiere;	 If not, take the rasp and place it in the gap, and turn the bone, and make two gaps where the bone touches inside the bone.
et soient li chiés des II fendures des II angles de l’incision que tu as copeit, et soit fais uns angles si que quant elles sont assemblees, que li figure soit ausi com li figure d’une lettre qui a non «I griesche»;	 and let the ends of the two gaps at the angles of the incision you made be aligned, and make an angle so that when they are assembled, the shape is as a letter with the name "Greek cross".
puis oste celle char, selonc la quantiteit que ses costez est agus desoz, de ceu qui enseut la papiere, puis ajoste les II parties desevrees, et les cout d’un fil de lainne;	 then remove that cartilage according to its size so that it is even with the bone on both sides of it, and join the two separated parts using a piece of linen thread.
puis lou cure de ceu que nos avons dit des medicines mollifians, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 then apply the medicine for softening as we have said, and let it heal until it is healed.
Et se li maladie vient de fendure ou de costure ou de cautere, si covient que tu fendes une fendure plainne desoz les poilz des papieres, et selonc ceu qui est ci devant;	 And if the patient's illness comes from a cut or stitch or burn, you must make a clean incision beneath the hair on the affected area, as described earlier.
puis desevre entre les II leivres d’une tente, si com j’ai dit;	 then separate the two sides of the wound with forceps, as I said.
et doit on faire l’ovraige selonc la forme de la maladie, car elle est mout diverse en forme, et li saiges maistres appareille engien de tout som pooir coment il faice revenir la figure a sa forme natureil;	 and the work should be done according to the shape of the illness, for it is very diverse in form, and wise masters prepare tools with all possible skill to restore the figure to its natural form.
et li malaides meisme, selonc ceu qu’il i covient d’ovraige et d’estrumens em plusors dispositions.	 and the patient himself, according to what work and instruments are required in various situations.
dou soudement de la papiere	under the skin of the paper
Quant ceste soudure avient a mains homes en teil maniere que li papiere desus est sodee avec le blanc de l’oil, et ne puet movoir ne faire ses ovraiges naturez, si covient donques que tu i boutes la pointe d’un raseur desoz la papiere, et la lieve en haut;	 When the suture of the skin is like the paper above is sewn with white oil and cannot move or perform natural functions, then it is necessary to insert a sharp instrument under the skin and lift it up.
et l’estent as pinceures, tant que tu copes ceu qui est aert au spatumile subtil, qui ne soit mie trop agus ne trop trenchans, si que li malaides ne puisse soffrir que li spatumile trop agus ne blecent l’oil;	 And hold it with forceps, until you grasp the cartilage that is near the subtletiespate, which should not be too sharp nor too pointed, so that the patient cannot suffer from the too sharp spatula pricking the eye.
et soit ton incision, dont tu escorche celle assemblee, legierement, si que li papiere reviegne selonc sa forme natureil;	 And make your incision, from which you scrape the gathered tissue, gently, so that the paper returns according to its natural shape.
et est sanee toute celle assemblee, et font aucune fois en l’oil aigue salee, et le leve d’aigue douce, et de coliere;	 And all the gathered tissue is healed, and sometimes in the sharp oil it becomes infected, and lifts of sharp vinegar and vinegar water.
puis met entre la papiere et l’oil une tente de lin, et met sus l’oil laine moillie en abun d’uef;	 Then put a tent of linen between the paper and the oil, and above the oil place wool soaked in plenty of egg.
et aprés le tier jor use dou coliere et des choses soudans tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And after three days use vinegar water and hot things until it is healed.
de l’ungle de l’oil	Of the nail of the eye
Saiches que li ungle est selonc II manieres:	 Know that the claw is according to two ways:
elle est nervouse et semblans a I dur syfac, et une autre qui n’est mie nervouse, mais est semblans a blainche moistor congelee, que quant on la touche de fer et on la cuide panre as pinceures, si ne puet om;	 the claw is either nerve-like and similar to hard horn, or another that is not nerve-like but resembles white frozen moisture, when it is touched by iron and cooked with pliers, it cannot be moved.
et l’une et l’autre semblance encomence devers le grant larmier, et croist poc et poc tant qu’ele cuevre toute la veue et toute la lumiere et le movement de l’oil.	 and both begin towards the great corner, and grow little by little until it covers the whole eye and all the light and the movement of the oil.
Et li maniere de l’incision si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, puis li oevre les eulz;	 And the method of incision is that the patient places his head on a healthy surface, then he opens his eyes;
et lieve la papiere a ta main, puis coil l’ungle as pinceures de petite doubleure, et l’estent au desus;	 and you lift the paper with your hand, then press the claw with small pliers and hold it above;
puis pren une aguille, et i met I poil de cheval, ou de vaiche, ou de buef, et I fil fort;	 Then take a needle, put horsehair or cowhair or bull's hair, and a strong thread;
et double la pointe de l’aguille un poc et la fiche emmi l’ungle, et la perce a tout l’aguille, et lie l’ungle d’un fil et l’estent au desus, et escorche a tout lou poil le costeit de l’ungle qui enseut la prunele et la soie au poil jusc’au chief, puis cope lou remanant en la racine dou larmier a tout lou spatumile subtil et as petites forces, et laisse la char natureil ou larmier, si que par l’incision ne veigne li cors des larmes acostumeement;	 and bend the tip of the needle slightly and thrust it into the nail, and pierce through with the whole needle, tie the nail with a thread and extend it above, and shave the hair from the side of the nail where there is the pulp and the silk to the root, then chop the remaining in the root of the armpit with subtle spatula and small force, leaving the natural flesh or armpit so that by incision the body does not bring forth tears as usual.
et aucune fois s’estent li ungle a l’oncine soulement, et au fil, si com nos avons dit;	 and sometimes the nail remains at the fingertip only, according to what we said;
puis l’escorche on a tout le spatumile souef de coi ci est li forme:	 Then scrape off all the fatty tissue of this kind, which is the shape:
Et garde que li spatumile ne touche la toile charnue et la rompe, et que li prunele ne soit percie;	 And ensure that the fatty tissue does not touch the muscular layer and break it, and that the muscle fiber is not pierced.
et aprés l’incision giete en l’oil un poc de seil broiet, et dou coliere fait de litargire, et le laisse jusc’a l’autre jor;	 And after the incision pour oil a little piece of egg yolk beaten, and with collirium made from litharge, leave it until the next day.
puis le cure de ceu qu’il i covient tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then heal the wound as necessary until it heals completely.
Et se li ungle n’est mie nervouse, et tu ne pues bouter l’aguille, et li uncines n’i puet entrer, maintes fois est curee ceste semblance d’ungle de medicines;	 If the nail is not nerve-rich and you cannot insert a needle and the unguent can't enter, many times this appearance of the nail is cured with medicines.
et naissent sicom j’ai conteit en la division, et se tu la vues coper, si oevre l’oil dou malaide, et pren le spatumile legier poc agut selonc ceste forme:	 And as I mentioned in the previous section, when they grow out, if you see them covered, open the oil for the patient, take a little sharp fatty tissue as per this shape:
Et reis l’ungle desus subtilment, et se tu vois qu’elle amenuise point et li rasion i apresse, si distille de ta bouche en l’oil coliere fait de litargire et dou coliere rouge et seil broiet, et estoupe l’oil jusc’a l’autre jor;	 And scrape the nail slightly above, and if you see that it does not diminish at all and the reason for this becomes apparent, distill from your mouth into the collyrium oil made of litargyre and red collyrium powder, and instill the oil until the next day;
puis rencomence l’autre ovraige selonc ceste meisme oevre, tant qu’elle soit toute ostee.	 Then repeat the other work according to this same method, until it is completely healed.
Se aucune chose ne t’est contraire en l’oil, si com aposteme chaus, adonques la lait, et cure premier l’aposteme chaut tant qu’il soit sanez, puis rencomence l’ovraige si com devant, tant qu’il soit sanez.	If nothing opposes you in the oil, like an abscess heals, then milk it, and first heal the abscess hot until it is healed, then continue the work as before, until it is healed.
Et se li apparance de la chair dou larmier nuit en l’oil par grant nuisement, si la sospent a l’oncine, et en cope une partie et non mie tot, que cors de larmes n’i viegne;	 And if the appearance of the flesh around the eye is harmed by the oil through great damage, suspend it on an onion, and cut a small portion, not completely, so that tears do not come.
puis distille en l’oil coliere rouge qui est fais de litargire.	 Then distill into the red collyrium oil made of litargyre.
de la char qui naist sus la prunelle	of the flesh that grows above the pupil
Es eulz d’aucuns homes naist aucune fois char rouge, et cuevre la prunele et restraint sus les papieres et les torne au defuer, et semble une rose de balauste;	 The hairs of some men sometimes grow red and cover the eyelid, rising above the paperwork and turning towards the outside, resembling a balanced rose.
et li ovraiges si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, puis li oevre les eulz, et coil toute celle char as uncines convenaubles a ceu, et la sostien a la force;	 and the work is that the patient places their head on a pillow, then opens the eyes, and all that red hair should be cut with appropriate scissors, and it must be held firmly.
puis cope la premiere char, et vai tout copant au raseur jusc’a la fin, et te garde que tu ne bleces l’oil a l’ovraige;	 then cut the first red hair, and continue cutting to the end with scissors until the very end, and be careful not to prick the oil during the work.
et soit li incision dou spatumile que nos avons dit en l’incision de l’ungle et as petites forces de coi on oste lou sebel, si com li forme aprés cest chapistre lou demostre;	 and the incision with the spatula, as we have said in the treatment of the nail and small forces like those used to remove a splinter, according to the form after this chapter.
et quant li incision est acomplie et ostee toute li char, si emple l’oil de seil broiet ou tu i distille coliere rouge et semblans medicines corrosives, et met sus l’oil defuer coton avec abin d’uef, si qu’il soit asseurez d’aposteme chaut;	 And when the incision is completed and all the flesh is removed, use oil of rosin broken or distilled red collyrium, which resemble corrosive medicines, spread it over cotton with egg white, so that it is securely hot on the abscess.
et s’il i demore rien, et li sans chaus te sormonte, et tu doutes aposteme chaut, si laisse l’oil et cure l’aposteme de choses apaisant aposteme chaut;	 If anything remains, and the wound becomes cold, and you doubt whether it is hot on the abscess, leave the oil and treat the abscess with things that soothe it.
puis revien a ton ovraige tant qu’il soit sanez, et ensi fai cant chars est ajostee en l’oil par ceste semblance.	 Then return to your work when it is healed, and in this way do all charms that are soaked in oil with this resemblance.
Mais toutevoie il covient que tu aliges la cure de chescun oil foible de la voie natureil;	 But you must lighten the treatment of each oil by the natural way.
et de la voie accident, en ovraige de fer;	 And of the accidental way, in work with iron;
et ne bouter mie ta main en aucun de ces ovraiges tant que tu voies que cist membres soit soffrans celui ovraige.	 and not to press your hand in any of these works until you see that this limb is suffering from the work.
des voines des eulz	The veins of the eyes
Sebel sont voinnes rouges que sont covertes sus l’oil, et tolent a la veue son ovraige et afoiblissent l’oil toz jors.	 Red veins that are covered with oil become visible and their work (operation) can be seen and the oil weakens completely every day.
Mestier est donques au premier que tu regardes se li oil, en coi sebel est, est fors, et n’i a autre maladie fuers que lou sebel;	 Therefore, it is necessary at first that you observe whether oil, in which the sebaceous gland is, is out or foreign, and has no other disease but the sebaceous gland.
adonques le coil en teil maniere:	 Then press your hand on it in this manner:
comande au malaide qu’il mette son chief en ton sain, puis sospent celles voines a tout l’oncine selonc sa sapience, et soit li oncines subtilz double selonc ceste forme:	 instruct the patient to place their head in your hand, then hold these veins all the way along according to his wisdom, and let the incisions be subtle doubles according to this form:
Et soient dui oncine par degrez en .i. cors selonc ceste forme:	And let there be two degrees of pressure in one stroke according to this form:
puis c’on coil as forces celles voinnes subtilment, et essue lou sanc houre aprés autre, tant que tu voies removoir celles voines fuers de l’oil;	 Then press these veins gently but firmly, and squeeze the blood hour after hour until you see the veins move away from the oil.
et garde que tu ne blecier l’oil as pointes des spatumiles, et fai cest ovraige a houre de midi devant lou soleil, et soies mout fervans en ton ovraige si que tu ne copes fuer que celles voinnes;	 And be careful not to bleach the oil at the tips of the splinters, and perform this task at noon before the sun, and be very warm in your work so that you do not catch these wounds.
et quant tu avras ce fait, si distille en l’oil coliere vert et rouge por corrumpre ceu qui est demorez dou sebel.	 When you have done this, if you distill green and red oil, it will heal the sores that are hardened by the scab.
Et se tu n’as pooir de coillir tout ceu en celle houre, si fai emplastre sus l’oil de choses apaisans la dolor des eulz, et le laisse aucuns jors tant que li dolors soit apaisie et soit asseurez d’aposteme chaut, puis rencomence selonc ceste maniere qui est devant tant qu’il soit sanez;	 And if you cannot collect everything in that hour, make a plaster on the oil of things that soothe the pain of the eyes, and leave it for some days until the pain is soothed and assured of abscessing hot, then continue according to this method as before until it is healed.
et c’est li forme des forces:	 And this is the form of forces:
de la fistule de l’oil	of the oil duct
Li mire si nomment «arissati» fistule:	 The tool called "arissati" is:
quant tu la cures per cautere et par medicine ague ardant selonc ceu que j’ai devant dit, et elle n’est mie sanee, si est engien en li que tu fendes sus l’aposteme, lai ou il doit meurer, et trai toute la moistor que i est, tant que li os soit descovers.	 When you cure it with cautery and burning medicine as I have said before, and if it is not healed, there is an instrument in it that you split above the abscess, where it should die, and drain all the moisture that is there, while the bone remains exposed.
Et quant li os iert descovers, et tu verras la corruption et la noiror, si la reis a tout l’estrument de coi ci est li forme;	 And when the bone is exposed, and you see the corruption and blackness, if it is completely in the instrument of which this form is:
et est apelez «aspre chief», et soit fait de feir inde a I chief reont, et soit pointoiez si com une lime si com il est en la presente forme:	 and is called "sharp head", and should be made of iron, with the head rounded like a spearhead as shown in this form:
Et met sus lou leu de l’os corrumput, puis le torne entre tes dois, et presse ta main un poc tant que tu saiches que celle corruption est rese;	 And place it on the bone of the dislocation, then turn it between your hands, and press your hand slightly until you feel that the dislocation is reset.
et fai ceu aucune fois, puis restoure lou leu de medicines exiccatives.	 And do this once, then restore the joint with medicine-absorbing substances.
se li leus est soudez, et char i naist, et li cors de la bowe est soudez, et remaint ensi XL jors, et il ne renovele et n’est mie apostemez, et accidens mavais n’i vient, saiches qu’il est sanez;	 if the joints are fused and char is present and the core of the bone is fused and remains so for 40 days without renewal and it is not abscessed or infected, know that it is healed.
se ceu non, si n’i a autre engien que de ramener la fistule au pertus dou neif selonc ceste forme:	 if this is not the case, there is no other device for bringing the fistula to the surface according to this shape:
et est que tu descuevre de l’os la seconde fois par fer, et par medicines agues, et quant il iert descovers si prent I foret selonc ceste forme, et soit li chiés de fer a III angles, et li fust soit atenuis jusc’a chief si com tu vois ci:	 and it is that you open the bone a second time with iron, and with hot medicines, and when it is opened, take the forceps according to this shape, and let the head of the forceps have three angles, and let the shaft be narrowed towards the end as you see here:
puis le met sus l’os delez lou larmier, et esloigne ta main de l’oil I poc, puis torne a tot le foret tant qu’il perce l’os et le sent li malaides par ceu que li vens en ist s’il tient sa main sus son neif;	 Then place it on the dislocated bone next to the socket, and move your hand away from the oil hole. Then turn the entire key all the way until it pierces the bone and the patient feels it if he holds his hand on his neck.
et pues restoure lou leu de medicines seches, si com je t’ai ensigniet, et quant li char naist et endurcist li leus, si vait li matiere au neif;	 And then restore the dislocation with dry medicines as I have shown you, and when the flesh heals and hardens the dislocation, the matter goes to the neck.
si est plus legiere chose au malaide.	 it is easier for the patient.
de l’issue de l’oil	of the flow of oil
Quant li eulz apert fuer dou tout en tout, et il ne vient point de destorbier au nef, ne amenuisement, si covient que tu lies lou malaide;	 When the eyes are wide open in all directions and it does not move to the neck or decrease, you must hold the patient.
puis le saine, puis li met ventouses ou haterel sens ferir por succier, puis met sus l’oil I liien fait d’acaice et de aloe et d’encens et de sarcocolle, et puis estrain l’oil, et l’emplaustre sus de bendes et de drapelz;	 Then heal it, then put on mustard or hot poultices without iron to help, then place on the oil made from acacia and aloe and incense and saracocolla, and then hold it in place, and apply ointment on bands and cloths.
et li maniere des drapelz si est que tu preignes drapelz assez molz, et double chescun en IIII, et puis met l’un sus l’autre selonc la quantiteit que li eulz en ait mestier;	 The manner of plasters is that you take soft plasters, fold each one into four, and then place one on top of the other according to the quantity that the eyes require.
puis l’estrain par desus d’un bendeil dur forment, et rencomence les ventouses por succier sens ferir;	 Then strain it with a hard bandage form and repeat the blisters for sucking without wounding.
puis oste les ventouses et laisse l’oil estraint jor et nuit, et se li liiens amolist, si covient que tu l’estraignes mout;	 Then remove the blisters and let the oil remain strained day and night, and if it becomes unstrained, you must strain it strongly.
puis oste lou liien aprés le jor et la nut, et se tu vois l’oil repairier, c’est boin;	 Then remove the bandage after the day and the night, and if you see the oil repair, that's good.
se ce non;	 but if not;
si rencomence l’emplaustre et les drapelz et lou liien et les ventouses tant qu’il soit sanez.	 If it is not so, repeat the plasters and the bandage and blisters and the wounds until it heals.
dou derrompement de toile uvee	The open wound of the eye does not heal on its own.
Quant disruptions vient en la toile uvee, puis apert, et vient fuer des papieres si com I grain de resins, et est espoantauble a veoir;	 When dislocations occur in the ruptured eye, it opens, and paper-like substances come out like drops of resin, and it is terrible to see.
adonques se tu la vues coper, li ovraiges est telz que tu boutes une aguille en la racine des la partie desoz jusc’a celi desus, puis boute une autre aguille ou il ait I fil double des la partie dou larmier;	 Then, if you see it, cover [the eye] with the work being such that you insert an awl into the root of the affected part up to where it is above, then insert another awl or double thread from the lid side.
et la fai percier, et laisse la premiere aguille selonc la disposition;	 and make it pierce through, and leave the first awl in place according to its position.
puis cope lou leu dou fil double et lie une partie de l’uve entor, et l’estraint bien, puis estrai l’aguille et met sus l’oil lainne moillie en abun d’uef;	 then take the double thread and tie a part of the eyeball around it, and tighten it, then remove the awl and put moistened egg yolk oil on it.
et le laisse tant que li filz chiece avec l’uve, puis cure l’oil de choses confortans tant que li plaie soit sanee;	 leave it until the threads stick to the eyeball, then heal the egg yolk oil with soothing things until the wound is healed.
et aucune fois li plaie est restrainte par l’uve chescune part d’un cercle de drap, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	 And sometimes the wound is bound on each side with a circle of cloth until it heals.
Et se li eulz done grant apparance, si le perce au spatumile subtil qui viegne em parfont de l’oil, et corre la moistor albuginé et dessende li eulz, et entre ens tantost;	 If the eyes appear swollen, pierce them with a thin splint coming from oil, and draw out the moisture and pus, then put medicine in immediately.
puis l’estrai tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then pull it out until it is healed.
de la bowe de l’oil	with a thin spatula coming from pure oil
Ceste maladie qui est apelee «alcunnati» nen est fuers que bowe qui est assemblee en l’oil, semblant a aigue dessendant, et ce n’est mie aigue;	 This disease called "alcunnati" is not foreign to one who has been assembled in oil, resembling an abscess, but it is not an abscess.
et li maniere de l’apparance de l’ovraige si est que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege appareilliet et droit, puis prent le chief entre tes mains de II pars, et lou muef tant que tu voies la bowe venir au desus a tes eulz;	 The manner of the appearance of this disease is that you make the patient sit on a prepared chair and upright, then take hold of its head between both hands, and move it until you see the abscess come to your eyes.
puis soit ens fichie, et ne dessende et soit descombree li lumiere, et voie li malaides les choses si com il soloit;	 Then let it (the affected part) be driven in, and do not withdraw (it), and clear the opening, and show the patient the things as he is accustomed.
et s’elle ne dessent desoz, saiches que c’est aigue, et se li dessendemens de la bowe n’est appareilliez si com nos avons dit.	 And if it does not withdraw, know that it is infected, and if the dressing of the bowl is not prepared as we have said.
si fai seoir lou malaide entre tes mains, puis prent le spatumile subtil et fent sus la toile cornee I poc par la continuation de la conjunctive avec la toile cornee et la corone, tant que li bowe isse;	 Make the patient sit between your hands, then take the thin spatula and make a hole in the cornified tissue through the continuation of the conjunctiva with the cornified tissue and the bone, as far as the bowl goes.
et quant elle ert issue, si distille en l’oil aigue chaude mellee a miel, ou aigue ou fenugreic est boillis et miel, puis soit curee d’autre cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	 And when it (the pus) comes out, distill it in hot sharp oil mixed with honey or hot oil of fenugreek and honey, then let it be treated with another remedy until it is healed.
des aigues de l’oil	The sharp points of oil
Nos avons jai les semblances des aigues en la division, et ceu qu’il covient por percier;	 We have similarities with the eyes of hawks in cutting, and those things that must be pierced.
si en oevre selonc la santeit.	 according to the healthiness.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains croisiet, fuers de la lumiere por le soleil, et li lie l’oil sain et estreint mout fort;	 You must make the patient sit between your hands crossed, away from sunlight and hold the oil saint and tighten very strongly.
puis met la papiere de l’oil a ta main senestre se li eulz est senestres, ou a ta main destre se li eulz est destres;	 then put the paper of the oil on your left hand if the eyes are left, or to your right hand if the eyes are right.
puis prent en ta main destre, se li eulz est senestres, l’estrument qui est apelez «almagda», ou a ta main senestre, se li eulz est destre;	 then take in your right hand, if the eyes are left, the instrument called "almagda", or in your left hand if the eyes are right.
puis met la pointe de l’estrument delez la corone par la groissece d’un rait en celle blenchor de l’oil a la partie dou menor larmier, puis boute l’estrument qui est apelez «almagda» vertuousement, et trestorne ta main tant qu’il perce en la blenchor de l’oil, et sente que almagda viegne a la chose vuide;	 then place the tip of the instrument under the crown through the thickness of a reed in that hollow part of the oil at the lower eyelid, then push the instrument called "almagda" firmly and hold your hand as long as it pierces the lower eyelid, and feel that almagda comes to an empty place.
et covient que li mesure de la voie almagda soit au parfont de la mesure des l’espaice qui est des la prunele jusc’a la fin de la noirour;	 The measure of the way (should be) equal to the depth of the space which is from the prunele up to the end of the nail.
et c’est li corone de l’oil;	 and it's the crown of the oil.
si verras l’os en celle papiere por la clarteit de la toile cornee, et pues met l’estrument jusc’a leu ou li aigue est, puis l’espresse desoz une voie aprés autre.	 If you see the bone in this paper through the clarity of the horned cloth, then put the instrument up to it or where the sore is, and then press down along another path afterwards.
se li aigue dessent maintenant, si voit li malaides devant lui et l’estrument en son oil.	 If the instrument is to be applied now, the patient sees it before him and the tool in its oil.
Aprés repose I petit, et se li aigue remonte la seconde voie, met la fuer avec l’estrument, et quant elle est ens fichie et ele ne monte, si estrai almagda legierement en tornoiant ta main poc et poc;	 After a little rest, if the sore rises along the second path, put the force with the instrument, and when it is firmly fixed and it no longer rises, it should be straightened gently by turning your hand slowly.
et puis remette en aigue un poc de seil gemme, et leive de ceu l’oil dedens.	 Then put some small gemmed silk thread on the sore again, and remove this oil from within.
Puis met par defuer l’oil estoupes ou lainne moillie en oile roset et en abun d’uef, et lie avec l’oil sain.	 Then, moist a cloth or woolen cloth with rose oil and egg, and bind it with clean oil.
Nos, et cil qui sont de nostre tens, mettons sus comin broiet avec abun d’uef.	 We, and those of our time, place on top, finely ground with much egg.
Et se almagda n’i puet entrer en l’oil par sa duresce, car il i a de teilz homes qui ont trop durs les eulz, si covient que tu preignes l’estrument qui est apelez «alberit», de coi ci est li forme:	And if almagda cannot enter into the oil due to its hardness, since there are some men who have excessively hard hairs, then you must take the instrument called "alberit," which is shaped like this:
Et perce donques la conjunctive soulement, et n’aler mie trop em parfont, mais fai I leu subtil, puis i boute almagda, si com nos avons dit;	 And then pierce the joint only, and do not go too deep, but make it subtle, then put in alum, as we have said.
et au complissement de l’uevre appareille au malaide I dorteur avenant, en coi il dorme sus son dos en I leu tenebrous;	 And for the completion of the work, prepare the patient, the sleeper, arriving, with him lying on his back in a darkened place.
et soit deveez de toz movemens, et preigne legieres viandes, et ne mueve son chief ne a destre ne a senestre, et soit liiez selonc sa disposition jusc’a tier jor;	 and let him be deprived of all movements, take light foods, and not move his head to the right or left, and bind him accordingly for three days.
puis le deslie en cele maison meisme tenebrouse, et esprueve sa veue, et lou fai veoir aucunes choses, et puis li remet lou lien jusc’a septime jor;	 then unbind him in the same darkened house, test his sight, and make him see certain things, and then bind him again for seven days.
et ne covient mie que tu faices ceu en l’oure de la cure ou aprés l’incision maintenant, mais il covient que tu aliges ceu, por ceu que li aigue monte hastanment.	 and it is not necessary that you do this during the hour of treatment or after incision now, but it is necessary that you reduce this, because the pain increases quickly.
se apostemes chaus vient, que tu desliies l’oil devant le septime jor, et l’adrece de ceu qui assouaige aposteme;	 If an abscess swells up, you should lance the oil before the seventh day, and follow the guidance of those who soothe abscesses.
et quant il est apaisiez, si deslie la veue et met sus sa faice I orilliet por covrir aucun jor, et soit adés en celle maison tenebrouse.	 And when it is soothed, you should close the wound with ointment to cover it for any day, and remain in that dark room always.
Et puis isse de la maison poc et poc, et se convertisse en ses cas;	 Then leave the house little by little, and return to your usual state.
et saiches que nulz deciples ne se doit entremettre en cest cas.	 And know that no disciple should interfere in this case.
Et uns vint a nos qui estoit de la Yrach, qui nos dist que en som pais faisoit om almagda perciet, a coi on succe l’aigue, mais toutevoie je n’en vis onques nul en nostre terre, ne je ne lou lis onques en livres des anciens;	 And one came to us who was from the East, who told us that in his land they make almond juice like vinegar, causing it to be sour, but I have never seen anyone do this in our land, nor have I read of it in any ancient books.
et par aventure c’est une novele chose.	 And by chance, it is a new thing.
Et ce sont les semblances des formes de almagda, por ceu que cil qui ne les conoit les voie;	 And these are the similarities of the forms of almagda, because he who does not know them sees them.
et soient d’arain proprement:	 and they are from a specific kind of arrow:
Et soient li chief d’aus de ceste meisme subtiliteit, et li derriene en .iij. angles ague.	And these are the characteristics of the heads of this same subtlety, and the rear parts in four corners sharp.
de la char sor le neis	of the pus in the nose
Aucune fois naissent ou neis chars ajostees diverses, de coi il i a aucunes qui semblent scorpions a mout de piez;	 Sometimes new or nascent charms resemble various different things, of which there are some that seem like scorpions with many feet.
et si i a de telz ou il ait char enchancree de fuxe color, et si a char souef de bone color.	 and if there are such [charms] or if the charm is swollen of this color, and if the charm is soft of bone color.
En celle donques de ces chars qui est souef, et ne mie enchancree, covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains encontre lou soleil;	 Therefore, in those cases of soft charms, and not swollen, you must make the patient sit between your hands facing the sun.
et oevre ses narines, et giete l’oncine a celles chars, et les trai fuers;	 and open his nostrils, and pour the onion juice onto those charms, and draw them out.
pues cope ceu que tu em pues sostenir au spatumile subtil agut d’une part, tant que tu saiches que celle char est toute ostee.	 Then take that which you can hold with a fine sharp spatula on one side, as long as you know that the charm is entirely extracted.
Et s’il en remaint aucune chose c’on ne puisse coper, si l’ovrez a tout I des estrumens subtil legierement, si qu’il n’i demoure rien;	 And if there remains something which cannot be captured, open it all with fine, light instruments so that nothing remains.
et se sans te sormonte, ou aposteme chaus, si lou secort si com il covient;	 And if the abscess swells or boils up, help as necessary.
et se c’est apostemes malignes, si te haste et lou cauterize tant que li sans soit estainchiez et soient ostees toutes les chars, puis giete ou neis aisil et aigue ou vin.	 If it is malignant boils, hurry and cauterize them until the pus dries up and all the charred matter is removed, then apply oil or cold water and vinegar or wine.
Se li neis oevre, et moistors en vient jusc’a palais, saiches qu’il est sanez;	 If it does not heal with the application of moisture, and malignity comes up to the palace (meaning the head), know that it is healthy.
et se moistors ne perce si com il covient, saiches qu’il i a char nee en l’os desus, a coi li estrumens ne vient mie por taillier:	 And if moisture does not pierce as necessary, know that there is pus formed in the bone above, to which the probe will not come for cutting.
adonques covient il que tu i boutes I fil de lin un poc gros, et soit noez de mains nous, et ait entre chescun nout d’espaice I doit ou moins;	 Then you must put a cotton ball made from flax fibers into it, moistened with our hands, and leave a space between each cotton ball of the required size or less.
et mette li malaides lou chiés dou fil en son neif a som pooir, et traie en odorant tant qu’il viegne par lou neif dedens la bouche;	 And place the patient's head through the hole in the cloth in his neck as far as possible, and draw it out while smelling it until it comes out of the neck through the cloth.
et maintes fois font ensi li enfant as escoles, et c’est legiere chose a celui qui le vuet faire;	 And children often do this in school, and it is easy for one who wishes to perform it.
puis tien le chief qui vient par lou neif a une main, et l’autre chief qui vient par la bouche a l’autre main, et saiche l’un aprés l’autre en soiant as nous qui sont ou fil.	 Then hold the head coming through the neck with one hand and the other head coming from the mouth with the other hand, and guide each other's head in turn while we who are filament-makers do it.
Fai ceu tant que tu saiches que li nout ont corrompue celle char, puis trai lou filz, essue le sanc, et moille lou fil en oignement egiptien, et le remet derechief au neis si com devant;	 Do this until you know that the knot has spoiled that flesh, then draw out the filament, cleanse the blood, and moisten the filament in Egyptian ointment and put it back into the neck as before.
fai ceu III jors ou plus, tant que li oignemens corrode tout ceu qui est demorez de char;	 Allow it to remain for three days or more, until the salve has corroded everything that remains of flesh.
et puis met ou neis une caine de plonc aucuns jors tant qu’il soit sanez, et s’il a mestier de medicines sechans, si en use;	 and then place or insert a plaster made of linen for some days until it is healed, and if there is a need for drying medicines, use them.
et c’est li forme de l’estrument por purgier lou chief, a coi on distille les oiles et les medicines ou neis:	 and this is the shape of the instrument to purge the head, by which they distill the oils and medicines and insert them.
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain, semblant a une lampe overte, si com une cainne, et li conduis ausi;	 And it should be of silver or brass, resembling an open lamp, like a plaster, and lead it in the same way.
et se tu vues, si fai une cainne close, et soit li estrumens plains por espurgier lou chief;	 If you see, then make a closed plaster, and let the instrument be flat to purge the head.
et ait I mainche au chief por lou tenir quant on chaufe l’oile ou aucune liquor.	 and have a handle on the head to hold it when heating the oil or any liquid.
de la char sor le neis	of the pus in the nose
Maintes fois naist au chief dou neis une maladie qui est apelee «telul», et croist et devient grans adés, tant qu’il est vis chose au regarder;	 Often, in the head of the nose, a disease named "telul" arises, which grows and becomes large, until it can be seen with the eye.
et por ceu covient que tu lou copes au comencement, et l’oste tout fuer, puis met sor leu lou cautere ou la medicine ardant;	 and for that reason, you should cut it at the beginning, completely remove it, then put the fire cautery or burning medicine on its place.
et s’on le tarde a coper tant qu’il soit grans, si pren warde s’il est durs, de fuxe color, de povre sens:	 If it is not cut immediately when it becomes large, beware if it is hard, of a dark color, and has poor sensation.
si ne lou touchier mie de fer car c’est uns apostemes enchancrez, car quant on le cope aucune fois, si en vient grant malice au malaide;	 do not touch it with iron because it is an abscess that swells, for when you cut it once, much harm comes to the patient.
et se li apostemes est de soef touchement, non mie de fuxe color, et tu vois c’on le puisse tout coper, si vuide le malaide et lou cope sens paor, et cure le leu de choses sechans et restraignans.	 If the abscess is soft to touch, not of a dark color and you can cover it completely, empty the patient and cut with caution, then treat the place with things that are dry and constricting.
quant li neis est copez et cosus	when the neck is cut and sewn up
Saiches que quant solutions de continuation vient en une de ces cartillagines ovraiges, i profite poc, fuer que en aucuns homes.	 Know that when solution comes in one of these articular cavities [joints], it benefits little, unless in some men.
Il covient donques cant ceu avient a aucun, si regarde se li plaie est fresche a tout son sanc;	 Therefore, whoever experiences this [issue], look if the wound is fresh with all its blood.
et adonques ajoste les II levres a une costure, puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	 Then align the two lips to a stitch, then heal it until it is healed;
et se les levres sont ja desevrees d’une part et d’autre, si covient que tu escorches toutes les parties de lor keur tant qu’elles sainent, puis assemble les II levres a une costure, et l’estraint, et poudre sus poudre de sanc de dragon, et encens broiet;	 And if the lips are disconnected from one side and the other, you must scrape all the parts of them until they heal, then bring together the two lips to a stitch, bind it, and sprinkle powder of dragon's blood and incense powder on it.
et met sus les poudres une piece d’emplaustre de fort ou d’autre emplaustre soudant, et le laisse tant qu’il chiece par lui, puis le cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And place a plug of plaster of strength or another plaster adhering to it, and leave it until it heals by itself, then heal it with ointment until it is healed.
Li maniere de la costure si est que tu assembles la solution:	 The method of stitching is that you gather together the solution (The way to sew it is by bringing together the solution).
ou par aguilles, si com nos avons dit en la costure dou ventre;	 with needles, as we said in abdominal stitching;
ou par fil, si com je le t’ai fait savoir.	 or with thread, as I have told you (The method of stitching is also by thread, as I have informed you).
des apostemes des levres	about abscesses from lips
A mains homes avient dedens les levres aposteme dur, semblans a grains de veces, et menor et plus grant;	 Inside the mouth, there appears an abscess hard like grains of wheat, both smaller and larger (Inside the mouth, an abscess appears that is hard and looks like grains of wheat, some are smaller and others are larger).
adonques couvient que tu tornes les levres, et fendes sus chescun nout, et le prent as pinceures et le cope en chescune partie;	 Then you must turn the lips, cut on top of each tooth, and take it with the forceps and crush it in each part (Then, you should turn the lips, make an incision above each tooth, take it with the forceps and crush it in each area).
puis emple lou leu aprés l’incision de vitriole broiet, tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	 then apply the solution after the incision of crushed vitriol, until the wound is cauterized (Then, use the solution after making an incision with crushed vitriol until the wound is cauterized).
