et puis lou leive d’aisil, et cure lou leu de choses seches tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then apply a salve to the dislocation, and treat the shoulder with dry things until it heals.
de la char des gencives	Of the flesh of the jaws
Maintes fois naist sus les gencives char ajostee, que li ancien apelent «albulus»;	 Often a cyst grows on the gums, which the ancients called "albulus".
si covient que tu la sostienes as tenailles, et la cope a sa racine, et laisse corre la bowe ou le sanc;	 You must hold it with tweezers, cut off its root and leave the cyst or blood to flow.
puis met sor le leu vitriole broiet, ou autres poudres restraignans et desiccatives;	 Then put on the wound vitriol powder, or other powders that contract and dry.
et se celle char revient aprés l’incision, et maintes fois avient, si la cope la seconde fois, et la cauterize:	 If the cyst returns after incision, which often happens, then cut it a second time and cauterize it.
si ne revient mie aprés le cautere;	 It does not return after cauterization.
et ce sont les formes des estrumens por coper.	 These are the shapes of tools for covering.
des sordens	Of the sores
Aucunes fois sont assemblees au chief des dens, dedens la bouche entre les gencives, escorces qui sont laides et aspres;	 Sometimes there are sores assembled at the root of teeth inside the mouth between the gums, which are ugly and harsh.
et aucune fois sont li dent noir et citrin et vers, tant que li corruption vient a la gencive, et sont li dent puant;	 And sometimes teeth are black and yellow and decaying, until the corruption reaches the gums, and they stink.
si covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains, et ses chiés soit en ton saint, et reis les dens ou les escorces aperent, tant qu’il n’i demore rien;	 You must make the patient sit between your hands, and his shoulders be on you, and remove the teeth or the scales that appear, until nothing remains.
et ensi fai de la noiror et de la verdor, et de la jaunice et des autres taiches, tant qu’elles soient mondees;	 And do the same with blackness, greenness, yellowing, and other spots, until they are cleaned.
et s’on oste ceu que i est a la premiere rasion, c’est boin;	 If you remove what is there at the first cause, it is good;
se ceu non, si rencomence a rere le secont jor et lou tier, tant que tu aies tout reis;	 If not, start again on the second or third day and continue until everything is removed.
et saiches que li dent ont mestier de diverses formes d’estrumens por reire, selonc ceu que li oevre lou demoustre, por ceu que li raseur dont on reit defuer les dens ont autres formes que cil dont on reit entre les dens;	 Know that teeth require various forms of instruments for cleaning, according to what the work demonstrates, because the one who cleans the teeth has different shapes than the one who cleans between the teeth.
et cestes formes et autres soient avec toi appareillies.	 And these forms and others be prepared with you.
Il covient quant tu cures lou dent de sa dolor que tu tardes dou traire tant com tu pues, car ce ne doit om mie faire;	 It is necessary that when you cure the tooth of its pain, you delay the pulling as much as possible, for it should not be done at all.
car c’est une substance mout haute jusc’a donc c’on n’ait point d’excusation dou raier.	 because it is a very high substance up to that point, so there can be no excuse for pulling.
Adonques quant li malaides est constrains dou traire, si covient que tu soies certains dou dent doillant.	 Therefore, when the patient is forced to draw, you must be sure of the correct tooth.
Maintes fois desoit li dolor lou malaide, et cuide qu’elle soit ou dent saint, et fait traire le boin dent;	 Often the patient experiences pain and believes it is a holy tooth, and pulls out the healthy tooth.
et toutevoie ne se depart mie li dolor per ceu, tant que li malvais estrais, car nos l’avons ja veut faire a ces sainors;	 Nevertheless, the pain does not go away because of this, until the bad one is removed, for we have already seen this in holy men.
et quant tu es bien certains dou dent doillant, si covient que tu escorches entor lou dent a tout i. spatumile fort por warder la gencive de toutes pars;	 And when you are certain that the tooth is loosening, it is necessary to score around the tooth completely. Spatula strongly to protect the gums from all sides;
puis le mues a tes dois ou as tenailles subtilz au premier poc et poc, tant qu’il soit bien eslochiés, puis i afferme bien les tenailles;	 Then turn your hands or subtle tweezers to the first joint and then gradually, until they are well dislocated, then firmly hold the tweezers.
et soit li chiés dou malaide en ton saint entre tes genous, et lou tien bien si qu’il ne se mueve.	 Hold the patient's arm in your lap, and keep it so that it does not move.
Aprés estrai lou dent droitement sens brisier, et s’il ne saut fuer, si prent aucun de ces estrumens et le boute dedens de chescune part legierement, et lou remuef si com tu as fait premier.	 After the tooth is extracted correctly to break it, and if it does not come out freely, take any of these instruments and gently push it from each side, and move it as you have done before.
Et se li dens est perciez et mengiez, si covient que tu l’emplisses de drapelz, lai ou li pertus sont;	 If the bone is pierced and eaten away, then you must fill it with rags where the wounds are.
et si l’estraint subtilment as tenailles, que il ne brise a l’estraindre;	 And if you hold it gently with tweezers so that it does not break while pulling.
et covient mout saigement ovrer entor la gencive por deschaucier lou dent.	 You must cut around the gum to remove the tooth.
Et te done bien en warde que tu ne le brises, et en remaigne une partie, et reveigne au malaide par la malice de la racine plus grans dolors de la premiere.	 And be careful not to break it and leave a part behind, or the patient will suffer greater pain from the root.
Et te warde que tu ne faices mie ensi com font li ignorant sainor, qui par lor haste et par lor hardiesce brisent aucune fois le charreit, et n’i amenistrent mie ceu que nos avons conteit;	 Be careful not to act like the foolish lord who in haste and recklessness often breaks the cartwheel, and does not bring about what we have described.
mais font venir aucune fois par l’oquison de ceu grant maladie por les racines que i demorent, ou por lou charreit qu’il brisent, si com nos avons sovent veut;	 But sometimes they come on account of the excretion of this great disease through the roots that remain, or by breaking the cartilage, as we have often seen.
et quant li dens est trais, si lavez lou leu de vin ou d’aisil et de seil;	 And when the tooth is pulled, wash the place with vinegar or alum and oil.
et se decorremens de sanc i vient, que sovent avient, si emple lou leu de vitriole broiet;	 If bleeding occurs in the process, as often happens, use vitriol powder.
et se ceu ne vaut, si le cauterize.	 And if that doesn't work, cauterize it.
Les formes des estrumens, a coi om muet les dens premier, soient a longes pointes et a gros mainches, qu’il ne doublent mie quant tu trairas le dent;	 The shapes of the tools used to mute the tooth first should have long points and thick handles, so that they do not bend when you pull the tooth.
et ce sont les formes:	 and these are their forms:
Et soient de gros membres si qu’il ne ploient mie au traire, et soient de fer inde bien fait, et soient dentez por mues tenir.	And should be large enough so that they do not bend when separating, and should be made of good iron, and serrated for holding onto the teeth.
de la racine des dens	From the root of the teeth
Quant li racine demoure au traire, si covient que tu mettes sor le leu coton moilliet em burre I jor ou II, tant que li leus soit amolis, pues i boute les tenailles qui sont apelees «algefri», de coi li chiés semblet bec de soigne;	 When the root remains to be pulled out, it is necessary that you place cotton soaked in butter for one or two days on the place until the place is softened, then insert the forceps called "algefri", which look like a beak of an instrument.
et soient dedens faites ausi com une lime et c’est li forme:	 And within it should be made like a chisel, and this is its shape:
Et se les racines ne vuellent issir a tout ces tenailles, si covient que tu descuevre la char tot entor la racine, et i met l’estrument qui est apelez «althali», c’est a savoir palainche, de coi ci est li forme:	And if the roots do not want to come out with all these tongs, you must uncover the entire cheek around the root and use the instrument called "althali," which is known as plier, of which this is the form:
Et soit fors et gros si qu’il ne brise mie, et se li racine saut par ceu, c’est boin;	 And it should be long and thick so that it does not break, and if the root jumps through it, that is good;
se ceu non, si t’aide de toz les estrumens, de coi les formes vienent ci aprés:	 If not, help yourself with all tools, so that the shapes come afterward:
Et si s’aide on de cest estrument qui ait .ij. rains, de coi ci est li forme:	And help with this tool having two prongs, of which this shape comes from it:
et d’autres ferremens qui sont devant en la rasion des dens, et de cest estrument qui semble unes grans tenailles, dont ci est li forme:	And other iron objects that are in front of the teeth roots, and with this tool resembling large pliers, from which this shape comes:
Et soit cist estrumens fors qu’il ne puisse brisier, et saiches que mout d’estrumens de dens sont;	 Let this tool be long so it cannot break, and know that many dense tools are needed:
et ausi d’autres estrumens, qui ne sont mie contez;	 And also other tools, which are not counted;
et li saiges maistres subtilz trueve par soi meisme son estrument, selonc ceu que ses ovraiges et li maladie li demoustre, car il i a de teilz maladies ou li ancien n’enseignerent point d’estrument por la diversiteit d’au;s et s’om brise point dou charreit ou des autres os, ou il porrit, si i cerche as estrumens qu’il i covient, que je t’ai dit, et t’aide des gestes, de coi ci est li forme:	 And the wise masters skilled in themselves find their tool according to what their work and illness require, for there are some diseases where the ancients did not teach an instrument because of the diversity of ailments, and if it breaks on the cart or other bones, where it can be, seek the tools that are necessary, which I have told you, and help with gestures, so this is the shape:
Et soient gros et bien tenant por tenir l’os, qu’il n’eschaipe, mais le puisse tenir et oster;	 And they must be large and sturdy to hold the bone, so that it does not slip away, but can be held and removed.
et puis restoure lou leu de medicines convenant a ceu, et s’il ait en l’os porriture, et elle est petite, si la reis a tout cest estrument:	 And then restore the joint with appropriate medicines, and if there is pus in the bone, and it is small, let the patient rest with this instrument.
Quant li dent apperent ne mie selonc lou cors natureil, et li forme est laide, et meismement en femmes puceles, si covient que tu saiches se li dens est neis aprés lou dent, et n’est mie en droit leu, et on ne lou puet soier ne limer:	 When the teeth do not appear in accordance with natural form and the shape is deformed, especially in young women; if this happens, you should know that the tooth has not erupted after the dent, and it is not in its proper place, and it cannot be removed or filed.
adonques lou raie;	 Then the ray.
et s’il est aers avec lou dent, si prent cest estrument dont ci est li forme, et est semblans a I petit bec, et soit de fer inde agut en som:	 And if it is outside with the tooth, take this instrument that has this shape and resembles a small beak, and should have sharp iron at its end.
Et lou cope poc et poc em mains jors por la duresce dou dent, et por ceu que tu ne mueves les autres, et s’il est apparans c’on le puisse limer, si lou lime d’une teil lime com ci est li forme:	And the tooth, little by little in many days, due to hardness of the dentin, and because you cannot move the others, and if it appears that it can be filed, file it with a small steel file as shown below in form.
et est ausi com li lime de coi on fait les aguilles;	 And it is as if the limb is like the mold for making needles.
et en lime lou dent poc et poc em mains jors legierement, si qu’il ne se mueve tant qu’il chiece;	 And in this mold the tooth is slowly and lightly carved day by day until it falls out.
puis la plaine en la fin a tout aucun raseur, et se li dens est trop trenchans et il blece la lengue, si covient limer l’aspreteit tant qu’il soit igalz, si qu’il ne blece la lengue ne ne corrompe la parole.	 Then the plane is finished at one end with any smoother, and if the tooth is too sharp and bites the tongue, then the roughness must be filed until it is even, so that it does not bite the tongue or corrupt speech.
quant li dent lochent	when the teeth fall out
Quant li dent devant lochent, ou par percussion ou par cheoir, et li malaides ne puet presser sus ceu qu’il menjue qu’il ne chient, et tu les as curez de medicines restrignans, et ceu ne vaut;	 When the tooth falls out in front, either by percussion or falling out, and the patient cannot chew food without it falling out, and you treat them with constricting medicines, that does not help.
si les covient restraindre d’un fil d’or, car li filz d’argent devient vert et porrit, mais li ors ne se mue onques;	 Therefore they must be held with a gold wire, for silver threads become green and rot, but gold never changes.
et soit li filz moiens ne trop gros ne trop menus, selonc la quantiteit de l’espaice entre les dens;	 And the rod should be neither too thick nor too thin, according to the space between the teeth.
et se tu vues adrecier les dens, si pren lou fil et lou boute double entre les II dens sains, puis met les chiés entre les dens meus, s’il en i a I ou plusors, tant que tu veignes saigement jusc’au dent sain d’autre part;	 And if you want to align the teeth, take the rod and place it between two teeth without damage, then insert the head between the adjacent teeth (if there is one or more of them), until you see it clearly up to the healthy tooth on the other side.
puis rencomence la coverture jusc’a la partie ou tu encomensas, et estrains ta main subtilment et saigement, tant qu’il ne se mueve point;	 then continue covering up to the part where you started, and hold your hand gently and skillfully so that it does not move.
et soit ta lieeure a la racine dou dent si qu’il ne puist eschaper.	 And bind the root of the tooth so that it cannot escape.
Puis cope les chiés dou fil a unes tenailles, et les assemble, et les repont entre le dent sain, et le met ensi qu’il ne blece la lengue;	 Then hold the head with the rod to tongs and assemble them, and place them between the healthy tooth, so that it does not pierce the tongue.
et puis le laisse ensi estroit tant com il puet demorer, et s’il deslie, ou li filz ront, si l’estraint d’un autre fil;	 And then leave it as tight as it can remain, and if it dislocates or loosens, pull on another thread to hold it in place.
si demorrait et servira ensi tout son tens, et c’est li forme des dens et li figure de l’adrecement des II dens sains, et des II meus, si com tu vois:	 If it remains and serves thus throughout its duration, this is the shape of teeth and the form of the alignment of two healthy teeth, or two molars, as you can see.
Et quant li dent chiet, si lou remet on en son leu, de fres en fres, si com nos avons dit;	 And when a tooth falls out, one puts it back in its place, freshly, as we have said.
et ne s’en entremette mie qui n’est saiges et soffrans, et aucune fois fait on la forme d’un dent d’os de vaiche, et lou met on au leu ou li defaute est, et l’estraint on si com nos avons dit, et demore et sert ensi lonc tens.	 And do not interfere with it unless one is wise and experienced; and sometimes a tooth-shaped piece of cow bone is made, and it is placed in the place where it is missing, and held as we have said, and remains and serves for a long time.
de coper lou liien de la lengue	to cover the ligament of the tongue
Aucune fois est cist liiens qui vient desoz la lengue ou naturez, que on naist ensi;	 At times there is a link coming from below the tongue, which occurs naturally;
ou par accident de plaie soudee;	 or by injury caused by a healed wound;
et li ovraiges est telz que tu oevre la bouche dou malaide, et ait sa teste en ton sain, et li lieve la lengue;	 and the procedure is such that you open the mouth of the patient, hold his head steady, and pull out the tongue.
puis cope lou liien nervous dou large, tant que li lengue soit desloie de son tenement, et se il i a duresce ou nout, et c’est de soudement de plaie, si i boute l’uncine et cope dou large celui liement;	 then grasp the nerve-like link with forceps, as long as the tongue is dislocated from its position, and if there is hardness or knotting, and it is due to a sudden injury, press the incision and crush the link with forceps.
et garde que li fendure ne soit mie trop em parfont, por l’artere qui est desoz;	 and be careful that the cut is not too deep, for there is an artery below.
et quant tu as fait, si leve le leu d’aigue rose et d’aisil, ou d’aigue froide, puis met desoz la lengue une tente de lin;	 and when you have completed, raise the place of fresh water or warm water, then put a linen tent under the tongue.
et la teigne li malaides chescune nuit, que li leus ne puisse soder.	 And the itch troubles the patient each night, preventing the limb from healing.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si met sor le leu vitriole broiet;	 If bleeding occurs, apply powdered vitriol to the wound.
et se li sans te vaint, si le cauterize au cautere lentiginout, qui est boin a ceu;	 And if the wound does not heal, cauterize it with the cautery of lentiginosum, which is good for this purpose.
puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez,	 Then treat it with another remedy until it heals,
et se tu lou vois de fusse color ou noir ou dur, si que li malaides ne lou sent, si n’i touchier point, car c’est chancre;	 And if you see a spot that is hard, black or dark, such that the patient does not feel it, do not touch it, for it is cancer.
et s’il est declinans a blenchor, et il i a moistor, si i giete l’oncine, et lou fent d’un spatumile subtil, et lou delivre d’une part et d’autre;	 If it is swelling and there is moisture, pour in onion juice using a thin spatula, then release it from both sides.
et se li sans te vaint a ton ovraige, si met sus vitriole broiet tant qu’il soit estainchiez, puis revien a ton ovraige tant que tu traies tout fuer;	 And if the bone protrudes at your work, place vitriol powder on it until it is cauterized, then return to your work when you have drawn out all fire.
puis leve lou leu d’aisil et de seil, et le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then lift the limb gently and carefully, and heal it with other treatments until it is healed.
des apostemes de la gorge	of throat abscesses
Aucune fois vient dedens la gorge boces qui sont apelees «godath», et les apele on proprement les II amandres, et quant tu les cures, si com nos avons dit en la division, et elles ne sont sanees, si pren garde:	 Sometimes boils called "godath" come up inside the throat. They are properly called "two almonds," and when you treat them as we have said in the division, and they are not healed, take care:
se c’est apostemes dur de petit sens et de fusse color, si ne lou touchier mie de fer.	 If it is a hard abscess of small size and darkish color, do not touch it with iron.
Et s’il est rouges et li racine est grosse, si ne lou touchier mie de fer, ausi por lou decorrement de sanc;	 And if it is red and the root is thick, do not touch it with iron, also for the flow of blood.
mais lou laisse tant qu’il soit meur, et adonques tu lou partiras, ou il rompirait par soi;	 But leave it until it is dead, and then you will separate it, or it would break by itself.
et s’il est de blainche color reont, et li racine est subtilz, si aies apareilliet l’estrument por coper, mais regarde premierement se li apostemes chalz repose et est apaisiez.	 If it is of white color and the root is thin, prepare the instrument for covering; but first check if the abscess is calm and soothed.
Adonques fai seoir lou malaide devant lou soleil, et ses chiés soit en ton sain, et li oevre la bouche et lou preigne li serjans entre ses mains, et presse la lengue desoz a tout l’estrument, de coi ci est li forme;	 Then make the patient sit in front of the sun, and his shoulders be on your side, and open his mouth and take hold of him by the sergeant between his hands, and press the tongue down onto the entire instrument, so that it takes this shape.
et soit d’argent ou d’arain subtil ausi com uns coutelz:	 And be made of silver or thin iron like a knife.
Cant tu presses la lengue a tout cest estrument, et tu vois l’aposteme, si pren l’oncine et lou fiche en l’amandre, et la trai fuer au desus plus que tu pues;	 Can you press the tongue onto the entire instrument, and if you see the abscess, take the probe and push it into the abscess and pull it upward more than you can.
et trai aucune chose des toiles avec, puis la cope a l’estrument, de coi ci est li forme, que semble unes forces;	 And draw no object from the cloth with it, then grasp it with the instrument, in this manner it is shaped, like a pair of pincers;
et toutevoie li chief sont corbé, et l’un endroit l’autre, et sont molt agut, et est fait de fer inde ou d’andainne:	 And if the neck is curved and bent to one side, and they are very sharp, made of iron or bone;
Et se tu n’as cest estrument present, si lou cope as tenailles, de coi ci est li forme:	And if you do not have this instrument present, hold the base with pliers, here is its shape:
Et soit trenchans d’une part, et d’autre part nom;	 It is called a traction on one side and a compression on the other;
et quant tu as copeit l’une des amandres, si cope l’autre selonc cele meisme maniere, et aprés l’incision gargarize li malaides aigue chaude, et aigue et aisil, et se decorremens de sanc avient, si gargarize li malaides aigue, ou escorces de pomes grenates soient cuites, ou fuelles de mirte, et semblans choses, tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	 And when you have grasped one of the nuts, grasp the other in the same manner, and after the incision, pour warm, hot, sharp, and sticky medicine on the patient, and if bleeding occurs, continue to pour warm medicine until the wound is sealed or cooked grape seeds are used, or pine needles, and similar things, until the wound is stopped.
puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	 Then, the care until it heals.
et aucune fois naissent en la gorge autres apostemes que les II amandres, si les cope donques ensi com les II amandres igament.	 And sometimes in the throat other abscesses than the two molars are born, so cut them as you would the two molars equally.
Et je medicinai une femme d’un aposteme que li estoit neis dedens la gorge, c’est a savoir I aposteme de petit sens;	 And I treat a woman of an abscess that was born within the throat, namely the abscess of small size;
et avoit jai bien pres close toute la gorge, si que li femme ne pooit expirer por le conduit qui estoit estoupez, et ne pooit ne mengier ne boivre, et fust morte s’elle demorast ensi I jor ou II.	 and had tightly closed the entire throat so that the woman could not exhale due to the narrowed passageway, and could neither eat nor drink, and would have died if she had remained thus for a day or two.
Et li apostemes estoit jai si montez qu’il avoit fuer mis II rains par les II pertuis dou neis.	 And the abscess was so swollen that it had been pressed in by two fingers through both nostrils.
Je hastai donques tantost, et fichai en l’un I oncine, puis lou traï fuers, et en traï grant porcion de bowe;	 Then I quickly made an incision in one of the armpits, and after that, I pulled it forcefully out, and removed a large piece of pus.
puis refis autreteil en l’autre pertus dou neis, et li ovrai la bouche et li pressai la lengue;	 Then reset another part on the other side of the neck, and open the mouth and press the tongue;
aprés fichai l’oncine en ces apostemes, et en copai une partie, et n’en issit fuers que un poc de sanc;	 After inserting the lance into these abscesses, and scraping a part of it, not more than a little blood was released.
et ensi fut destoupez li conduis de la gorge la femme, et comensa maintenant a boivre aigue et puis vin, et ne cessai de taillier de cel aposteme par lonc tens;	 And thus the woman's windpipe was cut open from the throat, and she began to drink water and then wine, and did not cease cutting into this abscess for a long time.
et li apostemes recroissoit adés, et remplissoit lou leu que je avoie vuidiet, tant qu’il refut mout gros;	 The abscess continued to grow again and filled the cavity that I had seen, becoming quite large.
adonques je l’engignai et lou cauterizai dedens la gorge:	 Then I trapped it and cauterized it within the throat.
ensi demora sens croistre;	 In this way, it stopped growing.
et me partis de ces parties, et ne soi que Deus fist de li aprés moi.	 And may these parts be divided, and let God restore them after I am gone.
de l’uve	of the eye
Quant reume dessent a l’uve, et elle est enflee et elle est longe, si est apelee «perpendiculaire»;	 When the rectum protrudes outwards and is long, it is called "perpendicular".
et s’elle est desoz grosse et reonde, si est apelee «uve».	 And if it is deep and round, it is called "bladder".
Quant elle est curee si com nos avons dit en la division, et li cure ne profite mie, et tu vois que li chaus apostemes est apaisiez, et elle est subtilz, si covient que tu la copes;	 If it is cured as we have said in the previous section, and the cure does not help, and you notice that the large abscess has subsided, and it becomes subtle, then you must cut it.
et celle qui est reonde assemblee et n’est mie longe;	 And the round one which is gathered together but not long;
et elle est sanguine ou de fusse color ou noire, si covient que tu eschues l’incision de li.	 And it is red or of pale color or black, then you must avoid cutting into it.
Car il i a grant peril sus lou malaide.	 For there is great danger for the patient.
Il covient donques, quant tu la vois, selonc la maniere que j’ai dit, de sa blenchor et de sa longesce, que tu faices seoir le malaide devant lou soleil, et li presse la lengue a l’estrument dont nos avons fait la remembrance ci devant;	 Then, when you see it, as I have said, according to its color and size, you must make the patient sit in front of the sun and press his tongue against the instrument that we have mentioned before.
puis fiche l’oncine en l’uve, et la trai desoz, et la cope a I des II estrumens que j’ai dit en l’incision des II amandres.	 Then push the onyx into the eye and pull it out, and tie it with the two instruments that I have mentioned in the incision of the two almonds.
Et covient que tu ne coper mie fuer que la superfluiteit qui est outre le termine natureil;	 And you must not cover anything that is beyond the natural limit.
car se tu en copes plus, si grieves a la voix, et a la parolle;	 because if you cover more, it will harm the voice and the speech.
et aprés l’incision, use de ceu que nos avons dit en l’incision des II amandres, et le cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	 And after the incision, use as we have said in the incision of the two arms, and treat it until it heals.
Et se li malaides a paor dou coper, si covient que tu i use d’engien a la cauterization de li sens paor.	 If the patient fears to be covered, then you must use an instrument for the cauterization of his fear.
Et li maniere dou cautere si est aigue ague.	 And the manner of the cautery is hot and sharp.
Et est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, et puis li presse la lengue a l’estrument que nos avons dit ou chapistre de cautere, et confis avec aigue vive chaus, si qu’elle ne soit mie trop espesse ne trop clere;	 The patient should place his head on your holy relic, and then press the tongue against the instrument as we have said in the chapter of caution, and bind it with hot, sharp iron, so that it is not too thick or too clear.
et en emple le chevement de cest estrument, de coi ci est li forme:	 and use the handle of this instrument, which has the following shape:
Et ait ou chief une cheveure ou om met la medecine, si com li chevemens d’une cuillier, et met l’estrument a tout la medicine sus l’uve;	 And have a head of hair where medicine is placed, like the handle of a spoon, and place the instrument over all the medicine above the eye.
et li malaides soit gisans sus son costeit, si que li salive et li muscillaige corre de sa bouche de la medicine dedens, si qu’ele ne dessende a la gorge, et lou blece;	 The patient should lie on his side so that the saliva and mucus flow from his mouth into the medicine, but not reach the throat or the wound.
puis tien ta main a tout la medicine et la presse sus l’uve, la quantiteit de la moitiet d’une houre, tant que tu la vois nercie et li mordications de la medicine soit apaisie;	 Then hold your hand on all the medicine and press on the eye for the quantity of half an hour, until you see it [the eye] shrink and the biting of the medicine is soothed.
et se tu vues, pren coton et l’envoloupe sus aucun estrument, et moille lou coton en la medicine, et boute l’estrument a tout le couton en la cainne desus, tant que li coton s’aerde sus l’uve;	 and if you see [something], take cotton and wrap it around some instrument, wet the cotton in the medicine, and press the instrument against all of the cotton on the eye socket, until the cotton adheres to the eyelid.
et fai ceu sovent, tant que li cauteres soit parfais, puis la laisse elle seche, et chiet aprés IIII jors ou V.	 and do this often, until the cautery is complete, then let it dry, and wash after four or five days.
Et se tu as mestier de rencomencier lou cautere de la medicine, si le rencomence, et aprés le cautere l’essue entor l’uve, de couton embut em burre, et mundifie ceu qui est entor de la medicine;	 And if you need to start the cautery again from the medicine, then start it, and after the cautery let water around the eye, with a cotton ball in butter, and clean what is around the medicine.
et soit arosez d’aigue froide, et soit curez de gargarismes tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And let it be cooled with cold water, and let it be cured with gargles until it is healed.
Ceste cure est plus save de l’incision, ne que li cautere;	 This cure is more effective than incision, not just the fire cautery;
s’elle est curee de fumigation selonc ceste maniere, pren calament et ysope et origanum et rue et camomille et avronne et semblans herbes, et les assemble toutes ou aucunes d’eles en I pot, et i met aisil, et fai bullir;	 if it is cured by fumigation in this manner, take calmant (calamint?), ysope, origanum (oregano), rue, camomille (chamomile), avronne (wormwood?) and similar herbs, and put them all or some of them together in a pot, and add asafetida, and boil it;
et li potz soit bien gluez de fort terre, et enmi le pot ait I estrument cheveit selonc ceste maniere:	 and the pot should be well sealed with strong clay, and in the pot there should be the instrument of hair according to this manner:
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain, et soit li uns des chiés boutez en la bouche dou malaide tant que li vapor monte a l’uve par la caine, tant que li uve soit mortifie;	 And it should be silver or gold, and one of the heads pushed into the patient's mouth until the vapors rise to the eye through the canal, until the eye is putrefied;
aprés lou rencomence sovent, tant que li uve seche, et garde que tu ne faices ceu au comencement de l’avenement de l’aposteme chaut, car plusors choses i avienent;	 Afterward, it often continues until the eye dries up, and ensure that you do not perform this at the beginning of an abscess's opening, for many things happen.
et ne faire mie ceu fuer que a la declination d’aposteme chaut.	 and not do this except in the decline of an abscess.
Et se cist estrument n’est presens, si pren une caine et met dedens lou chief une craiffe d’uef, si que li bouche au malaide n’ait mie trop chaut;	 And if this instrument is not present, take a tube and put an eggshell crack into the head so that the patient's mouth is not too hot.
car li craiffe d’uef ne lait mie la vapor grever la bouche, et c’est bone cure ensamble salut.	 because the eggshell does not let the vapor harm the mouth, and it is a good cure together with safety.
Maintes fois s’aert a la gorge os ou espinee de poisson, ou aucune chose;	 Many times it becomes lodged in the throat with bone or fish spine, or something similar.
si covient donc que tu traies ceu que tu pues veoir, et li presse la lengue au soleil a tout l’estrument, si que tu voies mues la chose;	 Therefore, it is necessary that you pull out whatever you can see, and press the tongue to the sun with all the instruments, so that you can see movements in the thing.
et ceu que ne t’apert mie et est reponus en la gorge, covient que tu faices vomir le malaide ainsois que li viande soit cuite en l’estomac;	 And whatever does not open and is lodged in the throat, it is necessary that you make the patient vomit as soon as the food is cooked in the stomach.
par aventure si istra li chose aerse par le vomissement;	 By chance if the thing escapes through vomiting.
ou li malaides englutisse une piece d’esponge, ou une piece de navel, ou une racine de laitue, ou I morceil de pain sec;	 Or if the patient swallows a piece of sponge, or a piece of naval, or a root of lettuce, or a piece of dry bread.
et lie a l’esponge I fil, et puis la transglutisse;	 And tie a thread to the sponge, and then make him swallow it.
et quant elle venra au leu, si s’aerdra, et puis trairas fuer;	 And when it reaches its place, if it hardens, then you will draw it out.
et s’elle ne vient fuer de ceu que nos avons dit, si pren I estrument de plonc selonc ceste forme:	 If it does not come out as we have said, then take the plunger according to this shape:
Et soit li estrumens corbés au chief si qu’il puist plus legierement entrer en la gorge, et ait le chief en haut leveit;	 And let the handle of the instrument be bent at the top so that it can enter more easily into the throat, and lift the head up.
et warde que tu ne touchier l’epiglote, que li tous ne li viegne, ne ne bouter mie l’os dedens;	 And watch that you do not touch the epiglottis, let it come slowly, and do not push the bone in.
et mues vaut que li malaides i boute l’estrument, por ceu qu’il seit mues ou li chose est aerse;	 It is better for the patient to insert the instrument, since they will move or the matter is urgent.
si la boute aval, ou il la traie fuer a tout l’estrument igalment, tant qu’elle soit fuer.	 If it goes down, or you pull it out with the whole instrument equally until it is out.
de la sansue de la gorge	the saliva of the throat
Aucune fois est medicinee li sansue, si com j’ai dit en la division, par la cure de medicines;	 Sometimes, sulphur is medicine, as I said in the division, through the use of medicines.
et quant ceu ne profite mie, adonques regarde en la gorge dou malaide au soleil, puis que tu li presses la lengue a l’estrument que je t’ai dit.	 And when that does not help, then look into the throat of the patient towards the sun, since you press his tongue with the instrument I told you about.
Et se tu vois la sansue, si la trai a tout I petit uncine, ou as tenailles subtilz que valent a ceu.	 If you see the saliva, take it away with a very small spoon, or fine tweezers that are suitable for this purpose.
Et se ceu ne vaut, si pren une caine chevee, et la boute en la gorge dou malaide, puis boute ou chevement de la caine I fer chaut, et fai ce sovent.	 If it is not successful, take a heated iron and put it in the throat of the sick person, then push or pull the iron up and down several times.
Et se teigne li malaides d’aigue toute jor.	 Make the patient drink water all day long.
puis pren plein I voirre d’aigue froide, et oevre la bouche, et la giete ens sens englutir, et la mueve a sa main sovent;	 then take a full eye dropper of cold water, open the mouth, and throw it in to swallow, and move it with your hand frequently.
et si tost com li sansue sent l’aigue, si chiet.	 and as soon as sulphur feels the water, it falls.
Et s’elle ne chiet si com nos avons dit, si subfumige lou malaide d’asefetide, a l’estrument que j’ai dit en la fumigation de l’uve;	 And if it does not fall as we said, sulphurize the patient with asafetida, using the instrument I told you about in the eye fumigation.
fai ceu maintes fois, car elle cherra sens targier.	 Do this many times, because it will require patience.
Et li maniere de la fumigation si est que tu preignes I pot ou il ait charbons vis, et soit li pos covert d’un coverseil perciet en mileu, et en celui pertus soit li chiés de l’estrument;	 And the method of fumigation is that you take the pot or it has charcoal in it, and cover it with a cover made from a perforated cloth in the middle, and put the head of the instrument in it.
puis i giete ta fumigation, et li malaides mette lou chief de la cainne en sa bouche, et cloie la bouche, si que li fumee n’en isse mie, mais viegne jusc’a la sansue;	 Then pour the fumigation, and the patient puts the head of the snake in his mouth, and closes the mouth so that the smoke does not escape but comes to the wound.
et la sansue cherra maintenant, et s’elle ne chiet, si rencomence la fumigation par maintes fois;	 and now the wound should bleed, and if it does not bleed, then repeat the fumigation many times;
et soffre li malaides soif, et menjuce choses salees et als, et ne boive point d’aigue;	 The patient suffers thirst, eats salty and raw food, and drinks no water.
et adonques li iert mestier qu’elle isse fuer par cest governement.	 And then it will be necessary for the wound to bleed through this method.
Et li forme de l’estrument a coi on trait la sansue, si est, quant on la puet veoir, semblans a tenailles corbés por mues entrer en la gorge;	 And the shape of the instrument with which one treats the vein, is, as it can be seen, similar to curved tweezers for entry into the throat.
et ait semblance au bec de soigne, et i ait asperiteit de lime, si que ceu qu’elle prent, elle ne puet lassier;	 and it has the shape of a probe, and it is covered in lime, such that whatever it grasps, it cannot release.
et vez ci la forme:	 here is its shape:
li chapistres des apostemes	The chapters on abscesses
Mout de semblances d’aposteme sont, selonc ceu que li remembrance vient ci aprés d’un et d’autre en cest livre, et sont diver en perforation et en taille;	 It has a similar form to an abscess, according to the remembrances that follow in this book, and they are various in piercing and cutting.
et c’est en II manieres dont l’une est en sa semblance meisme, et de ceu qu’il tient moistor.	 and it is in two ways: one of which resembles the same, and of that which it holds moisture.
Et li seconde maniere si est por les leus ou il sont au cors.	 And the second manner is for those that are in the body.
car li apostemes dou chief est autres que cil dou fondement, et li apostemes dou leu charnut est autres que cil qui vient en jointures, et chescuns ait son jugement en l’uevre.	 For abscesses of the head are other than those in the base, and abscesses in the hollow part of the bone are other than those that come at joints, and each should be judged according to its work.
Et si a apostemes c’on ne doit mie percier, tant que li bowe est meure selonc son acomplissement;	 And to abscesses, one should not pierce until the bowel is measured according to its completion;
et si a de telz qu’il covient percier quant il sont crut, et ne meurent mie selonc lor acomplissement, si com aposteme qui sont delez jointures.	 And if there are some that require piercing when they are ripe, and do not die according to their completion, like abscesses that have burst open from joints.
Car quant apostemes vient delez jointures, et on le laisse tant qu’il est porris entor, par aventure si sont corrumput li liien et li nerf de la jointure, par coi ce est cause de contraction en celui membre.	 When abscesses come to joints and are left until it is purged around them, by chance the ligament and nerve of the joint may become corrupt, which causes contraction in that member.
Ou li aposteme est delez lou membre principel, et se tu tardes la perforation tant qu’il soit meurez, si nuira au membre principeil;	 If the abscess is burst open at the main member, and you delay the piercing until it has decayed, it will harm the main member.
ou il est delez lou fondement, si le perce on ainsois qu’il soit meurs;	 if it has burst from the foundation, pierce it while it is still alive;
et ne covient mie que tu perces aposteme crut sens digestion acomplie, fuers que celui qui est delez lou fondement, qu’il ne porrisse em parfont, et soit alongiez dedens, et i viegne fistule;	 Do not pierce the abscess that is ripe without digestion completed, except for those which have burst from the foundation, it will not heal completely and a fistula will come.
et ne puisse saner en grant termine.	 and cannot heal in great time.
Et covient que tu saiches l’oure de la perforation de l’aposteme qui est meur selonc l’acomplissement, et c’est quant li dolor est apaisie, et li departemens de la fievre, et l’amenuisement de la dolor et de la roujor, et dou debatement et de l’aguisement dou chief de l’aposteme, et les autres signes;	 And you must know the hour of piercing the abscess that is ripe according to its completion, and it is when the pain is eased, and the disappearance of fever, the decrease in pain and redness, and the swelling and settling of the head of the abscess, and the other signs;
et covient que tu faices seoir la perforation ou plus dependant leu de l’aposteme, et la ou il apert mues;	 And you must make him sit with the perforation or closer to the abscess, and at the place where the wound has opened.
et soit li perforation dou lonc dou cors, et se li apostemes est as mains ou as piez, ou en jointures et au ners et as arteres, et en toz leus igalz ou il n’a point de ploieure.	 And the perforation should be along the length of the body, and if the abscess is in the hand or feet, or in joints and nerves and arteries, and in all places equal or without opening.
En ces que ploient, par selonc celui membre.	 In those who have swelling in such a member.
Et quant apostemes est en leu charnut, si vaut mues que tu laisses la perforation tant qu’il soit confermez en digestion acomplie, si com nos avons dit.	 And when an abscess is in a charred state, it is better to leave the perforation until it is confirmed by complete digestion, as we have said.
Car se tu lou perces devant ceu, si iert alongiez li cors dou venim de lui, et est plains de mout d’ordure;	 For if you pierce before that, it will be filled with the body's fluids and full of filth.
et par aventure endurcissent les levres et li parfondetez de lui.	 And by chance, harden the lips and plunge deep into it.
Et si a aucun aposteme que sont perciet selonc le large dou cors, selonc ceu que li membres en ait mestier.	 And if any abscess pierced in accordance with the body's width, according to what the limb needs.
Et covient que tu amenistres em petis apostemes, petis pertus;	 And you must bring small abscesses, small wounds.
et en grans apostemes, grans pertus, et maintes fendures selonc la semblance de la grandor de l’aposteme;	 and in large abscesses, large wounds, and many cuts according to the appearance of the size of the abscess.
et si a de tels apostemes ou il covient chever lou keur, et coper;	 And if there are such abscesses where it is necessary to cover and cure with lard, [that's the translation].
quant il est jai devenus ausi com I drapelz, et est amortis, si covient faire ausi com on fait as bubes:	 When it becomes like a cloth and is soaked, if necessary, do as one does with babies [that's the translation].
et si a de telz que sont fendut en III angles, et si a de telz dont on cope ausi com la fuelle de mirte, si com apostemes des angres;	 And if there are those which are split into three angles and those from which one cures as the furrow of a thorn-apple (mistletoe), like abscesses at joints: [that's the translation].
et si a de telz ou on fait une reonde taille, et autres tailles et semblant copeure.	 And if there are those where one makes a round incision and other similar incisions for curing.
Cil qui n’ont point de chief, si com aposteme souef superficial, il covient que tu lou perces plainnement;	 Those who have no head (like a superficial abscess), it is necessary that you pierce it fully [that's the translation].
et covient quant li apostemes est gros, et il a coillit grant bowe, et tu lou perces, si ne traire mie toute la bowe en celle houre, mais en trai une partie;	 When the abscess is large and it has collected much pus, if you pierce it, do not draw out all the pus in that hour, but only a part [that's the translation].
puis estoupe l’aposteme jusc’a l’autre jor, puis en trai aucune chose derechief;	 Then drain the abscess until the next day, then remove nothing wrong.
fai ceu par maintes fois de greit en greit, tant que li bowe isse toute;	 do it repeatedly for several days, until the bone is fully healed.
meismement se li malaides est de foible vertut, ou femme portans, ou petis enfes, ou viez hons decrepites.	 Similarly, if the patient is weak, or a woman, or small children, or old and decrepit men.
Car li esperis tressaut aucune fois avec l’issue de la bowe, que par aventure muert li malaides, et tu ne t’en persois.	 The sphincter sometimes jerks with the discharge of pus, which may accidentally cause the death of the patient, but do not worry about it.
Eschuez donques cest chapistre par grant cautele, et quant tu as perciet ton aposteme, si essue la plaie, et regarde se li plaie de l’aposteme est petite;	 Therefore, be careful with this chapter, and when you have pierced the abscess, suck the wound, and check if the wound from the abscess is small.
et se c’est une tailleure plainne, si amenistre tentes de lin ou de viez coton;	 and if it is a deep wound, bring linen or old cotton.
et se c’est uns grans apostemes, et il i a mout de pertus, si covient que tu boutes en chescun une tente si qu’ele viegne l’une contre l’autre;	 and if it is a large abscess and there is much pus, then you must insert one linen or cotton swab in each until they meet.
et se tu as copeit en l’aposteme une partie dou cuir, et tu l’as cheveit entor, si covient que tu l’emplisses de viel couton ou de rasure de dras de lin sens moistor, et le lie jusc’au tier jor;	 If you have dug into the abscess a part of the skin, and you have shaved around it, you must fill it with old cloth or linen thread without moisture, and tie it for two days.
puis l’oste, et le cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then, remove the bone, and cure it with ointment until it heals.
Et se decorremens de sanc avient a ton ovraige, si amenistre aigue froide et aisil, et moille I drapeil, et met sor le leu decorrant par maintes fois.	 And if bleeding occurs in your work, apply cold water and vinegar, wet the linen cloth, and place it on the wound repeatedly.
Et se li decorremens de sanc persevere, se i amenistre governement et cure, et les poudres que j’ai dit em mains leus en cest livre, et se c’est ou tens d’iver, et li leus ou li apostemes est est mout nervous, si couvient que tu mettes sus tentes et drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile chaut;	 If the flow of blood persists, apply governance and cure, and the powders I have mentioned in this book should be placed on the muscles or abscesses when they are very nervous. If it is winter time, and the area or abscess is very tense, you must place hot blankets and dampened woolen cloths on top of them.
et se c’est en esteit, et li leus est charnus, si covient que tu mes sus drapelz moilliez en aigue et en oile, ou en vin et en oile froit, jusc’au tier jor, si com nos avons dit;	 And if it is summer, and the area is fatty, you must place hot blankets and dampened woolen cloths soaked in water and oil or cold wine on top of it for two days as we have said.
et puis deslie l’aposteme et l’essue et le cure, si com il covient, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And then drain the abscess and the pus and heal, as necessary, until it is healed.
Et ceu covient il conoistre universement en cures des apostemes:	 It is necessary to understand universally in the treatment of abscesses:
or vos ai dit coment on doit aler avant as cures des apostemes, et vez ci le chapistre.	 Or have I told you how one should go before the treatment of abscesses, and here is the chapter.
des soros	boils
Ou keur dou chief vienent petis apostemes, et sont manieres de nous que sont en toiles, ausi com li josier d’une geline, et mout en i a de semblances.	 For small abscesses coming on the head, our practice is that they are wrapped in cloths, like the one who prunes a vine, and there are many similarities.
Il en i a de gras et de telz ou il a moistor ausi com poulz;	 There are some that are fat and others with moisture like boils.
et si a de telz qui sont dur et pierous au taillier, et n’i a point de doutance se li artere n’i fait contraire.	 And there are those who are hard and stony at the base, and there is no doubt that the arteries will not oppose.
Et li ovraiges de la taille si est que tu esprueve a tout I estrument qui est apelez «entromissoire», de coi li forme vient ci aprés, quel chose il contient.	 And the operations of the cut are that you try every instrument that is called "intermissory," from which the form comes later, what it contains.
Car s’il contient moistor, si lou fent par desus dou lonc.	 For if it contains moisture, they make an incision along its length.
Et quant li moistor est vuidie, si escorche sens rien laissier la peil qui contient celle moistor, car il revient adés quant on i laisse rien;	 And when the moisture is evacuated, scrape everything without leaving any hair that contains the moisture, because it will return again if you leave anything.
puis plonge coton en oignement egiptien, s’il est presens;	 Then dip cotton in Egyptian ointment if available;
se ceu non, en aigue et en seil, et en emple la plaie, et la laisse jusc’a l’autre jor;	 if not, use water and salt, and apply it to the wound until the next day;
et ceu corront ceu qui est demorez dou nit.	 and let those who are delayed by night stay on it.
Et pues rencomence lou coton, si com devant, le second jor, et lou tier, tant que tu saiches bien qu’il ne demoure point dou nit;	 Then repeat the cotton as before, on the second day and the third, until you know that it does not remain by night.
puis cure la plaie d’oignement a ceu convenauble, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 then treat the wound with suitable ointment until it is healed.
Et se li apostemes tient I nout gras, si le cope selonc ceste forme, dou lonc;	 And if the abscess persists without fat, squeeze it according to this shape, long;
et i giete tes oncines, et l’escorche de toutes pars, et met toute ta cure de traire fuer la cotte ou il gist;	 and throw your fingers into it, and remove all the scabs from all parts, and put all your care to draw out pus from where it lies.
et se li artere te fait contraire, si fai ceu que je t’ai dit aprés.	 And if the arteries oppose it (the dislocation), do as I have told you afterwards.
Et ausi fai de l’aposteme s’il est pierous, et dou taillier et dou curer si com je t’ai dit.	 And likewise treat an abscess that is hard, and cut and heal it as I have told you.
Et li taille sus l’aposteme pierous et le moiste, si est plus legiere, car il sont de poc de sanc.	 Cut through the hard abscess and moisten it, as it will be easier, for there is little blood.
Et si a aucuns de ces apostemes ou chief ou il n’a point de moistor, et de ces fut I apostemes que je copai ou chief d’une vielle femme;	 And if any of these abscesses or head has no moisture, and among those was the abscess that I cut from an old woman's head;
et trovai l’aposteme ausi com une piere xourde, aspre et blainche, et ne pooit brisier;	 And I found the abscess as hard as a stone, rough and white, and could not break it.
et s’on en eust ferut aucun, on li eust ausi bien fait plaie com d’une piere.	 And if one had stabbed it with a knife, it would have caused as much damage as being hit by a stone.
En autres apostemes venans ou chief, fuer que ces qui vienent as chief des enfans et as racines des oreilles, li overture si soit toz jors au plus dependant leu, por mues issir la bowe;	 In other abscesses that are near the head or at the roots of the ears, they should be opened always depending on the situation, in order to help the boil come out.
et les cure si com il covient.	 And heal them as necessary.
des scrophules	of scrofula
Maintes fois avienent cist aposteme au col, et desoz les asseles, et ens angres, et aucune fois vienent autre part ou cors, et sont mout, et sont enjanrees l’une avec l’autre.	 Often this abscess occurs at the neck, and under the armpits, and in groins, and sometimes they come from other places on the body, and they are large and connected to each other.
Et chescune scrophule est proprement dedens sa cote, si com li nout et li aposteme dou chief, si com nos avons dit;	 Each scrofula is properly within its side, as the abscess of the head and the boil at the roots of the ears, as we have said.
et les semblances de ces scrophules sont maintes.	 And the appearances of these scrofulas are many.
Il i a de teles que contienent moistor, et si a de malignes qui ne vuellent obeir a santeit.	 Some contain moisture, and some are malicious and refuse to obey health.
en celle donques que tu vois de bone disposition au tochier, et est semblans a la color dou cors, et muet de chescune part et n’est mie aerse as ners dou col ne a l’artere ne au conduit, et n’est mie parfonde;	 In that case, you see it well-placed at the neck, and similar in color to the body, silent on all sides and not pulsating in the neck nor the artery nor the vein, and not deep.
si covient que tu la copes par desus, et l’escorche de chescune partie, et estent les II levres dou keur as oncines, se tu en as mestier, si com nos avons dit en apostemes dou chief;	 Then you must cut it across from above, and strip the skin of each part, and apply the two lips of the curette to the edges, if needed, as we have said in head abscesses.
et la trai poc et poc, et soies seur que tu ne coper lou nerf ne la voine, et ne soit mie li spatumile agus ne trenchans, que li mains n’eschaipe, et ne voise trop avant, que tu ne coper mie ceu que tu ne dois.	 pull it slowly and carefully ensure that you do not cut the nerve or vein, and be neither too sharp nor cutting too deep, so as not to injure the hand, and look ahead so as not to cut more than necessary.
Et se tu copes la voinne ou l’artere, et ceu ne te laisse ovrer, si met en la plaie vitriole broiet, ou aucunes poudres que restainchent sanc, et estraint la plaie;	 And if you cut the vein or the artery, and it does not let you be over it, put vitriol powder in the wound, or any powders that stop bleeding, and hold the wound closed.
et la laisse tant que li apostemes soit apaisiez, et soit amollie li plaie, et encomence a porrir.	 And let it be until the abscess is calmed down, and the wound softened, and begins to rot.
Et quant li sans est estainchiez, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que tu l’acomplisses;	 And when the blood has stopped flowing, return to your work, until you finish it.
puis quier a ton doit indice s’il i demoure nules petites scrophules, si les cope et les munde.	 Then look for yourself if there remain small scrofulas, and cut them off and wash them.
Et s’il a en la racine de la scrophule voinne grant, si ne covient mie que tu copes celle scrophule en sa racine, mais la lie d’un fil double fort, et la laisse cheoir par li, sens nuisement;	 And if there is a vein in the root of the scrofula large open, it is not necessary that you cut that scrofula at its root, but tie it with a strong double thread and let it hang out, without harm.
puis emple la plaie de viel coton plongiet en oignement egiptien, puis la cure.	 Then use old cotton dipped in Egyptian ointment on the wound, then heal it.
Et se tu copes toute la scrophule, si covient que tu assembles les II levres de la plaie, et les cout maintenant, puis qu’il n’i a point demoreit de superfluiteit por la grandor de la scrophule.	 If you excise the entire scrofula, you must gather the two edges of the wound and sew them up now because there is no room for excess due to the size of the scrofula.
si covient que tu entendes a coper la racine de li, et traire fuer, et la cout si com nos avons dit.	 You must understand how to cover the root and draw pus, then sew as we have said.
Celles scrophules que tienent superfluiteit, perce lai ou il apert meure;	 For boils that have become excessive, pierce where they are softened to open.
et la perce ensi com celle devant dite, en dependant, puis i amenistre tentes avec oignement et semblans choses, si qu’elle corrompe ceu qui est demorez de la corruption;	 and pierce it as described before, depending on it, then introduce tents with ointment and similar things to corrupt that which remains of the corruption.
et quant li plaie est bien mundee, si la cure d’oignement enjanrant char, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And when the wound is well cleaned, heal it with fragrant ointment until it is healed.
de squinance	If the scrotum becomes inflamed and swollen, apply a poultice to it made from crushed barley, wine, and oil. Repeat this process daily for three days.
Li ancien dirent et parlerent de la tailleure de la gorge;	 The ancients spoke of the shape of the throat;
mais je ne vis onques en nostre terre qui la feist, et c’est li escripture de lor parole.	 but I have never seen it done in our land and it is the writing of their speech.
A ces qui ont squinance, il covient que li fendure de la gorge qui est apelee «epiglote» soit eschuee;	 To those who have scrofula, it is necessary that the division in the throat called "epiglotte" be cut open.
et c’on ne faice aide par ceu, por ceu que toutes les voines et li pormon dou malaide sont a ces qui ont aposteme chaut en la bouche, ou en la gorge ou en II amandres.	 And no help can be given through it, because all the veins and the opening of the patient's mouth are located in those who have an abscess hot in the mouth, or in the throat or in both cheeks.
Quant li maladie est en la chenal dou pormon, il covient coper l’epiglote por fuir la perdition qui vient de l’estranglement.	When the sickness is in the channel of the parotid gland, it is necessary to cover the epiglotte to avoid the strangulation that comes from the swelling.
Il covient donques, quant nos volons fendre l’epiglote, que nos le fendons desoz III cercles ou IIII une petite fendure dou travers, entre les II cercles ou par la quantiteit de la fendure dou syfac, ne mie en la cartillaige;	 Therefore, when we want to cut the epiglottis, it should be cut beneath three circles or four, a small slit through the center, between the two circles, or by the amount of the cut according to the size of the slit, not in the cartilage.
et cil leus si est covenaubles a la section de l’epiglote qu’il n’i a point de char, et li vasseil sont lonc d’enqui.	 And if the throat is susceptible to the section of the epiglottis, there should be no cartilage and the vessels are long in length.
Et se li maistres est paourous, si covient qu’il estende le cuir de la gorge a tout l’oncine, puis fende lou keur tant qu’il viegne a la cheneil;	 And if the master is fearful, it should extend the skin of the throat to its entire length, then cut open the wound until it reaches the trachea.
et eschue les vasselz de sanc, se tu vois aucune chose, et puis cope lou syfac, si com nos avons dit;	 And shake out the vessels of blood, if you see anything, then press the syringe, as we have said.
et est demostrez par la section dou fleume de la cheneil ki saut fuer par le leu qui est rompus, et par la defaute de la voix;	 And it is demonstrated by the section of the femoral vein that bursts through a broken limb and by the absence of voice.
et laisse la plaie overte une piece.	 Leave the wound open for a piece [of time].
Et quant li houre est passee de coi on doute l’estranglement, assemble les II levres de la plaie dou keur, et la cout toute soule sens la cartillaige;	 And when the hour has passed where there is doubt of strangulation, bring together the two lips of the wound with care, and stitch it all closed except for the cartilage.
puis aministre medicines qui font naistre char, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then administer medicines that cause growth of flesh, until it is healed.
Albucasim dist c’on ne faice ce jusc’a tant que li gorge est toute estoupee, et li malaides est jugiez a mort, et li defaut li alaine.	Albucasim says not to do this until the throat is completely stopped up, and the patient is judged dead, and the flight has fled.
Adonques cope on l’epiglote por ceu que li malaides ne puet alener, et il respire par la plaie, et ensi est gardez de mort;	 Then press the epiglottis because the patient cannot swallow, and he breathes through the wound, thus keeping him from death.
et por ce commanderent li anciain a laissier la plaie overte tant que li malice de la maladie soit passee, et elle est passee en III jors ou en IIII Et adonques il comanderent a coudre la plaie et curer, tant qu’elle fut curee;	 And so, the ancients commanded to leave the wound open until the malice of the disease had passed, and it had passed in 3 days or 4. And then they commanded to stitch up the wound and heal it, until it was healed.
et je vos dirai ceu que je vis.	 And I will tell you what I saw.
Je vis que une damoisele prist I coutel, et le ficha en sa gorge, et copa partie des chenelz dou pormon;	 I saw a maiden take a dagger and stab it in her throat, cutting part of the windpipe.
et je fui apelez por li curer, et la trovai ausi com morte.	 And I was called to heal her, and found her as dead.
Je descovris la plaie, et trovai le sanc qui en estoit issus, et soi bien qu’elle n’avoit mie copeit voine ne conduit fuer que la gorge, et li vens issoit fuer par la plaie.	I discovered the wound, and found the blood coming out of it, and knew that she had not breathed or spoken except through her throat, and the wind was flowing through the wound.
Je me hastai, et cousi la plaie, et la curai tant qu’elle fut sanee;	 I hurried, and sewed up the wound, and healed it until it was cured;
et n’avint a la damoisele fuer qu’elle fut roge de voix, et revint aprés a sa disposition;	 And nothing more happened to the maiden but she regained her voice, and returned to her normal state.
por ceu di je que en la tailleure de l’epiglote n’ait mie paour.	 Therefore I say, have no fear during the operation on the epiglottis.
de la grosse gorge	of the large throat
Cist apostemes est apelez «hernie de gorge», et est uns grans apostemes en color d’une jaisse, et est molt en femmes;	 This abscess is called "hernia of the throat," and is a large one of a greenish color, and it occurs mainly in women.
et est selonc II manieres:	 It appears in two ways:
naturez, et accidens;	 Nature and accidents;
ou natureil n’a point d’engien.	 And an artificial remedy has no effect.
Et li accidens est selonc II manieres, de coi l’une est semblans a gras nous, et li autre maniere est semblans a aposteme qui vient de nous d’artere;	 And accidents are of two kinds, one is similar to fat, and the other kind is similar to an abscess coming from the artery.
et il i ait paour, et ne covient mie ovrer de feir fuers que en celi qui est petite, et le prueve et cerche a tout l’intromissoire:	 and there is fear, and it should not be worked on forcefully except in small cases, and it must be proved and sought after thorough examination of the patient.
se tu le trueves ausi com I nout gras, et ne pent a nulle voine, si le cope, si com on cope les nous, et le trai a tout sa coife, s’il en i a point;	 if you find it like fat, and it cannot be opened in any way, then crush it, as one crushes a boil, and drag it out entirely, if there is anything.
et encerche bien tot, et le cure si com il covient, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	 examine it thoroughly, and heal it as required, until it is completely healed.
des nous	from us (we)
Maintes manieres de nous sont, dont je dirai toutes les semblances;	 Many methods concerning us there are, which I shall describe all their likenesses;
et or covient que je die toute la difference qui est entre nout et issue.	 and it is necessary that I say the whole difference that exists between knot and dislocation.
Je dis que issue est chalors et fievre tenans, tant que li ebulicions est passee, et est acomplie li porriture;	 I say that dislocation is heat and fever persisting until the ebullition has passed, and the boil has healed.
adonques repose li fievre et li chalor.	 Then the fever and the heat subside.
Avec lou nout n’a ne chalor ne fievre ne dolor, et contient I syfac, qui est ses propres sac et est selonc la color dou cors, et encomence ausi com une jaisse, et devient gros;	 With the knot there is no heat, nor fever, nor pain, and it contains the pus, which is its own sack and is according to the color of the body, and begins in the same way as a boil, and becomes swollen.
et sont selonc II semblances, ou grais, ou moiste, et mout de color sont si com j’ai dit en la division.	 and they are according to these likenesses, whether fatty or moist, and their colors are similar as I said in the classification.
Il covient, quant tu viens a la cure dou nout, que tu esprueves et l’enquier premierement a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «entromissoire», selonc ce que sa forme venra ou chapistre qui est aprés.	It is necessary, when you come to the treatment of the nose, that you examine and inquire first about all the instruments called "entromissoire", according to their shape and the chapter that follows.
Et li maniere de l’inquisicion des apostemes des nous est que tu preignes ou plus moiste leu que tu trueves en l’aposteme, et torne tes dois poc et poc, tant que tu saiches que li estrumens ait perciet le keur, puis que ce soit selonc la grandor de l’aposteme;	 And the method of incising abscesses for us is to take the moistest place found within the abscess and turn your fingers little by little, until you feel that the pus has been pierced, then as the size of the abscess dictates.
puis estrai l’entromissoire, et pren garde en ceu que saut fuer.	 Then remove the contents, and be careful to ensure it does not burst.
Se moistor corrans cort, queil color elle ait, si le fent si com j’ai dit des autres apostemes;	 If moisture flows out of a cold abscess, let it have its natural color as I said for other abscesses.
et se aprés l’entromissoire nen vient moistor, saiches qu’il est gras, si le fent donques en croix, et le prent as pinceures, et l’escorche legierement de chescune part et warde la cotte ou il gist que tu la traies saine avec le nout;	 And if no moisture comes out after removing the contents, know that it is fatty; then make a cross-shaped incision, take pincers to it and gently peel back from both sides and draw the skin or coat that you pull out safely with the knot.
et se tu ne la pues traire saine, si la trai par pieces si qu’il n’i demoure rien.	 And if you cannot draw it out whole, draw it out piece by piece so that nothing remains.
Car s’il i demoure rien, si revient li nous par maintes fois;	 For if something remains, it comes back to us many times;
et s’il en demore un poc, et li sans te grieve, si emple la plaie d’aucunes poudres corrosives agues, et estraint la plaie, et met sus choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	 and if a little bit remains and it does not trouble you, apply the wound with some corrosive powders, hold the wound closed, place warm things on the abscess to reduce it, and treat it with other treatments until it is healed.
et se li nous est grans, si cout les II levres de la plaie, et le cure de ceu qui enjanre char.	 And if it is large, cut the two lips of the wound, and treat it with lard.
et se li voine batans t’est contraire ou autre si te haste et emple le leu de vitriole broiet, et lou laisse liiet II jors ou III, tant que li plaie porrisse, et repose li ebulicion dou sanc;	 And if the vein is beaten against you or something else happens quickly and you have no vitriol at hand, use crushed glass and leave it for 2 or 3 days until the wound festers, and let the boiling of the blood subside.
puis revien au coper ceu que i est demoreit dou nout.	 Then return to cover what has stayed with the knot.
Vez ci les formes des estrumens entromissoires, et sont de III manieres:	 Here are the shapes of the intermediary tools, and they are of three kinds:
grans et moien et petit;	 large, medium, and small;
et s’en i a III quarrez qui sont apelez «albaret», et I qui est apelez «breb», et s’en i a de III manieres:	 And there are three squares that are called "albarets", and one which is called "breb", and there are three kinds of them:
grant, moien, et petit, por encerchier les apostemes de fistule;	 large, medium, and small, to surround the abscesses with fistula.
et sont ausi com les aguilles dont on cout les sorceles, et sont d’arain citrin, ou de fer, ou d’argent, et mues valent cil qui sont jaune, et sont plus esprovez de plonc noir por encerchier les corbeures de fistule;	 and they are like needles used to sew sacks, and made of citron wood, iron, or silver, and those that are yellow are worth more, and they are more skilled at closing black corborellous (a type of abscess).
et sont de III manieres:	 large, medium, and small, to surround the abscesses with fistula.
grans, moiens, et petis, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce des pertus.	 large, medium, and small, according to the size of the holes (pertus).
Les formes des oncines sont de mout de semblances, si com tu vois ci:	 The shapes of onions are quite similar, as you can see here:
grans, moiens, et petis;	 Large, medium, and small [objects or items]
et si a oncines qui ont II corbeures de III manieres ausi;	 and if the ones having three curvatures of three kinds [are present];
et si a oncines qui ont III corbeures, et sont ausi de III manieres;	 and if the ones having three curvatures and are also of three kinds are present;
et si a oncines qui ont II corbeures, et oncines d’une corbeure soulement, et sont de III manieres;	 and if the ones having two curvatures, and the ones with one curvature only, and are of three kinds are present.
et tuit cist sont necessaire en lor leu.	 And all these are necessary in their place.
Li chief de ces a coi on fent sont trenchant, et de telz i a qui ne taillent mie fuer que d’une part, dont on escorche les nous, por ceu c’on ne cope la voine ne le nerf;	 The head of these tools with which we cut are sharp, and of those who do not cut at all except from one side, from which we scourge the nerves, because one does not hit the vein or the nerve.
et de ces intromissoires sont les alemeles reponues en mainches, si que li malaide ne s’en persoivent a l’overture des apostemes;	 and of these instruments are the stirrups held in loops, so that the patient does not injure himself when opening abscesses.
et sont de III manieres:	 And they are of three kinds:
grant, petit, et moien, si com tu vois;	 large, small, and medium, as you can see;
et n’en use on mie fuer que en leu charnut, si com jambes, et bras, et mameles, et as angres, et en semblans leus;	 do not use them except in the case of swellings such as arms, legs, breasts, and wounds, and similar places.
et aucune fois fait on I autre estrument petit, semblant a escorces de fistices, selonc ceste forme, a coi on estainche sanc:	 And sometimes another small instrument is used, similar to the incision of blisters, following this shape, to drain blood.
et le met on aucune fois au leu qui saine a copement des voines, et as arteres, et aucune fois reont selonc ceste grant forme:	And one applies it [the cautery] sometimes to the place that is healthy to close veins and arteries, and sometimes in this large shape:
Aucune fois enflent les mameles d’aucuns homes quant cil encomencent estre corrumput, tant qu’eles semblent mameles de feme;	 Sometimes breasts of some men swell when they begin to become corrupt, until they resemble women's breasts.
et demorent laides et enflees, et qui les vuet curer, si le covient soier selonc ceste forme des ceste ligne .b. jusques a .g.:	 and remain ugly and swollen, and whoever wishes to cure them, it must be done according to this form of the line b. up to g:
puis escorche la graisse, et emple la plaie de medicine enjanrant char, puis assemble les II levres de la plaie a costure, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee;	 then cut the fat and apply the wound with medicinal herbs warming charcoal, then bring together the two lips of the wound to stitch it up, and heal it until it is healed.
et se li mamele cline aval, et est amolie por sa grandor si com il avient as femmes, si la fent en II costelz desus, par II semblans fendures;	 And if the breast (mammele) slants downwards and is flattened due to its size, as happens with women, then split it into two halves above, through two similar cuts.
de coi l’une soit tenans a l’autre a la fin de l’une et de l’autre, si que li plus grans ligne conteigne la menor selonc ceste forme, des ceste ligne .b. jusc’a la ligne .g.;	 thus one part remains connected to the other at the end of both, so that the larger line contains the smaller according to this form, from this line 'b' to line 'g'.
puis escorche le cuir qui est entre les II levres, et oste la graisse, et i amenistre ceu que nos avons dit de costure et de poudres, et ceu qui est necessaire en la cure, tant qu’il soit sanez;	 then scrape the skin that is between the two lips, remove the fat, and introduce what we have said about stitching and powders, and whatever is necessary in the treatment, until it heals.
et s’il n’est sanez, ou li incision n’est mie toute faite, por ceu que li malaides ne vuet reposer, ou por le decorrement de sanc, si covient que tu emplisses la plaie de coton moilliet en oignement corrosif;	 and if it is not healed or the incision is not fully made because the patient does not want to rest, or due to bleeding, then you must fill the wound with moist cotton in a corrosive ointment.
et le laisse tant qu’il menjuce le remenant et la graisse, puis le cure tant qu’il soit saneis.	 And leave it (the affected area) until it drains the remaining flesh and fat, then treat it until it is healed.
des apostemes des asselles	From abscesses in the buttocks
Cist apostemes que vienent desoz les asseles sont manieres de scrophules dures ou il ait cotes, et s’en i a que contienent moistor.	These abscesses coming from under the buttocks are managed as hard scrofulas where they contain moisture.
Cil donques qui contienent moistor covient qu’il soient copez selonc ceste forme, des la ligne .b. jusc’a la ligne .g.:	 Therefore, those containing moisture must be cut according to this form, from the line b up to the line g:
Et quant toute li bowe qui est en l’aposteme est vuidie, si emple la plaie de viel coton, et la laisse jusc’a l’autre jor, puis oste tout le coton, et cure d’oignement avenant a ceu tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when the entire hole that is in the abscess is emptied, fill the wound with old cotton and leave it until the next day, then remove all the cotton, and anoint it afterwards until it heals completely.
Et se li apostemes est de semblances de scrophules, si le fent si com nos avons dit en fendures des scrophules, et se li plaie rent bowe, si amenistre cautere si com nos avons dit devant.	And if the abscess resembles scrofula (scrofula is a chronic disease that causes swelling of the lymph nodes), then make an incision as we have said in the treatment of scrofula, and if the wound opens up, apply fire cautery as we have said before.
de la routure de l’artere	The severing of an artery.
Quant li artere est route, et li cuir est soudez qui est sus, si en vient maintes fois apostemes, et tout aussi avient il a la voine enflee et aposteme;	 When the artery is blocked and the skin above it becomes adhered, there are often abscesses, and this also happens at the swollen vein with an abscess.
et si le conoist on ensi quant c’est por l’artere, si est li apostemes lons em parfont;	 And if it is known in such a way that it is due to the artery, then the abscesses are long and deep.
et quant tu le sens a tes dois, si sens I estraignement;	 And when you feel it with your hands, pull it slowly;
et quant c’est por la voine, si est reons defuer aparans;	 and if it is through the vein, then it should appear in front.
et c’est folie de coper cest aposteme, et meismement quant il est desoz les asseles et as angres et ou col et em mout d’autres leus, et est mout grans.	 and it is foolishness to cover this abscess, especially when it is under the flesh and near the joints and neck and in many other places, and it is very large.
Il covient donques eschuir la cure de fer, et celui qui est a chief covient eschuir ausi, et en celui qui est d’enfleure d’artere fent par desus le cuir dou lonc;	 Therefore, one must use iron treatment, and for those with head problems, the same applies, and in those who have a swelling of an artery, make an incision above the skin long enough;
puis oevre la taille as oncines, et depart bellement l’artere des toiles, tant qu’ele soit descoverte;	 then open the wound at one place and carefully separate the artery from the veins until it is exposed.
puis boute desoz li une aguille, et la fai percier jusc’a l’autre costeit, et estraint l’artere d’un fil double en II leus, selonc ceu que je t’ai ensigniet en l’estraction des II arteres qui sont en temples;	 then insert an awl under it and make it pierce up to the other side, and tie the artery with a double thread in two places, as I have shown you in the extraction of the two arteries that are in the temples.
puis point le leu qui est entre les II liens d’un intromissoire tant que li sans en isse qui i est, et soit deliiez li aposteme;	 Then move the joint between the two ligaments of an intromissoir as far as the sanz isses allows, and release the abscess.
puis amenistre la cure que enjanre bowe, tant que li liien chient;	 then apply the cure that induces a bough, while the ligament is shaking.
puis cure ceu d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	 then cure him with ointment after that, while he is healthy.
et se li apostemes est por la taille de la voinne, si covient que tu teignes a ta main ceu que tu pues de l’aposteme a tout le cuir, puis boute l’aguille desoz le leu que tu tiens a ta main, et la fai percier, et i ait I fil double, si que tu le trais de l’autre costeit;	 and if the abscess is due to a wound in the vein, then you must dye your hand that part of the abscess on the entire skin, then push the needle under the joint that you hold with your hand, and make it pierce, and let it have double thread, so you can draw it from the other side.
puis lie l’aposteme, si com je t’ai dit, ou liien de l’une de II pars as II chiés dou fil;	 then tie the abscess, as I told you, or bind one of the two parts of the ligament with thread.
