et se tu doutes que li filz n’isse fuer, si i reboute une autre aguille a tout I fil desoz tout l’aposteme a l’incision de la premiere aguille, et estraint les filz en IIII leus;	 And if you doubt that the thread has gone in fully, push another needle all the way through under the abscess at the incision of the first needle and hold the thread in four places;
puis cope l’aposteme tant que li superfluitez en isse, puis cope la superfluiteit dou keur et laisse ceu qui est liiez;	 then squeeze the abscess until the pus comes out, then squeeze the hard part and leave what is connected;
puis met sus I drapeil moilliet en vin et en oile, puis li amenistre cures de tentes et d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then place a damp cloth soaked in wine and oil on it, then apply remedies of poultices and liniments until it heals.
des apostemes des ners	Of abscesses from nerves
Ausi com aposteme vienent en l’artere et en la voine, vienent aposteme as ners quant il sont ferut, ou par trop grant travail, et semblans choses.	As abscesses come in the artery and vein, they come on nerves when wounded, or from too much labor, and similar things.
Et ceu avient plus sovent as adjutoires et as dois et en toz leus ou il ait jointures, et c’est I grief apostemes, et sa color semble la color dou cors, et est em plusors dispositions sens dolor;	 This happens more often in the shoulder and the thighs where there are joints, and it is severe abscesses, and its color resembles the body's color, and it is in various conditions with pain;
et quant on l’estraint forment, si sent li malaides dolor, et n’est mie em parfont dou cors, mais desoz lou keur;	 And when it is being reset, the patient feels pain, but not fully within the body, but beneath the skin.
et muet bien de toutes pars, et ne va ne avant ne arrier, ne desoz ne desus, et celui qui est en jointures ne covient mie coper par fer:	 And it should be completely immobile in all directions, neither forward nor backward, nor beneath nor above, and the one in joints should not be covered by iron.
par aventure i vanroit contraction;	 It may contract by chance.
et cil qui est ou chief ou ou front, fent le cuir au spatumile.	 And if it is at the head or forehead, make the skin with the spatula.
Se li apostemes est petis, si le tien a unes tenailles, et le cope en sa racine;	 If the abscess is small, hold it with forceps and strike its root.
et s’il est grans, si le sospent a l’oncine, et l’escorche, puis l’oste et assemble la plaie a la costure, et lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And if it is large, suspend it at the incision, peel it, then extract the bone and close the wound with stitches, and let the cure continue until it heals.
des grosses boces pendans	Hanging large lumps
Aucune fois avient en ventres et ne mie autre part thelul, et est une maladie qui est apelee «funge» par la semblance d’aus, et est li racine subtilz, et li chiez gros;	 Sometimes happens in bellies and nowhere else, and it is a disease called "fungus" because of its resemblance to mushrooms, and the roots are subtle, and the heads are large.
et en i a de petis et de mout grans;	 and there are some small ones and very large ones.
et je vis I home qui en avoit II ou ventre qui estoient plus semblans a funges que ai autre chose, et n’i avoit point de difference, et estoient blanc, et avoient menue racine, et estoient jai fendut, et en corroit adés moistor.	 and I have seen a man who had two bellies that resembled mushrooms more than anything else, and there was no difference between them, and they were white, and had small roots, and were cut open, and ran moisture continuously.
Je les copai et trovai en l’un XVIII onces pesant, et en l’autre VI З., et li ovraiges en l’incision si est que tu regardes se li malaides est moistes, et li color de l’artelul est blainche et moiste et de subtil racine;	 I weighed them and found one weighing 18 ounces, and the other 6, and the work in the incision shows that if you look at the patient, the article (the affected part) is white and moist and has a subtle root.
si le cope au spatumile large, et soient en ta presence li cautere au feu.	 If the head (of a bone) is fractured widely, have the fire cautery ready in your presence.
Car au taillier vient maintes fois trop grans decorremens de sanc, et se li sans te vaint, si te haste donques dou cauterizer;	 For in the thigh there are often excessive bleeding, and if it escapes without you, hasten therefore to cauterize.
et se tu vois le malaide espoanteit et paourous de l’incision dou fer, si prent I fil de plonc bien fait, et en lie l’artelul si com nos avons dit, et le laisse II jors;	 and if you see the patient frightened and afraid of iron incision, take a well-made thread and tie the artery as we have said, and leave it for two days.
et puis le restraint, et ne cesser d’estraindre lou fil de plonc tant qu’il cope l’artelul, et chiece par lui sens travail;	 then release, and do not stop tightening the thread of the ligature until the artery throbs with pain.
et se les racines sont grosses, si a paour au coper meismement por le ventre, mais tu em pues bien coper la moitiet, puis le cauterize qu’il ne reviegne;	 and if the roots are thick, be afraid to break it with the belly, but you can break half of it, then cauterize so that it does not come back.
puis cure la plaie, et garde que tu ne coper le thelul qui est de fuxe color et de povre sens et de lait regart.	 Then treat the wound, and make sure not to cover the yellowish, weak-smelling, and milky-looking substance.
Car c’est uns apostemes enchancrez, et je venrai a la cure de chancre ci aprés.	For it is an abscess enlarged, and I will come to treat the scrofula hereafter.
quant li boude ist fuer	When the belly is filled [with something]
Se li apparance de la boude vient par cautere de plaie ou de fendure de syfac, et est sus le ventre et en ist aucuns des bouez, si com il avient en autres routures, ou de sanc qui cort de voines ou d’arteres selonc ceu qui est devant, ou de ventositeit;	 If the pus comes from the cautery of a wound or incision in the belly and is on some of the boils, as it happens in other routes, or blood that leaks from veins or arteries as described above, or wind-inflammation;
et se c’est par la routure dou syfac et par l’issue dou bouel, si est li color de l’aposteme semblans a la color dou cors, et est legiere chose sens dolor, et apert de diverse issue.	 And if it is due to the rupture of the siphon and the exit of the bowel, the color of the abscess resembles the color of the body, and it is a light thing without pain, and open with various outlets.
Et se c’est por l’issue de l’intestine, adonques est il plus divers, et quant on le presse a ses dois si se repont, et puis revient, et par aventure si est sarrez, et agrandist mout a l’entree dou bain et por fort travail.	And if it is due to the rupture of the intestine, then it is more diverse; and when you press it with your hands, it returns, and then it comes back, and by chance if it is sutured, it greatly enlarges at the opening of the wound and due to great labor.
Et se c’est por moistor, c’est legiere chose, et apert bien quant tu le presses a ta main, ne ne constraint mie;	 If it is due to moisture, it is a light thing and easily opened when you press it with your hand, do not constrain it.
et se c’est por sanc, si apert par ces signes li apostemes gros et dur, et est fichiez selonc une quantiteit;	 And if it is due to blood, the abscesses are large and hard, and filled according to a certain quantity.
et se c’est por ventositeit, si est souef au tochier, et li ovraiges si est que tu regarde se li apparance est por le sanc de l’artere, ou de la voine, ou ventositeit.	 And if it is due to ventosity (gas), it yields to the touch, and the work is that you examine whether its appearance is due to blood from an artery or vein, or gas.
Si covient que tu laisses la cure.	 It is necessary that you let the healing be.
Car il en a doutance et paor, si com je t’ai dit ou chapistre des apostemes, por l’artere et por la voine.	 For there is doubt and fear, as I have told you in the chapter on abscesses, regarding the artery and the vein.
Et se li apparance est por l’intestine ou lou boueil, si covient que tu comandes au malaide qu’il teigne son alaine, et soit estendus tout drois, puis seigne d’enche tout entor la boude;	 And if the appearance is due to the intestines or the belly, you should command the patient to lean his backside, and be fully extended straight, then hold around the abdomen.
puis le comande a gesir sovin entre tes mains, puis va entor le leu que tu as signiet a tout le spatumile, puis estent la moitiet de l’aposteme au desus a tout le grant uncine;	 then command him to push gently between your hands, then go around the area that you have held with a small spoon, then spread half of the abscess above on a large unguent.
puis le lie entor d’un fil fort, ou d’une corde de fort soie fermement, et soit li nous dou liien assolz;	 then tie it around with a strong thread or a cord made of strong silk firmly, and let the nose be bound with linen.
puis oevre la moitiet de l’aposteme estendut sus le liien, et i boute ton doit indice, et quier l’intestine;	 then open half of the extended abscess on the cord, and insert your finger, and search for the intestines.
se tu le trueves pris dou liien, si le deslie, et boute l’intestine au defuer dou ventre;	 if you find it seized by the cord, then undo it, and push the intestine out of the abdomen.
et se tu trueves le boueil, si le prent a l’oncine, et en cope la superfluiteit;	 And if you find the boil, take it at its base, and cut off the superfluous part of it;
et se li artere te fait contraire, ou li voine, si vai belement entor, puis revien a ton ovraige et pren II aguilles, et i boute II fors filz, et boute les II aguilles entor ceu que tu as fait en crois que tu feis percier;	 And if the artery makes it contract or the vein, go around it gently, then return to your work and take two needles and insert two sharp wires through them, and place the two needles around what you have made in a cross shape so that you can pierce it;
puis estrain l’aposteme en IIII leus sus les aguilles, et se tu vues, oste les aguilles, et laisse lou leu tant qu’il porrisse, et chiece li char morte par soi;	 then hold the abscess for three inches above the needles, and if you see it, remove the needles, and leave the place until it is ready, and let the dead flesh fall off by itself;
ou tu la cope quant elle iert subtiliie et porrie, puis le cure de ceu qu’il covient, et cheve l’aposteme si com nos avons dit;	 or you cut it when it is tender and can be pierced, then treat what is necessary, and let the abscess heal as we have said.
et estrai le sanc ou la moistor que tu trueves, puis cure le leu de ceu qu’il couvient, et soude le leu.	 Draw out the blood or moisture that you find, then heal the joint as necessary, and bind the joint.
dou chancre	the boil
Nos avons dit en la division les semblances de chancre, et coment on i doit ovrer par medicines, et coment on doit eschuer la cure de fer;	 We have said in the previous section the resemblance of scrofula, and how it should be treated with medicine, and how to remove the iron cure.
et disons le chancre enjanreit en la marris, et grant cautele a en la cure, et dirent li ancien que quant chancres est en leu ou on le puet raier si com chancre qui est em mameles, et en la cuixe, et en semblans leus, et le doit tout oster quant il est en l’encomencement;	 And we say the boil arises in the groin area, and great caution should be taken in its treatment, and the ancients said that when boils are present where they can be shaved like a common boil, and in the thigh, and similar places, it must all be removed when it is at the beginning.
et quant il est grans et anciens, si ne covient mie que tu l’aproches, car je n’en poi onques nul saner;	 and when they are large and old, do not approach them, for I never know anyone who can heal them.
ne nulz n’en sana onques devant moi.	 no one ever heals them before me.
Et li ovraiges, quant il est en leu ou on le puet oster, si com nos avons dit, est que tu purge aucune fois le malaide de cole noire;	 And the works, when they are in places where they can be removed, as we have said, is that you purge the patient of black bile once.
puis le fai sainier s’il ait manifeste repletion, puis afaite le malaide I boin leu por faire l’ovraige;	 Then make him purge if there is obvious fullness, then prepare the patient in good health for the procedure.
puis giete tes oncines ou chancre, et le cheve de toutes pars, et l’oste de toutes pars sens rien laissier;	 Then throw your onions or boilsores, and all the hairs from every part, and the bone from every part should feel nothing left;
et laisse corre le sanc tout fuer, et espreint bien le leu a ta main ou a aucune chose, et se li decorremens de sanc te fait contraire de l’incision de l’artere ou de la voine, si le cauterize tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	 And let the blood flow freely, and press well the place with your hand or any object, and if the bleeding makes you oppose the incision of an artery or a vein, then cauterize it until the wound is coagulated.
puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then heal it from another healing until it is healed.
de ydropisie	dropisy
Nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’idropisie, et en queil maniere li assemblee de l’aigue est faite, et les signes de chescune semblance, et la cure qui est faite par medicines, et cele qui est curee par fer:	 We have said in the division the resemblances of edema, and in what way the assembly of water is made, and the signs of each resemblance, and the medicine that is used for it, and the one that is healed by iron.
si est eclites soulement;	 It is split (or broken) only.
et ne doit on touchier de fer en ces II semblances:	 and one must not use iron in these two cases:
c’est a savoir, tympanites et yposarche, car c’est mortelz chose;	 that is to say, tympanites and yposarche (or epaschar), for it is deadly.
donques quant tu medicines ceste semblance de ydropisie qui est apelee «eclites» de medicines, et li cure ne profite, si regarde se li malaides est foibles, ou s’il ait autre maladie que ydropisie, si com toust et solution de ventre et semblans choses;	 therefore, when treating this case of edema known as "eclites" in medicine, and the cure does not help, look to see if the patient is weak or if he has another disease besides edema, such as abdominal distension and similar things.
si n’i touchier de fer, car il i a doutance;	 do not use iron because there is doubt.
et se tu vois le malaide de fort vertut, et il n’a autre maladie que ydropisie soulement, et il n’est mie trop jones ne trop vielz, si dois ensi ovrer:	 and if you see the patient with great strength, and he has no other disease besides edema alone, and is not too thin nor too old, then do as follows:
lieve le malaide droit sus tes mains, et li ministres presse le ventre em boutant l’aigue a la plus basse partie dou pis, puis pren le spatumile espinous selonc ceste forme:	 Lift the patient upright on your hands, and the ministers press the stomach pressing the water to the lowest part of the bladder, then take the pointed spatula according to this form:
Et soit trenchans de II pars.	 And let it be cut through from the second part.
a pointe, et toutevoie ne soit mie si entrans qu’il puist venir jusc’a l’intestine quant on le fiche ens, et ne le puist blecier;	 and it should not be so pointed that it can reach the intestines when inserted, nor should it pierce.
puis regarde se li ydropisie est enjanree devers les intestines:	 then look to see if the urine is diverted towards the intestines:
si covient que tu fendes ensus de la boude III dois droit desoz sus lou poignil;	 it is necessary that you make an incision below the bladder, 3 fingers' breadth right below the navel.
et se li ydropisie est por la maladie dou foie, si soit ta fendure au senestre de la boude III dois;	 and if the urine is due to liver disease, then make the incision on the left side of the bladder 3 fingers' breadth.
et se c’est por la miuce, si soit a destre, et ne covient mie que li malaides gise sus la fendure que les superfluitez ne corrent a celui foible leu;	 and if it is due to obstruction, it should be on the right side, and the patient should not lie on the incision so that excess fluid does not run to the weak place.
puis perce tout le cuir a l’estrument, et le boute, et lieve ta main a tout le spatumile entre le cuir et le syfac ausi com en escorchant a la quantiteit d’une ungle ou enqui entor;	 Then pierce the entire skin with an instrument, push it, and pull your hand with the spatula between the skin and the bone to the thickness of a nail or thereabouts.
puis perce lou syfac tant que li spatumile viegne au leu vuit, et c’est li leus de l’aigue, puis le trai fuer, et i boute cest estrument de coi ci est li forme:	 Then pierce the bone as far as the spatula reaches, which is the lower jawbone, then pull it out and insert this instrument in its place:
Et est semblans a une caine d’argent subtil, et est d’arain ou d’archaut legier, et a en la partie desoz I petit pertus;	 And it resembles a silver chain, thin, and is of fine wire or light arsenic, and there is one at the part below the little piercing.
et ou costeit d’une part, III pertus;	 and on one side, three piercings.
et II d’autre part, et I d’autre;	 and two on the other side, and one on the other.
et est li chiés tailliez si com une penne, et c’est li forme de l’incision dont li escrivains taille la penne:	 and the head is cut like a quill, and it has the shape of the incision that scribes make on a quill.
au chief desus est li alemele, si que quant li estrumens vient a l’aigue, si dessent maintenant sus l’estrument;	 Above the head is the anale, so when the instrument comes to the anus, hold it now above the instrument.
vuide la donques la moitiet ou la tierce part, car se tu en vuides plus qu’il ne covient en celle houre, par aventure si muert li malaides por la resolution de son esperit de l’arme, ou il chiet paumez, ou il aproche a la mort;	 Then empty the anus, that is, either half or one third, for if you see more than what is appropriate at that time, by chance, the patient may die due to the resolution of his spirit from the weapon, or he may fall flat, or approach death.
mais en vuide selonc la quantiteit de sa vertut, et selonc ceu que les dispositions de la vertut dou malaide signifient, et ses poulz;	 However, according to its potency and depending on the patient's condition and pulse.
puis trai l’estrument et retien l’aigue, et elle est retenue maintenant por le keur qui estoupe le pertus qui est sus le syfac, de coi j’ai parleit, que tu perces selonc ceste maniere;	 Then draw the instrument and hold the juice, it is retained now due to the cauterization that stops the perforation that is on the siphac, as I have spoken about, that you pierce in this way.
puis rencomence l’estrument l’autre jor, se tu vois le malaide soffrant ceu, et trai de l’aigue une petite quantiteit;	 Then use the instrument again on another day if you see the patient suffering, and draw a small amount of juice.
fai ce aucun jor, et te garde de foloier tant qu’il ni demore mais c’un poc d’aigue.	 Do this every day, but do not let it become excessive until it neither grows nor there is a small amount of juice.
Et se tu doutes sus le malaide, et tu i lais mout d’aigue, si le cure de la sepulture ou sablon chaut, et par mout sueir ou bain et au soleil, et se teigne de boivre;	 And if you have doubts about the patient and let too much juice accumulate, heal it with burial or hot sand, and by sweating, bathing, and sunlight, and apply wine.
et le cure de medicines desiccatives tant qu’il soit sanez, et cauterize sus l’estomac et sus lou foie et sus l’esplen aprés l’estraction de l’aigue, si com j’ai dit devant.	 And the medicine for drying should be administered until he is clean, and cauterize on the stomach, the liver and the spleen after extraction of the water as I have said before.
de l’estopement de la verge	For stopping the penis
Aucune fois naissent enfant qui n’ont point de pertus en la verge, ou li pertus est petis, ou il n’est mie en son leu.	 Sometimes children are born who do not have foreskin at all, or the foreskin is small, or it is not in its place.
Si le covient tantost qu’il n’aist percier a tout I spatumile molt subtil selonc ceste forme:	 If it is necessary to immediately pierce through every spittle very thinly according to this form:
puis met ou pertus I clo subtil de plonc, et le lie et le tien ensi III jors ou IIII et quant il vuet faire urine, si soit ostez li clos, et faice urine, et puis li remet;	 Then put soft cloth of linen and tie it for three or four days until he wants to urinate, then remove the cloth, let him urinate, and then replace it.
et par aventure nen i couvient point, car li urine qui vient fuer ne lou laisse close.	 And in case there is no need for this, because the urine that comes forth does not leave it closed.
Cil de cui li pertus est petis, si est medicinez dou clo de plonc, si com nos avons dit, si s’eslargera.	 The patient with a small purulent wound is to be treated with a cloth of plunged linen, as we have said, and it will swell up.
Cil qui n’ont mie le pertus en lor leu sont bleciet, car aucun naissent qui ont le pertus au chief de la verge, por coi il ne puient pissier avant s’il ne lievent lor verge en haut;	 Those who do not have the cloth in their place are bleeding, because no one is born who has the cloth on the head of the penis, which means they cannot urinate before tying their penis up.
et ne pueent enjanrer por ceu que li matiere ne puet venir jusc’a la marris, et c’est une male maladie.	 And they cannot heal because the matter cannot reach the sore, and it is a bad disease.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos, puies estent le chief de la verge et le cope ausi com la taille d’une penne, si ke li pertus chiece em mileu, si com il covient;	 The manner of work is that the patient lies supine on their back, with the head of the penis and its tip as flat as a feather's shaft, so that the testicles are in the middle, as it should be.
et te garde de decorrement de sanc qui i vient maintes fois, et s’il avient, si l’estainche de ceu qui estainche sanc, et cure la plaie tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And take care to prevent bleeding that often occurs, and if it happens, compress the area where blood is coming out, and heal the wound until it is healed.
des pustules de la verge	boils on the penis
Maintes fois vienent cist albathe en la verge, et est une apparance de char laide;	 Often this almond appears in the penis, and it is an ugly sign of sickness.
et en i a malignes et non malignes;	 And there are both harmful and harmless ones.
si covient que tu les preignes a I oncine subtil, et les cope et munde toutes, puis met sus coton moilliet en oignement egiptien;	 It is necessary for you to take them [the things] in one continuous motion, strike and clean them all, then put soft cotton in an Egyptian ointment on top.
puis le cure d’oignement diafinicon tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then heal it with diaphinicon ointment until it is healed.
Et se li albathe est maligne, de pute color et depuant, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere.	 If the ulcer is malignant, purple in color and weeping, you must apply a fire cautery.
Quant tu l’as copeit, et se li albathe est en som la verge, et en ait partie dedens la peil et partie defuer, si covient que tu oste l’albathe qui est dedens premier;	 When you have struck it [the thing], and the bladder is in the middle of the wound and has both parts inside and outside the skin, it is necessary to remove the bladder that is inside first.
et quant il est soudez, si le cure defuer.	 And when it [the thing] is sealed, heal it from the outside.
Car quant tu le cures ensamble, si n’est mie asseurez li chiez de la verge qu’il ne soit perciez, et vient noiror et corruption en son la verge et ou coion;	 For when you heal it together, there is not assured that the bladder of the wound will not be pierced, and there comes blackness and corruption in its wound and wherever.
si covient chever tout ceu qui est noir et corrumput, puis lie sus l’emplaustre de miel et de farine qui soit fait d’escorce de poumes grenates et de veces, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	 It is necessary to burn everything that is black and corrupted, then lay it on a plaster of honey and flour made from the peel of pomegranate rinds and leaves, then treat it with other treatments until it becomes healthy again.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si amenistre le cautere lunaire selonc ceste forme:	 And if bleeding comes out, bring the lunar cautery according to this form:
Li cauteres si aide as II dispositions ensamble:	 The cautery helps in the following combinations:
c’est asavoir, au decorrement de sanc, et a la corruption;	 This means "It is concerning blood circulation, decay.
et se li chiés de la verge est corrumpus et retrais, si covient que tu boutes ou conduit de la verge une cainne de plonc, et pisse li malaides parmi;	 And if the head of the penis is decayed and retracted, then you must drink or lead a cane from the penis, and make the patient urinate.
et quant li pelz iert aerse au chief de la verge qui avient a ces qui n’ont mie esteit circoncis, ou il avient por plaie ou por aposteme, si covient donques que tu l’escorches a I estrument cheveit, tant que li liiens soit desliiez, et soit delivrez li chiez de la verge de toutes pars;	 And when the skin is torn at the tip of the penis, which happens to those who have not been circumcised, or it happens due to a wound or an abscess, then you must shave it with the instrument of hair removal, until the ligaments are separated, and release the testicles from the penis on all sides.
et se c’est grief chose de deviser ceu, si covient que tu l’escorches a I spatumile aucun poc dou chief de la verge et de la peil;	 And if it is painful to discuss this matter, then you must shave it with the spatula a little bit from the tip of the penis and the skin.
puis dessevre belement entre II, et i met I subtil drapeil de lin moilliet an aigue froide, qu’il n’aerse derechief.	 Then carefully press them together, and place a thin linen cloth dampened with cold water between them, so that it does not dry up immediately.
de la circoncision	Of circumcision
Circoncision n’est mie desliemens de continuation si com les autres plaies;	 Circumcision is not the same as continuous wounds like other injuries;
toutevoie quant nos faison ceste oevre de nostre volenteit, et proprement as enfans, si est mestier que nos faisiens la millor oevre, et la plus legiere a salut.	 However, when we perform this work of our own accord and intentionally on infants, it is necessary to make the best and easiest work for healing.
Je dis que li ancien ne dirent mie la circoncision de lor enfans, car il n’en usent mie en lor loi, et n’en avons mais que ceu que nos avons aquis par experiment.	I say that the ancients did not mention circumcision of their children, for they did not use it in their law, and we have only what we have acquired by experience.
Car j’ai veut la plus grant partie des maistres et des sainors qui faisoient circumcision entor I dal, et as forces, et a tout une novacule;	 For I have wanted to gather the greater part of masters and healers who were performing circumcision at that time, and their methods, and a newborn.
si fuioit li keurs car il i a II toiles, et par aventure si cope on celi desus et demore celle desoz.	 Since there are two layers, one of them could be cut, and by chance the other could remain below.
Or la recovient coper, et est li dolor double, et a la mundification qui est dou dal n’est mie asseuree li pointe dou membre;	 Or the recovery is covered, and there is twice the pain, and in the healing of which from below the member is not assured.
et a la mundification de l’ungle par aventure eschaipe li fer, et corront l’uevre, et maintes fois naissent ensi qu’il n’ont mestier de mundification et je l’ai veut.	 And in the shaping of the nail by chance, the iron may slip and spoil the work, and it often happens that it doesn't need mending and I have seen this.
De la mondification qui est faite as forces a tout le liien de fil ai je troveit la bonteit de l’experiment, car les forces taillent justement ausi bien desus com desoz.	From the amputation which is done to all the chains of thread I have found the goodness of experiment, for the forces cut just as well above as below.
Car quant tu presses ta main, si tailles igalment en I tout soul tens;	 For when you press your hand, equalize the nails evenly at all times;
mais que li filz soit bien estrois entor lou cuir;	 but ensure that the nails are well narrowed around the skin;
et soit li maniere dou premier ovraige si est que tu faices penser l’enfant, s’il entent, que tu ne li fais fuer que liier le fil entor la verge tant soulement, et pues le fai esjoir en toutes les manieres que tu pues;	 and the method of the first work is that you make the child understand, if he can, not to make him tie the thread around the stick except only, and then let him enjoy it in all ways you can.
puis le fai ester entre tes mains tout droit, et repont les forces entre tes mains ou desoz tes piez que li enfes ne les voie, ne aucun des estrumens;	 then make him put it between your hands straight, and force the fingers between your hands or under your feet so that the child does not see, nor any instrument.
puis boute ta main a la verge et souffle ou keur, et la trai en haut tant que li chiés de la verge soit ens;	 Then place your hand on the shoulder and blow or cough, and pull it upwards until the head of the shoulder is in.
puis la mundifie bien de l’ordure qui i est assemblee, puis lie le leu signiet d’un fil double, puis la lie desoz I poc a I autre liien;	 Then clean it well of the filth that has gathered there, then tie the dislocated joint with a double thread, then tie it below the poke to another ligament.
et la tien as II dois par la seconde lieeure au pouchet et au doit indice, et cope entre les II liiens, puis lieve le keur desus hastanment et trai le chief de la verge;	 and hold it with the second ligature at the pouch and index finger, and press between the two ligaments, then remove the cough quickly and pull the head of the shoulder.
puis laisse corre le sanc poc et poc, car c’est li muedres;	 then let the blood flow freely, for that is the remedy.
et met poudre sus et sus la poudre I drapeil glueit d’un moieuf d’uef cuit destempreit d’aigue rose, confit avec oile roset boin et fres, et lou laisse sus jusc’a l’autre jor, et le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 and put powder on it and above the powder place a layer of egg white cooked with a little rose water, mixed with fresh rose oil; let it stay there until the next day, and treat it with another treatment until it is healed.
Li forme des forces a la mundification si est ceste:	 The form of strengths for purification is as follows:
li dui chiés soient tenves et soient trenchans, et soient li chiés ausi grant com li mainche igalment:	 The two shoulders should be slender and sharp, and the same size as the wrist equally:
li error de la mundification si est quant li keurs dedens fuit a l’incision;	 the error in purification is when the intestines within are incised;
donques il covient que tu l’estendes a ton ungle, ainsois que li leus faice aposteme;	 then you must stretch it with your nail, so that the flesh makes an abscess;
et le cope igalment, et se tu ne lou pues tenir a ton ungle, si le tien as tenailles, et puis le cope.	 and cover it equally, and if you cannot hold it with your nail, then take tweezers, and press it.
Et s’il trespassent III jors, et ceu qui est desoz la verge est enflez, si le laisse tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez, et l’escorche legierement;	 And if it lasts more than three days, and what is below the penis swells, let it be until the abscesses calm down, and lightly scrape off the scab.
si le cope si com tu pues mues, et te garde de la partie de la verge, ce ne li nuira niant.	 if you press it as much as you can move, and take care of the penis area, it will not harm anything.
Cure donques le leu de choses soudans plaie de poudre, que nos avons dit ou traitier des poudres, et s’on cope dou keur outre mesure, et il va au desus, si ne nuira point;	 Cure therefore the dislocated joint with powder for closed injuries as we have said in treating powders, and if one applies it excessively, it will go above but will not help.
cure le donques, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 keep the dislocation, as we have said, until it heals.
dou retenement de l’urine	the retention of urine
Li retenue de l’urine si est d’opilation de piere, ou de sanc congeleit, ou de bowe, ou de char nee, ou de semblans choses, que nos avons dit en la division;	 Retention of urine is caused by a stone, or frozen blood, or pus, or rotten flesh, or similar things as we have said in the section.
et se li urine n’est desliie , et tu vois estre la retenue por la piere qui est jai ou col de la vessie, si covient que li malaides soit corbés sus ses genoulz;	 and if the urine is not released, and you see it is retained due to a stone in or neck of the bladder, then the patient must be bent over his knees.
et li soient mis li piez sor le dos, et estende son ventre de la partie desus lou dos, et restraigne li malaides s’alainne tant com il puet;	 and place the feet on the back, extend his abdomen from above the loins, and hold the patient flat as he can.
et adonques est constrains li colz de la vessie a l’expression de la piere au desus, por coi li urine est desliie e;	 And then the bladder's neck is compressed towards the stone above, which causes the urine to be expelled;
et s’elle ne vient, si com nos avons dit, et li malaides sent grant dolor, si covient que tu i aministres extraction a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «siringue», de coi ci est li forme:	 If it does not come as we have said, and the patient feels great pain, then you must administer an extraction with all the instruments called "syringe," of which this is its shape:
et soit d’argent subtilz legiere chevee, si com li penne d’un oiseil;	 And it shall be of subtle silver, light and thin like the feather of a bird;
et soit li caine d’une palme de lonc et demie, et soit subtilz au chief.	 And the cable (or thread) shall be a palm and a half long, and fine at the end.
Et li maniere de l’issue de l’urine si est que tu pren I fil double, et lie au chief I poc de laine ou de couton, et boute le chief dou fil dedens la siringue;	 And the way of urine discharge is that you take a double thread, tie its end to a wool or cotton wad, and push the thread end into the syringe.
et cope la superfluiteit de la lainne et le boute jusc’au chief de la siringue, puis oint la siringue d’oile ou de burre et d’aubin d’uef, et fai seoir le malaide sus I siege, et li arose la vessie et la verge d’oile moiste et d’oile d’olive et d’aigue tede;	 Wrap the superfluous wool and push it to the tip of the syringe, then oil or butter and egg yolk the syringe, and make the patient sit on a chair, and rub the bladder and penis with oil moistened with oil and water.
puis met legierement la siringue en la verge, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la verge, puis double la verge desus devers la boude;	 Then gently insert the syringe into the rod until it reaches the root of the rod, then double the rod above towards the butt.
puis boute la siringue avant jusc’a la vessie, et la sente li malaides venir jusc’a la chose vuide, et ceu n’est mie fait selonc cest ordre fuer que por ceu que li conduis ou elle vait est tors;	 Then push the syringe forward until it reaches the bladder, and make the patient feel it coming to the empty place, and this is not done according to this order except for when the guide of where it goes is twisted.
puis estent le fil a tout la laine poc et poc, et li urine en suit la laine, puis l’estrai fuer, et fai corre l’urine;	 Then wind the thread around all the wool strands little by little, and let the urine follow the thread, then pull it out, and correct the urine.
et rencomence la siringue tant que li vessie soit vuidie, et soit aligiez li malaides.	 And repeat the syringe until the bladder is empty and the patient is relieved.
des maladies de la vessie	Diseases of the bladder
Quant escorcheures ou sanc vient en la vessie, ou porriture i est assemblee, et tu i vues distiller aigues et medicines, si fai a tout l’estrument qui est apellé «clepsedre», et c’est li forme:	When scratches or blood comes into the bladder, or pus is collected there, and you see it distill liquids and medicines, do everything using the instrument called "clepsydra", and its shape is:
Elle est close, et si a III pertus:	 It is closed, and if it persists for three days.
II d’une part, et I d’autre, si com tu vois;	 One on one side, and the other on the other side, as you see;
et li leus chevez par coi li medicine cort soit telz qu’il estoupe bien la verge sens adition, si c’on em puisse traire la moistor, et bouter quant mestier est;	 and the joints placed on both sides in such a way that the medicine stick closely to the shaft without addition, so that moisture can be drawn out, and pushed when necessary;
et quant tu vues giter tes medicines en la vessie, met le chief dou keusteur en la moistor, et trai au traiant qui est ens;	 and when you see the medicine thrown into the bladder, place the head of the couester in the moisture, and draw out the trail that is inside;
si trairas la moistor au kesteur, et puis reboute fort le traiant ens;	 if you draw out the moisture from the couester, then push the trail forcefully within;
si entrera li moistors ens, et venra a la vessie maintenant, si que li malaides la sentira;	 the moisture will enter it (the bladder), and will come to the bladder now, so that the patient feels it;
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil dont on clisterize la vessie:	 and this is the shape of the subtle suppository with which you administer a suppository to the bladder.
si est ci:	 If it is here (the case):
Et est d’argent ou d’archaut, et est li chiés plus haut;	 And it is of silver or iron, and the head is higher.
et desoz a I sein ou li liiens chiet;	 and underneath the chest or the liver lies.
puis pren une vessie de mouton et i met la moistor dont tu vues clisterizer la vessie, puis la lie entre les II seins forment d’un boin fil double, et chaufe I poc celle moistor sus le feu;	 Then take a sheep's bladder and fill it with the moisture you use to soften the bladder, then tie it between two breasts with a strong thread, and heat the bladder on fire.
puis boute le chief dou clistere en la verge, puis estrain ta main sus la vessie a tout la moistor avenanment, tant que li malaides sente que celle moistor est jai venue a la vessie;	 then insert the head of the bladder into the anus, then press your hand on the bladder with all the moisture coming out, until the patient feels that the moisture has reached the bladder.
et se tu n’as la vessie, si pren une piece de parchemin, et en fai I cercle, et le perce rondement entor;	 and if you do not have a bladder, take a piece of parchment, make it into a circle, and poke a hole in the center.
puis boute I fil fort en ces pertus, puis assemble le cercle si com on assemble I dal, et met dedens ceu que tu vues d’oile et de moistor et d’aigue, et le lie en l’estrument;	 Then insert a strong wire into these holes, then gather the circle as one gathers the needle, and put inside it what you see of oil and moisture and water, and tie it in the instrument.
et fai si com tu as fait de la vessie, de presser a ta main tant que li moistor veigne a la vessie.	 and do as you have done with the bladder, pressing on it with your hand until the moisture comes out of the bladder.
de la piere	of the stone (arrowhead or projectile)
Nos avons jai dit en la division les manieres de piere, et l’estraction ensamble medicines;	 We have said in the division the ways of stone, and extraction together with medicines;
et ai dit la difference entre la piere enjanree as rains, et toz les signes, et en queil piere on doit ovrer de taille;	 and I have said the difference between a stone caused by rain, and all the signs, and in which stone one must work by cutting.
et en la vessie, et en la verge;	 and in the bladder, and in the vein.
et je le vos dirai apertement et briément.	 And I will tell you openly and briefly.
Je dis que li piere qui est enjanree en la vessie si avient plus sovent as enfans, et c’est signe que li aigue saut de la vessie semblans a aigue en sa subtiliteit;	 I say that the stone which is embedded in the bladder occurs more often in children, and this is a sign that the urine jump from the bladder resembles urine in its subtlety.
et i apert harene, et graite li malaides sa verge, et li pent maintes fois, et puis enroidist;	 and it opens a hernia, and greatly injures the patient's penis, and he suffers many times, and then binds it up.
et a mout de ces saut li fondemens;	 and of these jumps the foundations are destroyed;
et est legiere li sanation des enfans jusqu’il ont IIII ans, et est mout grief en viellars, et est as jones moiene, a ces qui sont entre jonesce et viellece;	 and the healing of children is easy until they are four years old, but it is very serious in elderly people, and it is somewhat uncertain for those who are between youth and old age.
et est li cure plus legiere de ces qui ont la piere grans, que de ces qui l’ont petite.	 and the treatment of large stones is easier than that of small ones.
Et quant nos venons a la cure, si couvient premier mundifier le malaide per clistere, por traire tout le fiens qui est as intestines.	 And when we come to the treatment, it is first necessary to cleanse the patient with an enema, to draw out all the filth that is in the intestines.
Car il encombre aucune fois a querir la piere.	 For it often obstructs the search for stones.
Puis prenez le malaide par les piez, et lou deboutez et movez au desoz, si que li piere dessende au parfont de la vessie, et saille aucune fois dou leu haut;	 Then take the patient by the feet, and push down and move under, so that the stone descends to the bottom of the bladder, and does not move upwards.
puis le fai seoir entre tes mains appareilliet, et ses mains soient desoz ses cuisses, si que li vessie soit toute declinans aval;	 Then make him sit between your hands supported, and his hands should be beneath his thighs, so that the bladder is completely declining downwards.
puis la quier et la touche dedens;	 then touch it and probe inside.
se tu sens la piere en l’espaice, si te haste maintenant de taillier sus la piere.	 if you feel the stone in the cavity, hasten now to cut above the stone.
Et s’elle ne chiet au touchier dou tout, si moille ton doi indice d’oile de la main senestre, se li malaides est enfes, ou ton doi moien, se li malaides est jovencelz acomplis;	 And if it does not fall out with the touch, moisten your right index finger with oil if the patient is an adult, or moist your thumb, if the patient is a young adult.
et le boute en son fondement, et quier la piere, et quant tu la sens a ton doi, si l’amoine au col de la vessie;	 and push it into its foundation, probe for the stone, and when you feel it with your finger, pull it at the bladder neck.
puis presse sus a ton doi, et la boute au defuer lai ou tu vues taillier.	 then press with your finger and push it to where you intend to cut.
Et comande au ministre qu’il presse la vessie a sa main, et li comande qu’il estende a sa main destre les coions en haut, et a sa main senestre oste le cuir qui est desoz les coions en la partie ou on fait la taille;	 And instruct the minister to press the bladder with his hand, and also command him to stretch out his right hand towards the top of the testicles, and his left hand to open the skin that is beneath the testicles in the area where incision is made.
puis i boute le spatumile copant, de coi ce est li forme:	 Then insert the spatula-like tool, which has this shape:
Et fent entre ceu qui est entre les coions et le fondement, ne mie em mileu mais au costeit de la naige senestre;	 And make an incision between what is between the testicles and the bottom, not in the middle but along the left side of the scrotum.
et soit drois sus la piere, et tes dois soit adés ou fondement, et soit li taille dou traver si qu’ele soit large par defuer, et dedens estroite, selonc la quantiteit de la piere, ne mie trop grans;	 And the right side should be on top of the stone, and your fingers should be close to or against the bottom, and make the cut across, so it is wide at the outside and narrow inside, according to the size of the stone, not too large.
par aventure la presse si li dois qui est ou fondement, qu’elle saut fuer sens travail;	 By chance, the press must be applied to the base, as its foundation, so it may jump out of place.
et saiches qu’il i a teil piere ou il a angles, et marges:	 and know that there is always stone or angles and edges:
si est griés a issir;	 if it is to be extracted;
et si a teil qui est souez, semblans a une glant, et reonde, dont li issue est legiere.	 and if it is swollen like a plum, round, and the point of exit is light.
A celi donques ou il a angles et marge, fai la taille plus grant;	 To that one therefore where there are angles and edges, make the incision larger;
et s’elle ne saut, si covient que tu estraignes sus as tenailles qui sont ausi com une lime au chief, por mues estraindre la piere si qu’elle n’eschaipe;	 and if it does not jump out, you must pull up with the pliers that are like a file at the tip, to push the stone so that it does not escape;
ou tu boute desoz li I estrument subtil corbé au chief;	 or you drive under the instrument curved at the tip.
et se tu ne la pues engignier ensi, si eslarge I poc lou pertus, et se li sans decort, si l’estrainche de vitriole;	 and if you cannot deceive it in this way, you should make a small opening with a lancet, and if the edges are not cut, you should draw it out with a vitriol-coated probe.
et s’il i a plus d’une piere, si boute premier la plus grant au col de la vessie, puis cope sus, puis le trai fuer, et les petites aprés s’il en i a plusors.	 And if there are more than one arrow, push the largest one first into the neck of the bladder, then strike it, pull it out, and afterwards the smaller ones, if there are any more.
Et s’elle est mout grans, si la covient soier, et faire plus grant plaie.	 If it is very large, then it must be cut open more widely.
Car II choses avienent au malaide:	 For two things may happen to the patient:
ou il muert, ou li urine vient adés par lai que li leus ne puet souder;	 or he dies, or urine comes out immediately through the place where the bladder cannot be sealed.
mais toutevoie t’efforce dou traire, ou dou debrisier as tenailles, tant que tu la traies par pieces;	 but you must make every effort to draw it out or dissect with pliers until you pull it out in pieces;
et quant tu as acomplit ton oevre, si emple la plaie d’encens et d’aloe et de sanc de dragon, et l’estraint, et met par sus I drapeil moilliet en oile et en vin, ou en oile et en aigue rose et aigue froide, por apaisier l’aposteme chaut;	 and when you have completed your work, smear the wound with incense, aloe, and dragon's blood, press it together, and cover it with a damp cloth in oil and wine, or in oil and rosewater and cold water, to cool down the abscess.
puis resovine le malaide sus son col, et ne desliier lou lien jusc’au tier jor.	 Then hold the patient on his neck, and do not undo the bandage for three days.
Et quant tu le desliies, si arose mout bien lou leu d’oile et d’aigue, puis le cure d’oignement dyafinicon et d’oignement basilicon, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when you loosen the rope, wash the wound well with oil and water, then treat it with ointment of diaphinecon and basilicon until it heals.
Et se apostemes chaus vient en la plaie et corrosions, et congelemens de sanc en la vessie, et soit par ceu retenue li urine, qui est conue en teil maniere que sans saut avec l’urine:	 If abscesses grow in the wound and there is corruption of blood in the bladder and the urine is retained as if without leaping with the urine:
boutes donques ton doi en la plaie, et estrai celui sanc, car s’il i remaint, si corront la vessie, et la porrit;	 Therefore, stick your finger into the wound, and draw out that blood, for if it remains, it will cause the bladder to run and urinate.
puis leve la plaie d’aigue et d’aisil et de seil, et li aide en toutes les manieres que tu seis, tant qu’il soit sanez;	 Lift the wound from pus and inflammation and purulent matter, and help it in all ways you know, as long as it is healed.
et covient que toutes les oures que tu le cures, que tu li lie les II cuisses, et assemble les medicines sus le leu.	 And it is necessary that all the herbs you use in the cure, you bind the two thighs together, and place the remedies on top of them.
Et se li piere est petite, et ele est ou conduit de la verge, et fichie ens, et li urine ne puet issir;	 And if the stone is small, and it is conducted along the penis, and inserted, and the urine cannot flow out;
si le cure de ceu que je dis ainsois, que tu lou tailles maintes fois, est on escusez de la taille per ceste cure.	 if you follow what I say next, you will cut it many times, you are excused from the cutting for this treatment.
Je ai ja ce proveit ensi.	 I have already experienced this.
Pren .i. foret de fer selonc ceste forme et soit a .iij. angles fichiees en .i. tison:	Take one iron rod of this shape and sharpened at four angles on one tip:
puis pren I fil et lou lie entor la verge desoz la piere, si qu’ele ne puist venir arrier en la vessie;	 Then take the thread and tie it around the rod under the stone, so that it cannot return into the bladder.
puis boute le foret en la verge legierement, tant qu’il viegne a la piere;	 then push the awl gently into the rod until it reaches the stone.
et torne le foret a ta main en la piere poc et poc, tant que tu puisses percier la piere d’autre part;	 and turn the awl slowly in the stone, little by little, until you can pierce the stone from another side.
si venra tantost li urine, puis presse ta main sus ceu qui est demorez de la piere qui est dedens la verge.	 soon the urine will come, then press your hand on what remains of the stone that is inside the rod.
Si est tantost brisie, et saut fuer avec l’urine, et est garis li malaides;	 It will soon be broken and shoot out with the urine, and the patient will be cured.
et se tu ne pues ce faire por aucune chose qui le deffent, si lie I fil desoz la piere et I autre desus, puis fent la verge endroit la piere entre les II liiens, puis l’estrai fuer, et deslie lou liien, et mundifie lou sanc congeleit qui est en la plaie;	 and if you cannot do this for any reason that prevents it, tie the thread around the stone both below and above, then bend the rod towards the stone between the two threads, pull it out, untie the thread, and clean the frozen blood in the wound.
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And let the [patient] heal when he is sound.
de la piere des femmes	From a woman's stone (or pelvis)
Poc avient que piere soit enjanree en femmes, et s’il avient aucune fois, si est li cure grief, et est deffendut por III choses:	 It happens that stone should be inserted in women, and if it ever occurs, the cure is painful, and it is forbidden for three reasons:
l’une est que per aventure li femme est vierge;	 The first reason is that perhaps the woman is a virgin;
et li seconde est c’on ne puet trover femme bien saichant qui se descuevre as mires, meismement quant elle est caste.	 And the second is that no skilled woman can be found who uncovers herself before mirrors, especially when she is chaste.
Et li tierce maniere si est que par aventure on ne puet trover femme bien saichant en cest art de mains;	 The third manner is that by chance no skilled woman can be found in this craft of hands.
et li quarte maniere si est que li piere de la femme si est plus em parfont que li piere de l’ome, por coi il i couvient faire plus parfonde taille, et grant paour i a. Et se necessitez semont a ceu, si covient que tu preignes une mieresse bien sachant, et a poines la trueve on, et se tu n’en trueves, point si quier I caste mire subtil;	 The fourth manner is that the woman's stone (womb) is deeper than the man's, so it requires more profound cutting and causes great fear. If you need to perform such a procedure, then you must take a skilled midwife, although it may be difficult to find one, and if you cannot find one, do not hesitate to use a subtle chaste maiden;
et li presente une baile bien saige en la vie des femmes, ou une femme qui saiche une partie de l’art, et li comande qu’ele faice ceu que tu li comandes de l’inquisicion de la piere;	 and present a wise bailiff in the knowledge of women, or a woman who knows some part of the art, and he commands her to do whatever you command regarding the examination of the stone (womb).
et regarde mout bien se li femme est vierge:	 And look carefully if the woman is a virgin:
adonques li covient bouter son doit ou fondement et querir la piere;	 Then you must press your finger or probe and search for the stone.
et s’ele la trueve, si la constraigne desoz son doit, et li recomande qu’elle boute son doit ou con la malaide, et quiere et presse sa main senestre sus la vessie forment.	 If she finds it, you must hold it beneath your finger and advise her to press with her left hand on the bladder near the uterus.
S’elle la trueve, si covient qu’elle la mueve de greit en greit des l’entree de la vessie jusque desoz, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la cuisse;	 She must move it gently from the bladder's entrance towards the root of the thigh.
puis cope sus la piere en la racine de la cuisse encontre le mileu dou con, lai ou il est mues apparilliet, et sent la piere en celle partie;	 Then you should strike the stone at the root of the thigh near the middle bone, where it moves and feels the stone in that area.
et ne mueve son doi desus la piere ou desoz, et soit li taille au premier petite;	 Do not move your finger above or below the stone, and make a small incision at first.
puis boute lou rait en la taille, se tu sens la piere si acroi la plaie tant que li piere puisse issir fuer, et saiches que maintes manieres de pieres sont:	 Then push the hand (or implement) into the small of the back, if you feel the arrow, open the wound so that the arrow can exit freely, and know that there are many types of arrows.
c’est a savoir, petites et grans et aspres et souez, longes et reondes, et qui ont rains.	 it means small and large, sharp and blunt, long and round, and those with feathers.
si saiches les semblances por savoir l’issue.	 know the forms to understand the cause.
Et se li sans te vaint, si met au leu vitriole broiet, et li tien une houre tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	 And if the arrow avoids you (or "does not come out"), place pulverized vitriol at its location and hold it for an hour until the wound is cauterized.
puis revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer, et aies des estrumens que je t’ai dit en l’estraction de la piere as homes por toi aidier en ton oevre;	 Then return to your work when the arrow is out, and have tools that I told you for the extraction of arrows in men to help you with your task.
et se li sans te vaint, et c’est de l’artere qui est copee, si met la poudre sus le leu et l’estrain de tentes et de bendelz, et ne rencomencier plus ceu, et laisse la piere et ne la traire mie, que par aventure morroit li malaide;	 and if the arrow avoids you (or "does not come out"), and it is an artery that has been cut, place powder on the location and hold with tents and bindles, and do not start again, and leave the arrow and do not draw it, for there is danger of the patient dying.
puis cure la plaie.	 Then heal the wound.
Et quant li chalor dou sanc est apaisie, et li leus porrist, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer.	And when the heat of the blood has been relieved and the wounds have healed, then return to your work until the pain subsides.
de hernie carnouse	Of fleshy hernia
Ramice aquouse n’est autre chose que assemblee de moistor ou blanc syfac, qui est desoz lou keur des coions, que contient l’uef;	 Grind aqous is not anything else but an assembly of moisture or white soap, which is beneath the cartilage of the eyes, containing the yolk.
et est apelez «syfac», et aucune fois est proprement en la toile de l’uef, si c’on cuide que ce soit I autre oef;	 and it is called "syfac," and sometimes it is properly in the egg white, if one thinks that it is another yolk.
et c’est li cuir dou coion entre lou blanc syfac que nos avons dit;	 and it is the skin of the cartilage between the white soap (syfac) which we have said;
et ceu n’avient se poc non.	 and this only occurs in the toe nail.
Et li generation de cest ramice si est de foibleteit que vient as coions, et est espandue celle matiere.	And the cause of this watery hernia is weakness that comes to the testicles, and the matter spreads out.
Et aucune fois si vient de percussion sus les coions, et ceste moistor si a maintes colors:	 And sometimes it comes from striking the eyes, and this moisture may have many colors:
ou c’est color declinans a jaunice, ou c’est sans rouge, ou noir, ou aquous blans, et ce avient plus;	 or it is a yellowish discoloration, or without redness, or black, or white fluid, and this happens more often.
et ce sont li signe de conoistre ceste assemblee, car s’elle est ou blanc syfac que nos avons dit, si est li apostemes reons, I poc lonc si com li figure d’un oef, et n’apert mie li coions, car il a moistor tout entor.	 And these are the signs to recognize this assembly, for if it is white and soft as we have said, it is an abscess, which is long like an egg and does not open the eyes, because it has moisture all around.
Et s’il a moistor en la propre toile, si est li apostemes reons avec une partie de l’uef, et por ceu pense on que c’est uns autres oef;	 And if there is moisture in the very fabric [of the abscess], it is an abscess like a part of an egg, and for that reason one thinks that it is another egg.
et se li moistor est entre le cuir des coions et le blanc syfac, si le sent om bien;	 And if moisture is between the hide of the shoulders and the white flesh, one feels it well.
donques quant tu vues savoir la color de la moistor, si esprueve a tout l’intromissoire quarreit, de coi li forme est ci devant.	 Therefore, to know the color of the moisture, you must probe deeply with care, as its form has been described above.
Selonc ceu donques qui vient aprés l’intromissoire, juge de ceu qui est dedens.	Accordingly, judge what is inside based on the probe that follows.
Et quant nos la curons par fer, si covient que li malaides soit sainiez selonc som pooir et la repletion de son cors;	 And when we treat it with iron (cautery), the patient should be bled as much as our power allows and the state of his body requires.
puis le sovine sus son dos, sus une chose un poc haute, et met desoz lui mout de drapelz;	 Then he lies on his back on a small elevated object and covers him with many cloths.
puis sié sus sa senestre, et comande au ministre qu’il sié a destre, et estende la verge a l’un des II costelz dou keur des coions;	 Then he lies on his left side, and instruct the assistant to sit at his right, and extend the yardstick to one of the two shoulder blades.
puis pren le spatumile leit, et cope le cuir des coions parmi leu dou lonc jusque delez lou poignil, et soit ta fendure toute droite en devisant le cuir des coions jusc’a syfac blanc, et l’escorche subtilment selonc tom pooir;	 Then take the spatula in your left hand and cut the hide of the shoulders along its length until you reach the tip, making sure the incision is straight when cutting the hide of the shoulders up to white flesh, and carefully peel off the skin according to your ability.
puis perce lou syfac plain d’aigue a I large pertus, et estrai toute l’aigue, et puis met tes oncines, et estent lou syfac amont;	 Then pierce the syphac fully with water and let out all the water, then put your fingers in, and hold the syphac up.
et ne touchier le keur des coions, mais que le syfac soulement;	 and only touch the cavity of the bladder, but not the kidneys.
cope tout ou par pieces meismement le costeit de lui subtil, que se tu ne le copes bien saigement, si revenra li aigue;	 carefully break or in pieces the ribs of it entirely, for if you do not break it well, the water will return.
et se l’uef saut fuer a ton oevre, si le ramoinne en son leu quant tu avras acomplit l’uevre dou syfac;	 and if the egg jumps out of your work, reset it in its place when you have completed the work on the bladder.
puis assemble les II leivres dou keur des coions a une costure, puis le cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 then assemble the two bellies of the kidneys in a stitch, then treat it like other wounds until it heals.
Et se tu trueves l’uef corromput d’autre maladie, si covient que tu lies les vasselz que sont suspensoire, en doutant le decorrement de sanc;	 and if you find the egg corrupt with another disease, it is necessary to tie the vessels that are hanging, suspecting the discharge of blood.
puis cope le coion a tout le suspensoire, et estrai l’uef, et le cure si com nos avons dit.	 Then pull on the cords to their full extension, extract the egg, and treat it as we have said.
Et se aigue est assemblee en II parties ensamble, saiches que ce sont II ramices;	 And if the ail is assembled in two parts together, know that these are the branches.
si cope l’autre partie si com tu as fait la premiere igalment, puis essue lou sanc, et met en la plaie lainne moillie en oile roset;	 Then pull the other part equally as you did the first, then squeeze out the blood, and put linen moistened in rose oil into the wound.
et met defuer autre laine moillie en vin et en oile, et met sus les II coions, et met desus drapelz doublés, et le lie sus a tout le liien qui est selonc ceste forme:	 and place another linen moistened with wine and oil on the two cords, and put fabric doubled over them, and tie it above all the cord that is in this shape.
Puis pren II drapelz, et les emple de laine charpie selonc ceste semblance et soient assemblez par cousture en la gorle des braies, et li uns des chiés preigne sus le fondement jusc’au dos, et li autres a la partie dou poignil;	 Then take the fabric and use linen straps in this manner and sew them together into a girdle for the thighs. One of the cords should take hold at the base to the back, and the other at the handle part.
et li autre dui chief sus les II angres, et soit toute assemblee li restreinture en la boucle dou braier;	 And the other two bones above the two angles, and let all the restrictions meet at the loop of the bridle.
et aucune fois est medicinee ceste ramice de cautere en leu de taille de fer, et est que tu preignes I cautere cultellaire subtil, et cope le cuir des coions, et soit eschaufez si com nos avons dit, si que li syfac blanc que contient l’aigue est descovers;	 And sometimes this ramice of cautionery is medicine in a place where the iron-sized wound is, and it is that you take the cautery knife, touch the skin there, and let it be heated as we have said, so that the white pus containing water comes out.
si pren lou cautere selonc ceste forme, et perce celui syfac as oncines, et l’escorche a cest subtil cautere chaut:	 take the cautery according to this shape, pierce that pus at once, and scrape off this thin cautery hot.
Et lou cope en toutes les manieres que tu pues, tant que tu esraiches tout;	 And press in all ways as you can until everything is scorched.
et garde que li feus ne touche l’uef;	 and ensure that the fire does not touch the egg.
et saiches que ceste oevre est plus salve;	 and know that this work is more salvific.
et mues gardans de decorrement de sanc, et muedres que li ovraiges de taille;	 And guard against disorder of blood, and move those who have cuts.
et se nulle chose te fait contraire, ou aposteme chaus ou decorremens de sanc ou autre chose, si cure ce qui te fait contraire, selonc ceu qui est devant dit.	 If anything happens contrary to this, or if there is an abscess or bleeding or something else, then cure what happens contrary to this, according to what has been said before.
Et se li malaides est paourous, et ne vuet atendre cest ovraige por son horribleteit, si amenistre perforation, si com je te di, et est que quant tu es bien certains par les significations que nos avons dit que ramice aquouse est lai, si fai seoir le malaide sus I siege leveit;	 And if the patient is afraid and does not want to wait for this procedure due to its horribleness, then perform perforation as I tell you, and it should be that when you are certain by the signs we have mentioned that the anus is in the right place, then make the patient sit on a raised surface.
pues perce l’aposteme an la partie desoz a tout le spatumile large, et met la perforation dou lonc dou cors;	 therefore pierce the abscess in the part below the entire spatula-width wide and place the perforation along the length of the body.
et soit larges li pertus, si que toute li aigue corre fuer;	 And let the wounds be wide, so that all the sharp edges protrude.

des hermofrodites	Hermaphrodites

de la tentigene	Of the tenor (modern English)

et aucunes femmes l’ont ausi grant com une main, et c’est li cure.	 And some women have them as big as a hand, and that is their treatment.

et a une autre char que naist a la bouche de la marris, et l’emple, et par aventure saut fuer, et est selonc la semblance d’une kowe, et por ceu l’apelerent li ancien «maladie kowee». de erratique	The erratic growth is a hardened or stone-like tumor on the surface of the body; and it is called "erratic" because it cannot be removed by simple cutting. When this kind of swelling arises in the body, it should be cut open with a knife until it is completely severed from its base; then take a hot iron or an emetic and cauterize (sear) the wound, so that the bad humors do not remain there and cause more pain.
Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis;	 Erratic is when the nature of a woman is not perceived or if the opening is small;
et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est;	 and it is by birth or accident due to disease that it comes about.
ou c’est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit;	 Or it is by hot iron, or sharp needle fine or thick, and it is made completely in the marriage [operation], or in the chest, or under, or wherever it may be.
et deffent le concevoir, et l’enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir;	 and prevent conception, childbirth, and, by chance, the flowers to grow;
et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile.	 and the knowledge of these things is by the look of the woman's face.
Se li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait.	 If the swelling is close to appearing, it may be at your hand or arm.
S’il est dou syfac subtil, et il est prochiens as II leivres, si te haste, et la ront ensi:	 If it is a sharp needle that is near the liver, go quickly and pierce it thus:
met tes II dois indices ensamble, et li femme soit sus son dos, espandues ses jambes;	 place your two index fingers together, and the woman is above her back, spreading her legs.
puis estent les II leivres forment, tant que li subtilz syfac soit rons, et soit overs li estoupemens;	 then spread the two livers fully, so that the fine sharp needle is round and over the incisions.
puis pren laine, et la moille en oile, et la met sus le leu, et gise li femme a home chescun jor, si qu’il ne puist souder.	 then take wool, wet it in oil, and place it on the wound, and let the woman lie at home every day so that it does not heal [over].
Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte.	 And if the soft place is hard and thick, you must cut it with a tool resembling a myrtle leaf.
Se li estoupemens est de char nee, si la sospent a l’oncine et la cope;	 If the swelling is of flesh, suspend it at the onion and strike (it).
