puis soit curez d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then treat with other remedies until it is healed.
Et quant en la marris vient char nee, si la covient coper selonc ceste maniere, se ce n’est apostemes enchancrez.	 And when snow falls in marriage (meaning winter), it should be covered in this manner, unless the abscesses are aggravated.
Car a l’aposteme enchancreit qui est en la marris, ne doit on touchier de feir.	 For an aggravated abscess that occurs during winter, one should not intervene with fire.
des emorroides	1. Hemorrhoids
Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul;	 Hemorrhoids are openings of veins without cort (cortex) treatment, and when hemorrhoids become old, they turn into a scab.
et nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’aus, et les signes, et je dirai ci celles qui resoivent curation.	 And we have said in the previous section similar things about them, and their symptoms, and I will say here the ones that can be cured.
Je di que les emorroides et li thelul, quant il sont em parfont en la marris, et il n’aperent au sentir, si n’est mie li cure par fer.	 I say that hemorrhoids and ulcers, when they are completely in winter and cannot be felt, should not be cured by fire.
Cil qui sont a la bouche de la marris, c’on puet sentir, sont cil c’on puet curer.	 Those which are at the mouth of winter, can be felt, are those that can be cured.
Il covient donques que tu mettes la femme en une maison froide, puis estent l’altelul as tenailles, et le cope en ses racines, puis poudre sus medicines restraignans sanc, si com acaice et sanc de dragon et encens, et semblans choses;	 Therefore, you must put the woman in a cold house, then heat the iron at the tongs, and strike its roots, then sprinkle powdered medicine that stops blood, such as cinnabar and dragon's blood, and similar things;
puis boute ses piez a la paroit une houre, puis la met en aigue froide;	 Then press her feet to the wall for an hour, then immerse her in cold water.
et se decorremens de sanc i vient, si la fai seoir en une decoction de sumac et d’escorce de pomes grenates et de gales et de semblans choses, et puis pren farine d’orge, et la confis avec miel et aisil, et en fai I emplaustre sus son dos.	 And when bleeding occurs, make her sit in a decoction of sumac and apple peel, gall, and similar things, then take barley flour, mix it with honey and egg white, and apply it as a plaster on her back.
Et se il estainche, c’est boin.	 And if it stops bleeding, that is good.
Se ceu non, se li fai aerdre ventouses au dos et as mameles sens ferir;	 If that doesn't work, make her breathe inflated bladders on the back and the breasts without cutting them;
puis pren lainne, et la moille en jus de plantain ou en jus d’aglentier avec vin viel, et fai aerdre au leu.	 Then take flax, wet it at the end of plantain or elder with old wine, and apply it to the place.
Et quant li aposteme repose, si cure lou leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;	 And when the abscess rests, heal the wound with ointment until it is healed;
et celle qui est apelee «albathir» est rouge, et est semblans a I chief aspre, si le covient coper si com j’ai dit le thelul;	 And that which is called "albathir" is red and resembles a sharp head, if it needs to be covered as I have said in the thelul;
et puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And then heal it until it is healthy.
des apostemes de la marris	abscesses in the womb
Maintes manieres d’aposteme vienent en la marris, si com chancre et aposteme pierous et herpes et estiomenes et fistules et emorroides et aposteme chaut, et plusors autres maladies que j’ai dit en la division.	 Many kinds of abscess come in the marriage (procreation), such as boils and pus-filled abscesses, herpes, fistulas, hemorrhoids, hot abscesses, and other diseases that I have mentioned in the division.
Il covient donques que je die en cest traitier l’aposteme chaut qui vient en la marris, qui n’est mie des apostemes que coillent bowe;	 Therefore I must say in this treatise about the hot abscess that comes in marriage, which is not one of those abscesses that are collected with a clamp;
et se tu vues savoir l’ovraige de fer, si regarde se li apostemes est agus en l’encomencement de sa venue, et plain de chalor et de fievre, et s’il devient rouge se tu le pues veoir.	 And if you want to know the work of iron, look and see if the abscess is acute at the beginning of its coming, and full of heat and fever, and if it becomes red if you can see it.
Adonques ne te haster mie de percier, mais lou fais meurer tant que li dolor soit apaisie;	 Then do not rush to puncture, but let it heal until the pain is eased;
et puis fai seoir lou malaide sus I siege, et ait II petis sieges ou il se cline, et apoie sus son dos et assemble ses piez as parties defuer la jambe;	 And then make the patient sit on a chair or two small chairs where he leans, and support his back and gather his legs to the opposite sides of the leg.
et soient ses cuixes espandues, et mette ses braz desoz ses genous, et les lie bien d’un boin liien;	 And spread out his thighs, and place his arms under his knees, and tie them well with a good rope.
puis succe li baille devers lou destre costeit, et i amenistre l’estrument dont on oevre la bouche de la marris, de coi ci aprés vient li forme;	 Then bring the ball to the right side, and introduce the tool used to open the mouth of the bladder, from which comes the shape.
et covient que quant tu i vues amenistrer cest estrument, que tu fiches le rait premier ens por savoir la parfondeté de la marris, si que ceu qui entre ens de l’estrument n’i viegne plus em parfont qu’il ne doit, et qu’il ne blece la malaide;	 And it is necessary that when you introduce this tool, that you pierce the right side first to know the depth of the bladder, so that what enters within from the tool does not go further than it should, and does not prick the patient.
et se li estrumens est plus grans, si covient covrir la parfondesce de la marris de drapelz, si que li estrumens ne li grieve;	 If the wound is larger, it is necessary to cover its depth with cloths so that the wound does not hurt.
et covient qu’il mette le cornet de l’estrument au desus, et qu’il teigne l’estrument.	 It is necessary that he puts the horn of the instrument on top, and that he stains the instrument.
Et quant li apostemes apert, et on lou fent a la main mol, si le covient coper au chief, au spatumile leit;	 And when the abscess is opened and softened by hand, it should be covered with linen cloth.
et quant li bowe est vuidie, si covient que tu mettes en la plaie tentes moillies en oile roset, ou en oile vert sec;	 And when the bladder is emptied, you must put in the wound wet linen soaked in rose oil or dry green oil.
et met la tente fuer de la plaie au parfont de la marris, et met par defuer sus la marris et sus le poignil lainne nette moillie en aigue ou malves soient cuites;	 Place the skin of the wound over the cloth, place the cloth on the inside and outside of the wound, and on the end of the arrow place a clean wet linen soaked in vinegar or wormwood.
puis le cure aprés II jors d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	 Then cure after two days of ointment application, as long as he is healthy;
et aucune fois leve on la marris et la plaie par clistere d’aigue et de miel, et puis d’aigue ou racines de lis et aristologe longe soient cuites;	 And sometimes one raises the wound and the sore with clysterium of water and honey, and then with water or liquorice roots and Aristolochia longa should be cooked;
puis reveigne a l’oignement.	 Then return to the ointment application.
Et se li plaie est reponue en la marris, si covient que tu te gardes de cuire de fer, mais cure la si com nos avons dit en la division.	 If the wound is healed in a marriage (union), it is necessary that you abstain from iron cooking, but treat it as we have said in the division.
de l’enfantement	Of childbirth
Mestier est premier a la baile qu’elle conoisse la figure de l’enfantement natureil, et li signes si est quant tu vois la femme apresser aval, et desire odorer l’ar:	 First, the midwife should recognize the figure of natural birth, and signs if you see the woman pushing in the lower part, and desiring to smell the anus;
adonques se haste li enfes de fuer issir;	 Then hasten the child to come out with force.
adonc saiches que cil enfantemens est selonc la figure natureil, et est li issue soz son chief, et li secondine avec lui;	 Then recognize that this childbirth is according to the natural figure, and it is the issue under the head, and the second one follows with it.
et quant tu vois ces signes, si covient presser legierement son ventre, si que li enfes isse tost;	 And when you see these signs, it is necessary to gently press his abdomen so that he defecates quickly.
car quant il dessent sus son chief, si ist li secondine avec lui, et est mondee li marris de ses superfluitez par bone mundification;	 For when he defecates on top of his head, the second one should follow with him and clean the husband of his superfluidities through good cleansing.
et cist qui vient autrement ne vient mie naturelment.	 And this which comes otherwise does not come naturally.
Car il vient aucune fois sus ses piez, et vient fuer li cors ou li chiés, et les mains, ou il vient sus son ventre, ou sovin, et est convertis par aventure sor son col, et par autres figures malvaises;	 For it sometimes comes on his feet, and the body or chest, hands, or stomach erupt, or it turns around his neck, or in other bad forms.
si est mestier a la baile qu’elle soit saige et subtilz en ces choses, et se warse d’error et de decevement, et je vos mostrerai toutes les figures coment on li doit aidier.	 Therefore it is necessary that the bailiff be wise and skillful in these things, and to guard against error and deception, and I will show you all the forms in which one should help him.
Se li enfes vient sus son chief par issue natureil, et li femme enfante griement, et li vertus de li est foible, si la fai seoir sus une selle, ou les femmes la tienent;	 If a child comes out of the head naturally, and a woman gives birth with difficulty, and the strength of the child is weak, make her sit on a saddle, or let women hold her.
et arose sa nature d’oile ou fenugreic soit cuit, et puis boute li baile entre ses dois le petit spatumile dont ci est li forme:	 and anoint its nature with oil or fenugreek that has been cooked, then insert the pledget (or small spatula) between its two fingers in the shape of this model:
et fende la secondine, et cope a son ungle tant que li moistors qui est ens corre fuers;	 and split open the second incision, and press on the nail to force out the moisture that is inside.
et preint lou ventre de la femme tant que li enfes dessende, et s’il ne dessent, si covient clisterizer la femme de muscillaige de fenugrec avec oile de sisament;	 and tie the woman's belly tightly until the child is born, and if it does not come out, you must cleanse her with a poultice of fenugreek with camomile oil.
puis la fai preindre et esternuer de condisi, et tien sa bouche et son neis une houre:	 then make her take and expectorate condusi (medicine), hold her mouth and nose for an hour:
si istra maintenant l’enfes.	 Straighten the intestines now.
Et se les II mains issent fuer, si covient que tu les ramoinne legierement poc et poc;	 If both hands come out (of the body), it is necessary that you gently reinsert them little by little;
et s’elles n’i puent entrer, si met la femme sus I siege, et li lieve les piés en haut;	 and if they cannot enter, put a woman on the seat, and raise her legs.
puis deboute le siege sus terre, et teigne on la femme, qu’elle ne chiece au deboutement;	 then tilt the seat onto the ground, and bind the woman so she does not move during the procedure.
et se li mains n’i puet entrer, et li enfes muert, si li cope les mains au couteil qui est ci devant mis, et estrai l’enfant, et ramoine igalment.	 and if the hands cannot enter, and the intestines are dead, strike the hands with the knife that is placed before you, extract the child, and reset it (the intestines) equally.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses piés	 of the issue of the child upon its feet
Quant li enfes vient sus ses piez, si lou covient bouter en haut;	 When the intestines come out onto the feet, you must push them upward;
et puis le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit igalz;	 and then twist it little by little, until it is even.
puis preigne I des piez et l’estende poc et poc.	 Then take the pieces and extend them little by little.
Cant il saut jusc’as cuixes, si la comande a preindre, et la fai esternuer de condisi;	 Can it jump up to the hips, if commanded, and make it vomit of condish? (In English: If commanded, can it jump up to the hips and cause it to vomit of condish?)
si saut fuer, se Deus vuet.	 if it jumps away, if God wills. (In English: If it jumps away, if God wills.)
Et s’il n’ist fuer si com nos avons dit, si le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit selonc la figure natureil.	And if it [the dislocation] is not as we have said, turn it gently until it is according to the natural figure.
Car adonques ist il legierement.	Here comes the translation: Gently turn it.
Et s’il ne vient fuer si com nos avons, dit si pren muscillaige de altee, et oile de sisament, et gomme fondue, et broie tout en I mortier;	 And if it does not jump away as we have experienced, say take musk-garlic of high altitude, oil of sesame, and melted gum, and grind everything together in the mortar. (In English: And if it doesn't jump away as we have experienced, say take musk-garlic of high altitude, oil of sesame, melted gum, and grind everything together in the mortar.)
et met sus la nature de la femme dedens et defuer cest oignement, puis la fai seoir en aigue tede jusque desoz les costelz;	 and put it inside the woman's nature and anoint this ointment, then make her sit in a cold sweat below the ribs. (In English: And put it inside the woman's nature and anoint this ointment, then make her sit in a cold sweat below the ribs.)
et quant elle est moillifie desoz, se li fai I coliere de mirre, et li met desoz, et li laisse une houre;	 And when it is softened inside, make the myrrh collar and place it underneath, and leave it for an hour.
puis la fai seoir sus I siege, puis la fai esternuer et estraint sa bouche et son neis, et li preint le ventre legierement, car li enfes saut maintenant.	 Then make him sit on the seat, then make him cough and hold his mouth and nose, and press lightly on the belly because the infant is about to come now.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses genous	From the birth of the child on its thighs
Quant li enfes vient en ceste forme, si i mette li baile ses mains poc et poc;	 When the child comes in this form, place the bailiff's hands near it.
puis soit sovinee sus son col, et li pendent li piez aval, et soit gisans sor I lit;	 Then lay it on its neck, and hang its feet downwards, and let it lie on the bed.
et plie ses mains poc et poc, et puis li preint les mains sus lou ventre, et li oste les cussins desoz, tant qu’elle soit appareillie aval;	 Fold its hands near each other, then press on the hands on its belly, and push out the cushions underneath, until it is delivered.
et se li enfes ne saut, si pren ses piez et li muef forment, puis li muef lou ventre amont, puis i boute tes mains;	 If the child does not jump out, take its feet and move it, then move its belly upwards, and push your hands inside.
et ewe l’enfant poc et poc;	 And pull the child little by little;
et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse.	 And instruct the woman to take care of herself until the children are born.
de l’issue de l’enfant qui vient dou large une main pendant	The newborn child coming out, one hand holds it from above.
I covient engignier a ramener la main:	 It is necessary to devise a way to return the hand:
s’on ne la puet ramener, si fai lever la femme, et aler;	 If it cannot be returned, make her rise and walk.
s’elle ne puet aler, si la fai gesir sus I lit, et li deboute les jambes forment;	 If she cannot walk, make her lie on the bed, bend her legs properly;
puis amenistre lou muscillaige que j’ai conteit;	 Then bring me the mustard poultice that I mentioned.
et s’elle n’enfante, si la fai seoir sus I siege, puis estudie au rameneir la main;	 And if she does not give birth, make her sit on the chair, then study on how to return the hand;
et ewe l’enfant selonc la figure natureil, et la fai esternuer, et li comande qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse fuer.	 Pull the child according to its natural shape, make her vomit, and instruct her to take care of herself until the children are born.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus son col, et ait espandues ses mains, et sa faice tornee devers lou dos sa mere	For the delivery of the child on its neck, have her spread her hands and turn her face towards the back of its mother.
I covient que li baile teigne sa main, puis le torne poc et poc, et l’ewe legierement;	 It is required that the bailiff grasp his hand, then turn it little by little, and pull gently.
et quant il est igalz, si met sus la nature muscillaige de altee et oile, si com nos avons dit, puis li comande qu’elle se mueve poc et poc;	 And when it is equal, place the natural muscle balm of althea and oil upon it as we have said, then instruct it to move little by little.
et quant tu avras ce fait, si la fai seoir sus I siege, et li comande k’elle se preigne;	 And when you have done this, make her sit on the seat, and command that she takes hold of herself.
et la fai esternuer.	 Make her vomit.
de ceste meisme maniere a tout la secondine	In the same way, administer treatment to all those affected in turn.
Quant il vient fuer en ceste maniere a tout la secondine, si cope la secondine a ton ungle, tant que li moistors soit vuidie;	 When the feces come in this manner completely from the anus, you press the rectum with your nail until the moisture is emptied.
et se li enfes pent sus sa faice et sus son col, si la cope des la boude, qu’elle ne soit retenue, et muere li enfes;	 If the infant's head is pushed against its face and neck, you press down from the buttocks so that it is not held back, and the infant dies.
puis boute l’enfant dedens, tant que tu l’aies mis si com il covient, et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne aucune fois:	 Push the child inside, as far as necessary, until it is properly positioned; and command the woman to take hold of herself once.
adonques si istra legierement.	 Then slightly move him from side to side.
de l’issue des gemelz	of the twins' birth
Saiches que gemeil naissent maintes fois, et aucune fois en naissent III ou IIII;	 Know that twins are born often, and sometimes three or four are born at once.
et ceu n’est mie estrainge chose, et poc avient.	 And it is not strange, but it happens occasionally.
Dui sont estrainge chose, et ne vivent mie, se poc nom;	 Twins are strange things, and they do not live if they can be named.
je sai ceu, qu’il soient multipliiet, et sont desevrez par lou syfac qui les devise, qui est liiez a la boude;	 I know that they multiply excessively, and are driven by the siphac, which is connected to the uterus.
et aucune fois issent ausi naturelment com uns tous sous, si com nos avons dit.	 And sometimes they issue naturally like an animal giving birth, as we have said.
Et s’il issent griement, si la cure si com nos avons dit, et soit li baile subtilz, et faice tost et legierement ceu qu’elle fait;	 If they issue with difficulty, then the cure is as we have said, and let the midwife be skilled, and do quickly and gently whatever she does.
et faice ensi com il vaut mues a salut.	 And do as is fitting for salvation.
de plusors enfans	of many children  --> multiple children (in this context)
Aucune fois sont formez en la marris I ou II ou III ou IIII ou V ou VI ou VII, ou plusors jusc’a XV, et sont tout formeit en forme d’enfant par le mesurement dou saige glorious, et couvient que li baile saiche tout ceu, car par aventure semblans chose li avient;	 Sometimes they form in the marriage from the first to the second or third or fourth or fifth or sixth or seventh, or more up to fifteen, and they are all formed in the shape of a child by the measurement of the wise man. The bailiff should know this, because by chance similar things can happen;
si faice selonc ceu qu’il covient.	 Follow as required.
de l’enfant mort	of the dead child
Quant tu cures la femme de l’enfant mort ou ventre, si com j’ai dit en la division, et il ne vient fuers, et tu es constrains d’ovraige de mains;	 When treating a woman with a stillborn child or an unborn child, as I mentioned in the division, and it does not come out spontaneously, and you are forced to work by hand;
si covient que tu saiches se li femme est de saine vertut, et n’ait accident ou elle ait paor de mort;	 then you must know whether the woman is of good virtue and has no accident or fear of death.
si covient que li femme soit sovinee sus son dos, et soit ses chiés enclins aval, et les jambes levees;	 The woman should be placed on her back, her head inclined downward, and her legs raised.
et li ministre la teigne de II pars, ou elle soit liie au lit si qu’elle ne soit traite au dessendement de l’enfant;	 And the minister should hold her by two parts or tie her to the bed so she is not treated for the delivery of the child.
puis frotez la bouche de la marris d’oiles moistes avec muscillaige de altee et de fenugrec et semence de lin, puis oigne li baile ses mains de ces oiles et de ces muscillaiges;	 Then anoint the mouth of the mother with moist oil mixed with myrrh and comfrey and flax seeds, then anoint the midwife's hands with these oils and this myrrh.
puis les boute en la marris legierement, puis quiere I leu ou elle boute les oncines que soient covenaubles a ceu, et pren warde se li enfes est apparilliez qu’il dessende sus son chief;	 Then push it gently into the socket, then look for the joints where it can be repositioned and take care that the tendons are not torn apart as they stretch over its head.
si fiche les oncines en ses eulz ou en son col ou en sa bouche ou en som palais ou desoz la barbe ou en la forcele ou pres des costez, et se li dessendemens est sus piez, se li fiche ou poignil et as costes moienes;	 If the tendons are driven into the elbows or neck or mouth or palate or under the beard or wrist or near the sides, and if there is tearing of the tendons, drive it or push it towards the mid-rib.
et covient qu’il teigne l’oncine a sa main destre, et mette la corbeure entre ses dois de la senestre main, et li boute a tout sa main legierement, et fiche l’oncine en aucun de ces leus que nos avons dit, tant qu’il viegne a la chose vuide;	 And you must grip the tendon with your right hand, place the crook between your left fingers, and push it gently to its full extent, and drive the tendon into any of the places that have been mentioned above until it reaches the empty space.
et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	 And this is the shape of the scythe:
puis fiche encontre I autre oncine, ou le tier se tu en as mestier, si que li estractions soit igalz;	 Then point against the other scythe, or whichever one you need to extract, so that the extractions are even;
et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	 and then stretch it equally by moving from one side to the other so that the scythes move out, and let the teeth of the scythe hold them, as shown in the shape:
Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie;	 And if there remains any part, then press one of your oil-soaked thumbs against it and push into that part, pulling the other part.
et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	 And if there remains none at all, then place this scythe or higher up and continue until it comes out completely.
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement, si covient que tu envoloupes sus I drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote;	 And if one hand comes before the other and cannot be brought back by pressure, then you must wind around the fabric until it comes out completely.
puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as II piés.	 Then hold the heel at the joint of the foot or toe, and similarly you must do with the other hand, and for both feet.
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee, si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue;	 If the child's hip is fat and narrow at the exit, or if it has a sharp point assembled, you must insert the pointed spatula between your fingers and push the sharp point and draw out the projection.
ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;	 or you will rotate it with the instrument called "almidach", from which the shape comes with the instruments or chapter that follows this.
et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;	 and similarly do so if the child naturally has a large head.
et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles, et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;	 Then pull the bones apart with the tongs, and if the hip jumps out and it is tightened in the socket, it should be cut, as long as the moisture that is deeper inside is.
et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;	 And if it cannot come out, you shall chop it into pieces as you can.
et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	 And if it is inflamed in the belly or under the ribs, then it must be pierced until the moisture escapes.
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	And if the swelling is on top of the feet, the attraction is slight, and the reduction to the mouth of the bladder is easy.
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a I drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	 And if it is strangled in the belly or under the chest, then it must be opened with the glove enveloped over the hand;
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	 And the belly or chest should be cut open until the moisture which is there escapes.
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure, si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	 And if another member is separated and the head remains, then put the thumb of the hand into the opening of the wound, and pull it out to the mouth of the wound.
puis i boute I oncine ou II, et le trai fuer;	 Then insert the finger or two and pull it further.
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier, ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	 And if the mouth of the sore is narrowed by abscess heat that has come, it should not be worked on, instead it should be provided with moist and fat things.
et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	 And apply ointments, and let them bathe in warm soothing and moistening liquids.
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	 And if the bone is on the ribs and can be leveled, provide what was said earlier for a live infant.
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	 And if there is no ability to do that, break it into pieces and leave nothing of the secondary part.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	 And when you have done this, provide what was said earlier for abscess-covered sores in the sore.
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	 If blood flow occurs, it should be stopped by warm compression and other treatments provided.
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut .i. autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	And I saw a woman whose womb had killed an infant, then consulted another about it and revived the other infants.
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	After a long time an abscess came to his armpit and swelled so much that it opened and started to burst.
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	I was called for the treatment, but I thought for a long time and could not heal the wound.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	I put on strong plasters with great adhesion, and an bone came out, and after several days another one.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	I marvel much, because the belly has no bones.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	It seemed to be the bones of a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em millor point;	 I probe the wound, and with my hands I touch the bone until the woman is in a better position.
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	 and let the woman lie there for a long time, and thus slightly bend her leg towards the side.
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	 I have not encountered this chapter except when masters find something strange that they know how to help with it.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	To bring back the dislocated shoulder to its place
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres;	 Here comes the form of the press, to which we apply the books.
et a II tornans as II chiés des II liiens.	 and turn the heads of the two screws.
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	 Moreover, the horn should be finer than the restrictor, and made of ebony or boxwood;
et soit li bouche dou fust I doi de large, et li marge des arbres I doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	 and the mouth of the cylinder should be wide, and the edge of the tree should be even, and a half palm long;
et enmi les II liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	 And between the two limbs there are two shoulder joints of the same bone, which are joined firmly in both, half a palm length or a little more;
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les II cornes.	 and these two joints are pushed into the mouth of the socket to open when one turns the two horns (or limbs).
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	 Another form, with a more subtle and lighter appearance, is made of ebony or boxwood, resembling pliers (or tweezers);
et ait as II chiés II ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et II dois de large;	 and let the size of the two joints, as you see, be one palm length, and two fingers wide;
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor I lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes, puis boute les II ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	 and when you see opening the socket with all the instruments, make the woman sit on a bed, her feet hanging and legs apart, then push the two joints together into the socket, and hold the head of the instrument between her knees.
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	 Then work your hand with all the instruments as you have done with the pliers equally, according to the quantity that you want to open the mouth of the anvil, until the bail does what it wants.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances;	 All these instruments are covered and multiplied in their similar forms;
et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	 And when the blacksmiths have prepared them, it is more eagerly worked and higher above men because of their quantity.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	Do not hastily prepare the instrument without first arranging it, as its necessity is not easily excused.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	 When the secondine is confined in childbirth, you must command the patient to hold her anus, and then make her strain with contractions, and hold your hands at the mouth and nose.
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	 If she jumps because of that, it is good.
Se ceu non, si prent I pot, et fai I pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	 If not, it takes a pot, and makes a pot or lid, and places herbs that can open the mouth of the wound, such as calamint, rue, chamomile, cascara sagrada, and centaury.
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu;	 all these herbs, or some of them, should be cooked or boiled in water over the fire;
puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris, et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris;	 then place a cloth or lid on the pot, and hold the other end in the mouth of the wound, and press until the vapors enter the wound.
puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	 then make it vomit, as we have said.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	If the second one jumps quickly.
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature, et quiere la secondine;	 And if it remains after this treatment and does not fart, instruct the woman to moisten her left hand in sesame oil or musk oil from aloes, and then insert it into her anus and press gently.
et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	 And when she has found it, take and stretch it little by little straight, so that the muscles do not resist the extraction.
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie;	 but it must be moved gently to the right and to the left, and then pull.
si venra et se desaerdra.	 if it comes out and detaches itself.
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	 And if the mouth of the muscle is stretched wide open, we have said the treatment for purges and fumigation with herbs.
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	 and if it is not any of what we have said, make sure you do not force when pulling.
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	 but it must be that the one at the mouth of the muscle, you tie it to the woman's thigh, then clysterize with an ointment formula four.
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer;	 If it [the dislocation] can be restored and returned, it will heal.
mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	 But nonetheless, when it [the dislocation] cannot be restored, if it comes out badly, it puts the patient in danger.
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu:	 Therefore, it is necessary to use appropriate fumigations for this:
aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	 Any of the ancient ones have proven fumigation of dill and dried figs.
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	The shape of the instrument used for fumigating a woman to retain flowers and afterbirth is as follows:
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	 And it is to be observed that it resembles a piece of glass, and the head is placed delicately in its natural position, and the larger parts are heated over the fire.
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	 And let the fumigation be on the embers, and the heat until it is destroyed, and start another one.
de percier lou fondement	To drill the foundation.
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	 Many children are born without the foundation pierced, but it has been plugged up by a subtle substance:
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	 Therefore, it is necessary for the patient to pierce that bone at its proper place, and not with a sharp splint, and ensure that the ligament is not touched.
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then put soft linen soaked in wine and oil on it, then treat with salve until it heals.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	And if you doubt that it does not recur, put or place a plum stone there, and leave it for many days, and it should be removed when the patient is seen to go to bed.
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme;	 And sometimes there comes this kind of swelling of sudden wound or abscess;
si covient coper celui soudement:	 it is necessary to cover that swelling.
si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	 If it's a wound, treat it as we have said with the solution of lead.
de la fistule dou fondement	From the fistula base
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des II parties, si a une fistule ou plusors;	 Fistulas that come from under the foundation are knotty and larger than those that come from above the foundation, or in the space between two parts, either one fistula or more.
et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe, et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans;	 And when that knot is old, it works again, and moisture awakens white or subtle pus, and sometimes they become Persian fistulas.
et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	 They are known by those who have it, either excretion or flatulence when the patient makes excretions, and occasionally leaps one sidewards.
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge;	 And if it is fistulas that penetrate up to the bladder, and up to half of the penis;
et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	 They reach up to the knee joint, and up to the knuckle of the cow.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	 And thus, one knows a Persian fistula by its foundation, not necessarily Persian.
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	 And you press your finger or foundation into it, and push a thin needle of copper or iron into the fistula when there is no twisting.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou I poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	 And if it has tortuosity, push a tent of thin plank or horsehair against it until you feel the tent or the hair at your fingertip;
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	 and if you do not feel it, and it does not produce pus, inflammation or worms, as we have said:
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie;	 know that it does not pierce.
si te haste dou curer.	 hasten to cure it.
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	And when the fistula penetrates up to the bladder or leads to the conduit of urine, if it shoots out urine and cannot be sealed with medicine.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	 If it pierces up to the knee joint, the tendon is coming out at the level:
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	 if there is no tortuosity and the pain subsides around it, then it is already bowed, and no medicine or treatment with liniment will help:
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	 and in these Persian blisters, there is no cure but hard work, and the vain efforts of foolish people who meddle with it.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit, et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos;	 In one who is not a Persian and is not old, with hope of health through fire, as I have experienced, the patient lies between your hands on his back.
et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	 and lift the legs up to the thighs, and bend the thighs towards the stomach.
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	 then insert a tent of linen or of willow if there is curvature, as long as you know where the dislocation comes from.
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice, se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet;	 If the patient feels it around the base, then you must insert your index finger there, and if it feels as though the dislocation has been pierced.
et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	 and expose where you feel the dislocated joint or bone, then know that it is dislocated.
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	 If one does not work on it, it cannot be healed.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	 One should however know that one can heal some, but this happens seldom;
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	 And the aid one gives to it, it is that one heats the cautery gently according to the width of the wound, as has already been said.
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement;	 and push everything hot into the wound until it comes out from the base;
et faice ceu II fois ou III, tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	 and do this two or three times, until you know that these charred pieces are burned, which resemble the quill of a bird;
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	 and then treat it with moistened tents in butter until the charred pieces are gone, then treat it with a healing ointment that is warm and soothing.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	 If it can be healed well, that's good.
Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	 If the head cannot be made whole;
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	 and if it tries to enter but does not pierce to the point that is its foundation, and between your finger and the head you put a thick covering of flesh or gauze, and you see the fistula at the head where the covering had been placed;
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	 if the tip of the fistula starts from the head and advances towards the shoulder, and then the cautery is applied afterwards until it reaches the base of the shoulder;
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra;	 and the shoulder will be released and will heal.
puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	 Cut off the fatty tissue that resembles a bird's feather, and none should remain.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	And if the bone breaks through [the skin], and pierces you, either burn it with fire or apply a medicinal cure.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble II bones choses:	 For fire cauterization has two good effects:
c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	 This is to know, the arthritis of these disjointed joints, and the draining of blood and removal of moisture.
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	 then, treat wounds soaked in butter or in crushed cheese, until the flesh is boiled in the butter, and let the joints be submerged in the butter.
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	 then, treat the wound with onion juice mixed with hard charcoal, and use dry medicines.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	When it is reset, it heals and does not dislocate again.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	If a fistula comes up to the surface of the foundation and is separated from the body, push your thumb or the foundation into it and probe it.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre II est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des III manieres:	 If you feel the wound and between it is fabric or leather or joint that is about to burst, there should not be fear except for a way of faith and hope, by the administration of one of the three methods:
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	 or you cauterize it as we have said, or you push it to the bottom, or if it is filled with pus, apply hot compresses and treat it as first.
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	 And do not go too deep, cover the holding device that holds the foundation, and the evacuations come by their own will.
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	 then heal, as we have said.
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	 If by chance it becomes healthy again, remove that covering and clean it when it is removed from the foundation, either by force or with some other tool.
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	 Then mold the charrue (plow) in the wound as you can.
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement:	 Then study to restore the wound, and keep the fistula on the side away from the foundation.
si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	 If it is easier for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere:	 And sometimes there are fistulas in this manner.
et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus, si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	 When you force the tent into the fistula and it is on the side of the foundation under the skin above, take a pointed tent in its head according to this form.
Et i boute .i. fil tort en .ij., et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	And put .i. thread twisted in .ij., and push the tent peg through the entire length of the thread into the fistula until it reaches the head.
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	 If it is perforated on the edge of the foundation within, then draw out the thread of that pierced one, thus you press your finger or foundation.
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les II chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse I jor ou II;	 and draw out the head of the thread, and bring together the two shoulders, and press one against the other, and leave it for a day or two.
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	 and do not move it at any time, until the threads heal the sores that are between them, and close.
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	 then treat the wound until it is healed and healthy.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	If the fistula does not open by itself, make it open in all possible ways as you can, if it is not too deep.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	It is not advisable to cover a wound with a plaster while it is healing, as previously mentioned, until it is healed.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	 The shape of a spiked splint, from which a fistula is made, is very sharp at one end and notched.
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	 and not on the other side, because you should not touch what you should not touch, as you can see here:
des emorroydes	hemorrhoids   (medical condition characterized by the swelling of veins in the rectum and anus)
Emorrydes sont selonc II manieres:	 Emordizes are of two kinds.
ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc, et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement;	 They are within the foundation, as in a lump of resin, and there are both small and large ones, and on the surface there is blood, and there may be one or more, and they are displaced from the foundation and at the base of the foundation.
mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor, et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	 But those that are displaced have little moisture, and there is either a small amount of acidic citrus juice or a small amount of blood, and they have the color of flesh.
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	 and the treatment for those that have them within the foundation is to command the patient to strain in order to relieve themselves in chambers, until the foundation settles, and this can be felt by the fingers.
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	 if you hurry up, hold it with tweezers, or grasp it with your nail, then strike at its roots.
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a I drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	 And if the shoulder joint cannot be held due to moisture, take a cloth or linen, or a piece of silk;
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	 and straighten it [the shoulder] with your hands, then strike it [the dislocated joint], and powder some hot powders in place of cautery over it.
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, pues les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	 or you can cauterize it as mentioned in the "cautery" chapter, then heal it with other treatments until it heals.
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	 and if the foundation cannot come out [of the wound], then apply a biting and harsh enema to the patient to cleanse what is in the foundation, so that it can come out easily.
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	 if the patient washes himself and the thread [of sutures] comes out of the wound, then the treatment is simple.
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	 And it is that you grasp them with your fingernail or tweezers, strike them, then heal as we have said, until they are healed and fear the incision by iron.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere:	 It is necessary to apply the suturing in this manner:
pren I fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les II chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille, et si soit dou large;	 Take the twisted thread, put it in a needle, then pull the thread above and pierce the needle from the other side, and turn the two ends of the thread below the needle, making sure it is wide enough.
et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse I por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	 tighten the thread, then knot it, pull out the needle, and do the same for all the others, leaving the excess blood to flow.
puis met sus le fondement I drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	 then place a moistened linen cloth soaked in rose oil or pitch on the wound foundation and place it on top, and instruct the patient to rest.
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And then let it drain until it stops, and when it has ceased, treat it with salves and other remedies, until it heals.

Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	Often there is a drying of fevers in the intestines and due to natural constraint; and when the disease is old and medication has no effect.   (It seems there might be a mistake in this line as "sechement" doesn't correspond to the context provided.)
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	 You must puncture the bark of a willow or your fingernail on top to prevent it from getting wet.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	 then treat it until it is healed as required.
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	 If it cannot heal, you must shave more forcefully than before, until it heals and is barked.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 then treat it until it heals.
dou fremit	The trembling / shuddering
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	 A scab is a small appearance on the body and it goes deep.
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	 And sometimes the scab breaks open the skin, and it feels like death trembling, and spreads throughout the body, more in the hands than other parts.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	 And the cure is that you take a cane from an ostrich feather, or a strong bird's feather, and place it on the patient's pulse, so that the purple circles surround the pulse completely.
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	 Then turn your hand around the whole cane so that you cover the pulse entirely and insert it deeply, and stiffen the pulse from its roots.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	And if you see, do this with a cane made of iron or wood in the following shape, and be thin underneath and wide above:
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser.	 Do not pierce it, but hold it tightly and press it.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	 And if you see that the pulse needs to be cauterized as described in the chapter on cautery.
de la forme dou clistere	of the shape of the clyster (enema)...
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet;	 Sometimes one does a silver or pitch cloister, or melted tallow or honey.
et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	 And sometimes these small and large instruments are made according to those for whom they are intended.
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	Therefore, it is applied in the treatment of children who are weak and suffering, they are small.
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	The form of the cluster is either small or large, where the belly is bound in this manner:
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez;	 And it has an opening where the abdomen is sewn, as you can see, and the shoulders are pierced within.
et ait a l’un des costez II pertus, et en l’autre I;	 And it has one wound on one side, and another in the other.
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus, et ait entre chescun pertus I doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus I fil fort de fil crut tort en X ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	 and the abdomen should be filled with medicines from a beast's bladder or parchment, and pierced all around with small wounds, and have an interval of one space between each wound, then thread thick yarn through the wounds in the shape of an X or square, and sew up the abdomen like a goatskin.
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize;	 And when the medicines are inside, tie it with a strong thread to the instrument in front, then apply a clyster.
et c’est li forme dou cercle:	 and this is the form of a circle.
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	 And let the medicine not be too hot nor too cold, and anoint the head with caster oil or egg yolk ointment, or something similar, then gently apply it.
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses II mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit, et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet;	 Then the attendant should press the patient's ears between both hands until it becomes visible, then remove the ointment, and make the patient lie down with his legs exposed, if the medicine comes out, wipe it as much as possible.
et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	 And if he sleeps all night, it is more helpful.
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you plaster the patient with a belly disease of discharge, and the medication begins to heal quickly, continue to treat it until he is well.
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por I enfant;	 If there are hemorrhoids or abscesses, let the ointment be as thin as for a child.
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	 and this is the form of the subtle ointment where the skin is tightened:
des plaies	wounds  (plural of "plaie")
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies;	 We have said in the section on treatment of wounds;
or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	 You will be told about treatments for hands and medicine, according to their completion.
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	I say that wounds are diverse according to how they are made, and according to the places where the wounds are made, and of what kind they are made.
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	 The things by which wounds are made are by thrusting with a spear, cutting with a sword and knife, or lance or fist or arrow, or similar objects.
ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres;	 Or those wounds are made according to the laws of the body, such as when a wound falls on the neck, or head, or chest, or abdomen, or liver, and similar limbs;
et je vos dirai la cure de chescune plaie, et encomencerai as plaies dou chief simples, car li remenbrance venra en son chapistre.	 And I will tell you the treatment for each wound, and I will begin with simple head wounds, for it will come in its chapter.
Je dis que quant simple plaie vient ou chief, et li os n’est brisiez, si pren garde se c’est de gitement de piere ou de semblans choses, et li cuir est toutevoie rompus et est li plaie grans, et tu doutes levement d’aposteme chaut:	 I say that when a simple wound comes to the head and the bone is not broken, take care if it is from being thrust with a spear or similar objects, and the skin is completely torn and the wound is large, and you doubt the formation of an abscess, clean the wound hot:
si le fai tantost sainier de la cephalique meismement s’il vient poc de sanc de la plaie, et soit li sainie au contraire de la partie navree;	 If he quickly cleanses the head itself immediately, if a little blood comes from the wound, and the cleansing is contrary to the injured part;
et eschuisse li malaides repletion de vin et de viandes grosses.	 and the patient should empty his repleteness of wine and heavy foods.
Et s’il ne vuet sainier, si soit amenuisie sa viande, et ne boive point de vin, ne ne menjuce point de char;	 And if he does not want to cleanse it, let his meat be reduced, and drink no wine, nor eat flesh.
et met sor la plaie, se apostemes chaus i vient, coton moilliet en oile roset soulement, ou en vin stiptice;	 and put on the wound, if an abscess grows there, moistened cotton in rose oil only, or in vinegar.
et s’il n’i a aposteme chaut, si met sus la plaie, s’elle est fresche a tout son sanc, et elle n’est muee par l’air, poudre, que je dirai un poc ci aprés;	 and if there is no abscess hot, put on the wound if it is fresh with all its blood, and it is not moved by air, powder, as I will say a little later.
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucuns oignemens, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And if the arm has moved it, place some hot poultices on it until it heals.
Et se li plaie est grans si com de tailleure d’espee et de semblans, et les levres ne se pueent assembler par tentes, si les assemble par cousture, si com je dirai as plaies dou ventre, de la costure.	And if the wound is large, like the size of a sword and similar, and the lips cannot be brought together by stitches, then bring them together by suturing, as I will say about wounds in the abdomen, by suturing.
Se li plaie est descoverte de l’os, et pent, et ne tient mais que a un poc, si le cope;	 If the wound is exposed of the bone, and gaping, and does not hold together, close it (the wound).
puis cure la plaie de medicine, et restoure char dure en leu de cuir, et comande au malaide a mengier grosses viandes, si com testes et froment cuit, ausi com poulz, et semblans choses.	 Then heal the wound with medicine, and restore hard skin in place of skin, and instruct the patient to eat large foods, such as roasted meat, peas, cabbage, and similar things.
Et se tu trueves ou cuir porriture, et il n’aert a l’os, si cope lou porrit tot, et giete fuer, puis le cure;	 And if you find a rotten flesh or skin that is not on the bone, remove it all and let it fester, then heal (the wound).
et se il ait artere en la plaie ou voine, dont sans cort, et il ne puet estainchier par medicines, si quier l’artere, et se tu la trueves desloie, si la lie d’un fil;	 And if there is an artery or vein in the wound or near it that cannot be stopped without cauterization, and you find it dislocated, tie it with a thread.
et se ceu ne profite mie, si la cauterize.	 And if that does not help, cauterize (it).
Et se ces plaies sont petites et simples, si est li cure legiere:	 And if the wounds are small and simple, the treatment is easy:
et est que tu mettes ens ceste poudre qui soude ainsois que li ars l’ait muee.	 and it is that you put this powder which will heal as soon as the wound has moved (healed).
Et li maniere de la poudre si est:	 And the way of the powder is:
pren encens une partie;	 Take incense a part;
sanc de dragon II parties;	 blood of dragon 2 parts;
chalz vive III parties, et le poudre subtilment, et emple la plaie, et l’estraint forment, tant qu’elle s’aerse bien et se joigne a tout son sanc;	 Calf live in three parts, and the powder finely, and apply it to the wound, and press firmly until it drains well and joins with all its blood.
et puis la lie bien, et la laisse sens desliier, s’elle n’enfle;	 Then bind it well, and let it heal on its own if it does not swell.
car on n’oste la madicine tant qu’ele soit sanee.	 because the medicine is not taken out until it has healed.
Et aucune fois fait on ceu de chalz soulement, quant on n’ait l’encens ne lou sanc de dragon, mais que li ars n’ait muee la plaie.	And at times this is done only with coal when neither incense nor dragon's blood is available, but the wound has not yet healed.
Et se li ars ait mueit la plaie, meismement en esteit, si n’i met om mie ceste poudre;	 And if the wound has been opened by fire, most certainly do not put this powder on it.
mais met sus aucuns oignemens digestis, ou poulz de farine d’orge faites d’aigue et de miel, tant qu’ele giete bowe;	 but put some digested ointments or barley flour made with water and honey on it until it exudes pus.
puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then heal it with other treatments until it has healed.
Et se li brisure d’os vient avec la plaie, et elle est petite, si l’estrai as pinceures subtilz;	 And if a bone fracture comes with the wound and it is small, extract it with fine forceps.
et je vos dirai ci aprés les brisures dou chief.	 And I shall tell you after the fractures of the head.
de la plaie dou col	About the wound of the neck (or throat)   (I am assuming that 'col' here means 'neck', but it could also mean 'throat'. The original French term is ambiguous in this context.)
Se plaie vient ou col et elle est simple, si n’a point de difference entre li et celi dou chief, mais se li ners dou col ou li artere est copee.	If the wound comes or affects the neck and it is simple without any difference from that of the head, but if the nerves of the neck or the arteries are cut.   (The original French term 'col' is ambiguous in this context, meaning either neck or throat.)
Se c’est li ners, si n’i a autre engien que laissier la cure, et n’i mettre nulle chose restraignant, car il nuit as ners et les fait retraire;	 If it is the nose, there is no other remedy than to let it heal naturally, and not to apply anything binding, because it hurts the nose and causes it to retreat.
et ne mettre sus la plaie rien froit, car li substance des ners est froide, et li continuation d’aus si est avec le cerveil, qui est li plus haus membres;	 And not to put anything cold on the wound, because the substance of noses is cold, and their continuity is with the brain, which is the highest member.
mais soit li medicine souez, si com chalz lavee en aigue douce, et mellee avec oile roset, et cucie lavee ausi en aigue douce, et autres pieres de mine selonc ceste maniere, et oignemens moistes.	 But if the medicine is warm, as boiling water sweetened with rose oil, boiled and washed with gentle warm water in the same way, and other stones of that kind according to this manner, and always kept moist.
Et se li plaie est grans, si la cout et lie de bendes, puis la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the wound is large, bind it with strips, then heal it until it heals.
Et se les plaies sont parfondes et ele est chevee et pleinne de bowe, si la perce ou plus bas leu;	 And if the wounds are deep and pus-filled and swollen, pierce or lower it.
et se li artere est copee, et decorremens de sanc en vient, si la desoivre, et la loie, et la cauterize se mestier est;	 If the artery is cut, and blood flows out, then tie it off, let it lie still, and cauterize if necessary.
et se li espinee de la gorge est copee, ou li keurs, et li conduiz est gardez, par coi la viande va, si cout le keur sus la cainne de la gorge, et ne touchier la gorge mais la remet selonc sa figure naturel;	 If the spine of the throat is cut, or the veins, and the conduit is kept, so that the flesh goes through it, then raise the vein above the throat and do not touch the throat but put it back according to its natural shape.
et puis l’estraint avenanment, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le cure d’oignemens desechans tant qu’il soit sanez;	 Then, apply pressure and let it be for some days, then heal it with infusions of dissolved herbs until it heals.
et se li plaie a fait empression en l’os, si la quier;	 If the wound presses into the bone, pierce it.
et s’il i a pieces d’os, si les trai fuers toz se tu pues, et ces que tu ne pues avoir, si laisse tant que li plaie porrisse, et soit desevree et aligie li issue;	 If there are bone fragments, pull them all out if you can, and those that you cannot, leave until the wound discharges, and align and seal the exit.
et se li plaie est fresche, si poudre sus la poudre que j’ai dit.	 If the wound is fresh, sprinkle the powder I mentioned on it.
Et s’il a en la plaie os et il i a fistule, si la cure ensi com j’ai dit en son chapistre.	If there is bone in the wound and it has a fistula, cure as I have said in its chapter.
de la plaie de lance ou de coutel	of the wound from spear or knife.   --> Of the spear or knife wound
Se c’est cop de lance ou de coutel, et li plaie est parfonde, si regarde se de la plaie saut ventositez cant li malaides alainne:	 If it is a spear or knife wound and the injury gushes air from it, look to see where the air escapes from the wound:
saiches adonques que li plaie est mortelz;	 Know then that the wound is fatal;
et s’elle n’est parfonde, et elle est fresche a tout son sanc, si n’i mettre mie a la premiere houre la poudre, ne ne la liier mie por le sanc que ne demorse em parfont, et reviegne au cuer, et ocie lou malaide;	 and if it is not deep, and it is fresh with all its blood, do not put powder on it at first hour nor bind it due to the blood that it may dissolve entirely, and return to the heart, and kill the patient.
mais i met oignement atractif, et le lie II fois le jor;	 but apply an attractive ointment, and bind it twice a day.
et se tu n’as oignement, si met en la plaie viel coton por succier fuers la moistor, et fai dormir le malaide sus la plaie III jors, ou IIII, ou plusors;	 and if you do not have an ointment, place old cotton in the wound to absorb the moisture, and make the patient sleep on the wound for 3 or 4 days, or more.
si n’i venra mie spasme, ne tremor male de cuer n’estraingnemens d’alainne;	 if no spasm, nor a bad tremor of heart or strange alien symptoms come.
et quant tu vois les bones dispositions, si saiches que li plaie est sauve.	 And when you see the good alignments, know that the wound is healed.
Cure la donques de tentes et d’autres cures, tant qu’il soit sanez;	 Then cure the wounds and other remedies, as long as he is healthy;
et s’elle ne puet saner, et oevre, adés saiches que il i a fistule;	 And if it cannot heal, then open it, knowing that there will be a fistula.
si la cure si com on doit.	 Cure it as one should.
Et se li plaie est d’incision d’espee ou de coutel, et elle est simple, ou pis ou au dos, si la cure de ceu qui est devant;	 If the wound is from a sword or knife incision and it's simple, or worse, or at the back, then cure what is in front of it.
s’elle est grans, de cousture;	 If it is large, stitch it up.
et s’elle est petite, de poudre, et s’elle est empressee en l’os, et en a copeit pieces, si quier la plaie, et les trai fuers s’il sont desevrez;	 If it is small, use powder, and if it has entered the bone and there are fragments inside, open up the wound and pull out the shards if they are exposed.
et s’il ne sont desevrez, si laisse porrir la plaie, si aligera li estractions;	 If they are not drained, let the wound fester, align the extractions.
et des autres plaies as autres membres est li jugemens si com nos avons dit.	 And regarding other wounds on other limbs, make judgments as we have said.
dou derrompement dou ventre	The dislocation of the abdomen
Li derompemens dou ventre est grans et moiens et petis;	 The ruptures in the abdomen are great and medium-sized and small.
de la grant plaie saut aucune fois li intestine, ou li ners des intestines, par coi li intromission d’aus;	 From a large wound, the intestines may jump out once or the nerves of the intestines, by which the insertion is made.
et li costure est plus malaisie, et aucune fois vaut pis li petite plaie que li grans, por ceu c’on remet plus a poinnes les intestines en, s’on ne les i remet de chaut en chaut;	 And the sewing is more difficult, and sometimes it is worth less to close a small wound than a large one, because you must be more careful with the intestines when closing, if not sewn carefully from inside out.
por ce que li intestine enflent tantost qu’il sentent le froit, si rentrent plus a poinnes, et por ceu vaut mues li moieinne plaie, por ceu c’on ramoine mues l’intestine a son leu que as autres II.	 Because the intestines swell quickly when they feel pain, and therefore it is necessary to be more careful with them, and for this reason, a medium-sized wound is preferable because you are more careful to move the intestines back in place than with others.
Et saiches que li routure dou ventre est selonc IIII manieres:	 And know that the hernia of the belly is according to four kinds:
les II costures communes avienent en la costure dou ventre, et li costure des autres plaies dou cors et II autres costures propres sont communes as autres plaies;	 The two common kinds occur in the abdominal hernia, and the other kinds of hernias in the other body parts have their own specific kinds.
et toutevoie elles sont plus propres avec la costure dou ventre, et je dirai une chescune et declairerai.	 And indeed, they are more proper with the abdominal hernia, and I will say one kind and explain it.
Je di que quant li plaie est petite, et aucune chose de l’intestine ist fuer, et griés chose est dou remettre, ceu est par l’une des II manieres:	 I say that when the hernia is small and nothing of the intestines protrudes, and it is easy to replace it, this is one of the two kinds:
ou por la petitece de la plaie, si com nos avons dit, ou por ce que li intestine est enflez por le froit.	 either because of the small size of the hernia, as we have said, or because the intestines are swollen due to cold.
Et quant il est frois, eschaufez lou en teil maniere:	 And when it is cold, warm it in some way:
moillie une esponge ou I mol drapeil en aigue tede soulement, ou tu cuis en aigue squinant et cipre et spique, et arose l’intestine tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	 Moisten a sponge or a cloth with warm water only, or cook in hot wine and cypress and spike, and anoint the intestines until the inflammation is removed.
et aucune fois fait ce vins restraingnans, et est muedre que awe soule por desenfler.	 And sometimes make this wine-based restraint, and it is mixed with sulphur to reduce swelling.
Et quant tu vois l’enfleure departir, si amoiste l’intestine d’aigue ou altee et malves soient cuites, car par ceu est aligie li entree a poc de chose;	 And when you see the inflammation spreading, anoint the intestines with warm or hot water, because this stops the entry of anything to a great degree.
et s’il n’i puet entrer, si fent un poc la plaie a l’estrument de coi on cope les emorroydes;	 And if it cannot enter, make a small wound with the instrument used for treating hemorrhoids;
et li premiere cure est muedre que li taille, que nus n’i doit taillier sens grant necessiteit n’i ait;	 And the first treatment is mixed with resin, and we should not cut it unnecessarily.
et c’est li estrumens por le fendre:	 And this is the instrument for breaking:
si trenche dedens en la corbeure et defuer non, et vez ci la forme:	 It should cut inside the hump and not pierce through, and look at its shape here:
Et quant li plaie est enlargie, et li intestine saut fuer, si le remet arer selonc la forme naturel en son leu propre, se tu en as pooir, car ce vaut mues.	 And when the wound is enlarged, and the intestines come out, put it back in its natural shape in its proper place, if you have the power to do so, for this is necessary.
Quant li plaie est large, et elle est en la partie desoz lou ventre, si covient que tu faices gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et met ses jambes plus haut que son chief;	 When the wound is wide and located in the lower part of the belly, it is necessary to make the patient lie on his back, and raise his legs higher than his head.
et s’elle est en la partie desoz le ventre, si met le chief et le pis plus haut que les parties desoz, et ausi se li routure dou ventre est en l’une des II parties si met t’entente en ceu que li partie navree soit plus haute que li autre;	 If it is in the lower part of the belly, then put the head and feet higher than the parts below, and thus when the wound is in one of the two sides, pay attention to the fact that the affected side should be higher than the other.
et ensi covient amenistrer ceu que je dis en plaies grans et moienes.	 And it is necessary to do what I say in large and small wounds.
